
-----title
常州 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8b6623eed63747f380700598363f2a5c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8b6623eed63747f380700598363f2a5c");'><span id='8b6623eed63747f380700598363f2a5c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1076')">1060-1076年</a>，1-17岁</div><div id='8b6623eed63747f380700598363f2a5c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年10月18日</a>　公出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1074')">1061-1074年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　居乡。公十六岁而学成，天资仁厚，器量闳博，事亲以孝称，端重寡言。坐不踞，立不倚，处屋漏暗室，其容肃然也。夜寐恐见祖先，卧必叉手。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　居乡。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7bc9337db6434781acded966913398a9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7bc9337db6434781acded966913398a9");'><span id='7bc9337db6434781acded966913398a9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1097')">1096-1097年</a>，37-38岁</div><div id='7bc9337db6434781acded966913398a9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年2月</a>　丁父保之公忧，解官居制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年8月</a>　丁父保之公忧，解官居制。有文。作品：曾祖诗训后语。<div id='poem_1209515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>曾祖诗训后语<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209515")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209515'>此诗乃曾祖舍人所作，而自书以遗先祖于入仕之初者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209515_comment'></div>先祖以天禧三年擢进士甲科，至至和元年，仕三十六年，年六十三以没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209515_comment'></div>盖由军事推官积累为都官郎中、郡太守，未尝一日不奉训诲，故所至以官为家，以民为子，惟恐朝廷之恩不下流而叹息愁恨有形于声者，阴德及人，不已多乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209515_comment'></div>孟子曰：「不得乎亲，不可以为人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209515_comment'></div>不顺乎亲，不可以为子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209515_comment'></div>先祖于是尽人子之道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209515_comment'></div>先考都曹尝语浩曰：「吾将以诗本刻石，传示子孙，世世奉承，此心弗坠，庶几稍称前人所以垂裕之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209515_comment'></div>一有违叛，是辱其先，是大不孝，非吾子孙也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209515_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209515_comment'></div>音犹在耳，而先考奄弃诸孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209515_comment'></div>凡是生平一言一事，苟可以追念者，莫不心铭焉，而况此其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209515_comment'></div>顾浩不肖，不足以仰对遗训，尚赖祖考之泽，未即陨灭，敢不遹成先志而刻诸石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209515_comment'></div>先祖有兄九人，其后散居四方者多矣，亦将以此示之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209515_comment'></div>盖曾祖之意无所不在，不直为先祖发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209515_comment'></div>绍圣三年八月一日，浩谨书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1209515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　丁父保之公忧，解官居制。作品：邦典序。<div id='poem_1209494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邦典序<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209494")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209494'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209494'>真淡翁，隐者也，少举进士，有能赋声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209494_comment'></div>已而用其伯父质肃公之荐仕州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209494_comment'></div>一日不合意，莞然笑曰：「道其在是乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209494_comment'></div>拂衣以归，遂闭关于汉水之上，殆二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209494_comment'></div>元祐八年冬，予以教官至襄阳，求见翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209494_comment'></div>翁弗予拒也，而登其堂，造其室，亲炙其言行，而知其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209494_comment'></div>盖尝论辩至于经史百氏之书，从横稽据，如出乎其时而目睹其事，如即乎其人而躬受其旨，未尝不覤然惊，喟然叹，以翁为邈不可际也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209494_comment'></div>其后集《论语》《春秋》者分为二卷，合四十四篇，且以六典治邦国之义名之曰《邦典》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209494_comment'></div>顾自《三传》以来，相踵而私其见者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209494_comment'></div>独于众言殽乱之中，取《周官》而折衷焉，以畅孔子不说之意，如执规矩以验方圆，如引绳墨以分曲直，虽三尺童子亦举知其可信不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209494_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209494_comment'></div>《春秋》，日月也，传注者食之，不有人焉袪阴阳之慝而还其光明，则伥伥于世者孰待而成功乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209494_comment'></div>翁之有功于经，可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209494_comment'></div>览者以天默而成之之心观其默而成之之说，则《邦典》之奥当自得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209494_comment'></div>姑掇其大概，并翁之所以出处者发其端云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209494_comment'></div>翁唐氏，名既，字潜亨，号真淡翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209494_comment'></div>绍圣四年月日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1209494_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　丁父保之公忧，解官居制。有铭文。作品：故朝请郎张公行状。<div id='poem_1209643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故朝请郎张公行状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209643")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209643'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209643'>公讳次元，字希一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209643_comment'></div>其先广陵人，自天章公归老于常州，遂为常州武进人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209643_comment'></div>六世祖升，仕唐为滁州清流县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209643_comment'></div>生约，为金吾卫长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209643_comment'></div>生训，即公高祖也，仕杨行密，为黄州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209643_comment'></div>有智勇，与其等辈三十六人号淝上英雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209643_comment'></div>曾祖璆，仕南唐为校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209643_comment'></div>祖佖，擢进士第一，为右内史学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209643_comment'></div>金陵既平，从后主归本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209643_comment'></div>太祖闻其清节，授右赞善大夫、知荣州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209643_comment'></div>太宗时数言治要，多见听用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209643_comment'></div>考温之，以直道自奋，仁宗深器之，尝待制天章阁，隐然为一时名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209643_comment'></div>生二子，公其季也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209643_comment'></div>皇祐二年，用天章公奏为太庙斋郎，再奏守将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209643_comment'></div>至和二年，签书江阴军判官事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209643_comment'></div>年尚少，守将易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209643_comment'></div>初不为沮，事枉必争，如道理而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209643_comment'></div>富民孙氏缘守将数燕其池亭，浸有所谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209643_comment'></div>公察其端，每遇燕集，力以疾辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209643_comment'></div>自是孙氏严惮，不敢逞，而守将益知公非碌碌贵游子也，尊礼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209643_comment'></div>嘉祐三年，转太常寺奉礼郎、知常州武进县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209643_comment'></div>每岁输纳甫期，吏必豫率私财，探邑官之欲而置其所须以阴中之，然后肆行诛求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209643_comment'></div>公先谕以不可，乃为禁令，且峻惩其犯者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209643_comment'></div>迄公去，所输无虑数十万，而民间卒无一钱入吏手，欢然为俚谣传于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209643_comment'></div>白鹤溪导滆湖，溉民田甚广，岁久湮塞，公力浚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209643_comment'></div>大姓有冒其地者飞语撼摇，竟不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209643_comment'></div>初流亟还，绵百馀里，无复旱暵，至今赖焉，目为奉礼河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209643_comment'></div>转大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209643_comment'></div>丁天章公忧，服除，遇神宗即位，转卫尉寺丞，监楚州粮料院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209643_comment'></div>熙宁三年，转大理寺丞，用淮南转运使陈安石荐，知通州静海县，兼监都盐仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209643_comment'></div>岁适大旱，苗且槁死，惟漕河衍溢而法不可决，慨然身任其责，决以便民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209643_comment'></div>郡果操法按治，章甫上，今翰林学士蒋公之奇方领漕事，闻而止之，且以书劳公曰：「真古良吏用心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209643_comment'></div>海濒瘠卤，民窘寒饥，类以鬻盐为生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209643_comment'></div>每捕至庭下，不忍遽寘于法，诲而遣之，约毋犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209643_comment'></div>往往怀公之恩，转就它业，而冒法者益少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209643_comment'></div>转太子中舍，同提举淮南东路市易事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209643_comment'></div>元丰元年，赐绯衣银鱼，转殿中丞，以官制换奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209643_comment'></div>市易法行，奉承之人多不喻上意，于是选置使者，分董诸路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209643_comment'></div>而大丞相王文公雅知公才，首被除擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209643_comment'></div>使既称旨，留久其任凡五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209643_comment'></div>转承议郎，通判太平州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209643_comment'></div>未行，丁谯郡太夫人忧，服除，遇今上即位，转朝奉郎资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209643_comment'></div>任事直，知信阳军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209643_comment'></div>时河朔水灾，洺州尤甚，遂改知洺州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209643_comment'></div>朝廷方务赈恤，公条约三十馀事以辅导之，吏绝巧谩，民受实惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209643_comment'></div>按察使朱光庭嘉其所为，深得仁圣恻隐之意，推示诸郡，使矜式焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209643_comment'></div>漳河距城才五里，遥堤高峻，下视城中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209643_comment'></div>方涨溢时，一失固御，则冲注无前，荡为陂泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209643_comment'></div>公每至岁初，饬属县谨不虞，苟可以致力者，无不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1209643_comment'></div>一夕河暴决，水怒至齧堤，举城号救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1209643_comment'></div>亟出慰之曰：「吾已有备矣，无患」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1209643_comment'></div>即率兵夫巡护堤上，冒盛暑、忘寝食，如是三日而水退，人争鼓舞歌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1209643_comment'></div>地居重法，素多贼盗，其魁桀者咸有号名，曹聚雠劫，人逸不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1209643_comment'></div>及公赏罚明信，人乐用命，不日就擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1209643_comment'></div>初，鸡泽境内最为渊薮，耕蚕岁入悉辇致邑中，民以为苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1209643_comment'></div>至是犬卧不警，遂不为避盗计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1209643_comment'></div>俗祀崔府君尤敬，亦或乘之济其诡谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1209643_comment'></div>一日方退食，遽闻百馀人拥一黥者直入据黄堂曰：「我府君也，来为太守福」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1209643_comment'></div>公命左右缚于庭，状立见，悉诛之，其俗遂革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1209643_comment'></div>代还，知蕲州，改信阳军，转朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1209643_comment'></div>信阳逾百年进士无显者，首兴学校，延致望士，于其讲日亲主豆觞，而学者感孚，术业自劝，且立生祠著公德焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1209643_comment'></div>长社李氏子讼其弟本黄氏，不当弟，挽女兄为證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1209643_comment'></div>女亦黄氏也，助之力，故狱屡变而听者咸取决焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1209643_comment'></div>自庆历至元祐，李讼不已，后以属公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1209643_comment'></div>公顾其弟貌言不类兄，且诘其女所以證者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1209643_comment'></div>女指亲在时献神状语，取状视之，则纸弊而墨鲜，又有桑枝痕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1209643_comment'></div>折之曰：「岂非染纸为弊色，以桑枝暴于日中乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1209643_comment'></div>女矍然无以应，即具首伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1209643_comment'></div>数十年间，听者几人，至公立谈决之，人皆神以为异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1209643_comment'></div>代还，以先茔在清流，求知滁州，转朝请郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1209643_comment'></div>未行，改虢州，又改除江淮荆浙福建广南路提点坑冶铸钱事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1209643_comment'></div>坑冶散布九路，多在山谷险绝中，使者罕到，弊久益深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1209643_comment'></div>公不以为惮，躬自按之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1209643_comment'></div>期年遍五路，以其所见，条利害四十有三事请于朝，书可行者三十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1209643_comment'></div>至睦州，感疾，犹欲东去，浸剧，乃还杭州，至则革矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1209643_comment'></div>然而经画鼓铸，谆谆在口，家人勉公姑少休，毅然曰：「食君之禄，而尸素可乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1209643_comment'></div>比卒，无一语及私事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1209643_comment'></div>实绍圣四年三月二十六日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1209643_comment'></div>享年六十有七，积勋至上护军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1209643_comment'></div>娶鲁氏，赠扶风县君，参知政事肃简公宗道之孙，尚书驾部郎中有功之女，谯郡太夫人之犹子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1209643_comment'></div>继室严氏，封华阳县君，直秘阁颖之孙，衡州军事判官孟坚之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1209643_comment'></div>子男八人，基，宣德郎，以文学政事称于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1209643_comment'></div>坚、域、垣、坦、坰、埙、壑，皆举进士，有贤声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1209643_comment'></div>女三人，长适进士方希纯，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1209643_comment'></div>次适承奉郎吕切问，次适郊社斋郎崔颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1209643_comment'></div>孙男五人，铎、铉、錞、锡、銮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1209643_comment'></div>女八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1209643_comment'></div>公天资孝友，遇事刚明，斩斩不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1209643_comment'></div>天章公既老，未尝去左右，虽勉之使仕，非数舍近，不废问安，不往也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1209643_comment'></div>太夫人嫠居二十年，承颜养志，惟恐不逮如一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1209643_comment'></div>女兄归都官员外郎蔡天球，惟一女；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1209643_comment'></div>女弟归著作郎石约，惟一子宽民，尚幼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1209643_comment'></div>皆丧其夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1209643_comment'></div>取以归，俾无愁叹终其身，又择名士以归其女，今朝进郎、通判庐州凌浩则其婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1209643_comment'></div>择师友以成宽民，其后中进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1209643_comment'></div>元祐初，将变役法，诏郡邑言利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1209643_comment'></div>公建以为先朝行免役久矣，民安之，愿毋变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1209643_comment'></div>当路或擿公曰：「此非庙堂意，亟改奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1209643_comment'></div>公曰：「臣事君当勿欺，所见如是，曷可改也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1209643_comment'></div>使淮东时，布衣使敏功持钱千万，懋迁多乾没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1209643_comment'></div>公绳之，或以告曰：「敏功乃丞相王禹玉亲党也，奈何不纵」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1209643_comment'></div>公曰：「吾职在奉法，忍废法以奉权贵乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1209643_comment'></div>已而遣都提举司勾当官吕震按公职事，一无所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1209643_comment'></div>比公还朝，当升郡守，遂沮不行，送吏部为通判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1209643_comment'></div>人人为公不平，而公恬然无怨色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1209643_comment'></div>郡吏稍不自强，必面折之，然卒归于恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1209643_comment'></div>或不幸大故，如洺州临洺监镇滁阳林师忠、信阳军司理参军河南宋瑜，则力为主其后事，且计其乡远迩，以资助其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1209643_comment'></div>微至食饮，亦具风棱峭厉，若不可屈折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1209643_comment'></div>一闻人之善，则靡然向慕，尤于山阳先生徐公积倾心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1209643_comment'></div>先生亦伟公趣操，爱敬之，每形于诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1209643_comment'></div>读书成诵该洽，尤悉本朝事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1209643_comment'></div>常慕「籯金不如一经」与「多财损智益过」之说，用以诲子孙甚严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1209643_comment'></div>而禄廪之馀，一以周艰阨、施宗族，于其亡也，衣衾犹有不备者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1209643_comment'></div>自远祖以来，皆葬清流，凡无后者，至其终日，必即其处用浮屠法追享之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1209643_comment'></div>今遂循以为式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1209643_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1209643_comment'></div>公以天章公直道终始为朝野推重，常惧奉承失坠，贻识者之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1209643_comment'></div>今以其生平大节观之，虽年位弗充，不极其志，亦可谓无愧乎前人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1209643_comment'></div>诸孤迫于吉卜，既以其年六月二十七日己酉葬于清流县昌城乡安仁村之原，尚念幽刻未就，将以求铭于世之显人，则相与泣血而属状于某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1209643_comment'></div>某愚不肖，视公盖外曾祖行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1209643_comment'></div>蚤辱知怜，恩德隆厚，顾虽衔哀在庐，死亡无日，不敢辞命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1209643_comment'></div>于是迹其实而次序之以告云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_121_1209643_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　丁父保之公忧。有记。作品：承天寺大藏记。<div id='poem_1209607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209607?labeling=true' target='_blank'>承天寺大藏记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209607")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209607'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209607'>毗陵郡城中名刹相望，而传法者凡六院，惟承天据城之东南，实隋司徒陈杲仁之别圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209607_comment'></div>杲仁死非其所，其妻用浮屠法荐助之，遂舍以为寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209607_comment'></div>唐长庆二年，赐号正勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209607_comment'></div>至真宗皇帝即位之初，改赐今额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209607_comment'></div>越在一隅，风埃不到，眺听所接，阒如岩栖，四方禅者乐居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209607_comment'></div>顾经藏未建，众以为虑有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209607_comment'></div>元祐某年某月，道人德岑既领住持事，遂以告于人曰：「夫五千四十八卷，虽不足以尽禅之说，然其语非不多也，而祖师《心要》犹以为教外别传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209607_comment'></div>审如委付，示以全提，则虽绕床一匝，适半藏尔，况区区于五千四十八卷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209607_comment'></div>然初机者以此笃志，罢参者以此證解，游戏自在者以此遮眼，一言半偈，皆是善因，展轴抽函，无非妙用，以方便济群生者，亦何可废也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209607_comment'></div>信者翕然出力，为新其厨堂，新其浴室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209607_comment'></div>最后绍圣四年某月，因水陆殿广之为藏院，集所谓五千四十八卷者为若干函，以栖于其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209607_comment'></div>然后院之形胜益闳伟动人，而人益信岑之所存为可尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209607_comment'></div>岑嗣扬州建隆昭庆禅师，盖临济之苗裔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209607_comment'></div>方圆照禅师宗本传法中外时，岑未尝须臾离左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209607_comment'></div>一旦受请，孰不曰此圆照之的子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209607_comment'></div>及升座焚香，不嗣圆照，则嘈然非之，而闻者亦耿耿不快，宜其建立莫有应者，而所成就反如此，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209607_comment'></div>余闻众之初非岑也，甚者面斥，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209607_comment'></div>岑不为沮，徐告之曰：「吾心了然，不敢自欺耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209607_comment'></div>余尝怪世之禅者见圆照法席之盛，自京师至于东南，自王公至于士庶，莫不归仰，往往讳其得法之自，望风承托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209607_comment'></div>世曾不察，亦争向之，宁废父母晨昏之奉，而惟恐不当其意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209607_comment'></div>宁夺贫穷毫发之入，而唯恐不厚其施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209607_comment'></div>意彼欺世以自售且如此其偶，而况不自欺其心者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209607_comment'></div>不自欺其心者，诚也，不期于诚而诚至焉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209607_comment'></div>由方寸以充之，神明以生，变化以形，天地归吾掌握，万物出吾埏镕，何往而不济，而况介然于其间者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209607_comment'></div>此岑之所以贤于其徒而经藏不劳而成者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209607_comment'></div>昔住是院者多矣，百馀年间，如蕴、世珍、了素、仲文四人者尤以道德为世所高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209607_comment'></div>珍尝南徙其门，又为大殿而塑绘其像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209607_comment'></div>素为法堂，又为僧堂，又为东西廊，又为后架，又为屏隈之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209607_comment'></div>蕴则至今真相存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209607_comment'></div>郡人尊奉之，有祷辄应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209607_comment'></div>以其俗韩氏，号为韩长老，所以护助其院甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209607_comment'></div>今又得岑以成之如此，又将易其路以正于南，而跨池为梁，以便往还，是可书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209607_comment'></div>于是迹其院之本末而并载之，使后之览者得以考焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1209607_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d0a9ba66d7dc44d196117439b2fce3ef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d0a9ba66d7dc44d196117439b2fce3ef");'><span id='d0a9ba66d7dc44d196117439b2fce3ef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1111')">1106-1111年</a>，47-52岁</div><div id='d0a9ba66d7dc44d196117439b2fce3ef' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年4月</a>　到常州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年4月</a>　在常州，是月朔日，有序文。作知恩堂。作品：怀恩录序。<div id='poem_1209497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>怀恩录序<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁五年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209497")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209497'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209497'>余以元丰五年进士赐第，获缀仕版，自惟其分，未尝求荐于人，然所至荐者辄倍同列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209497_comment'></div>既无德行、文学、政事之实，又无家世、朋友、气力之助，其取而论之，使名声品秩因以遭遇于时，宜必有误其知者而不可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209497_comment'></div>夫惟公心直道，为天子求贤能以辅太平之治，固不以此为私恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209497_comment'></div>然恩之所被，自非兼忘天下之人，则岂不知所怀哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209497_comment'></div>客谓信陵君曰：「人有德于公子，公子不可忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209497_comment'></div>公子有德于人，愿公子忘之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209497_comment'></div>余尝三覆斯言，夙夜黾勉，思有以称其万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209497_comment'></div>又虑岁月浸久，或失其详，于是集荐词而编次之，谓之《怀恩录》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209497_comment'></div>盖非特自怀其恩而已，又将使子子孙孙怀之而不忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209497_comment'></div>怀之而不忘，则见其子孙如见其父祖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209497_comment'></div>《诗》不云乎：「无言不雠，无德不报」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209497_comment'></div>盖必如是，而后庶几可以无愧云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209497_comment'></div>崇宁五年四月一日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1209497_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年10月</a>　在常州，有铭文。作品：张唐英墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《张唐英墓志铭》题下注“崇宁五年十月”）</span><div id='poem_1209655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209655?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张唐英墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁五年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209655")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209655'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209655'>君张氏，讳某，字唐英，常州宜兴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209655_comment'></div>曾大父延矩、大父麟、父宗道，皆晦殖厥德，至君遂奋立为儒家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209655_comment'></div>才出就举，即为举首，修简胡公宗愈、司封丁公骘皆一时领袖，乃居其次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209655_comment'></div>二公得其文读之，欣然无异语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209655_comment'></div>自至和迄元丰，二十年间，六试于礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209655_comment'></div>元丰八年，当以累举特持恩与其类策试，既已为第一，与进士试又入第三第，遂赐进士出身，调蜀州江原县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209655_comment'></div>终更，当进秩，会修简公帅成都，辟置幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209655_comment'></div>不行，辟监嘉州丰远监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209655_comment'></div>考满，当改官，有司辄疑沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209655_comment'></div>例故可辩，惧扳以累人，弗辩，遂受淮南节度推官，监高邮税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209655_comment'></div>用辟移监海州临洪场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209655_comment'></div>以建中靖国元年十月十五日卒于官，享年七十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209655_comment'></div>君以奇童子拔起垄亩，不舍昼夜，博极群书，作赋以赋称，治经以经显，学者翕然师之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209655_comment'></div>张庄张氏，赀高一方，筠州高安尉稹实主家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209655_comment'></div>人以利，故多为其窃笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209655_comment'></div>独君居其馆，训诲其子弟，十年未尝干一毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209655_comment'></div>高安畏服，待之礼有加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209655_comment'></div>君赴江原且行，高安已得疾，犹力疾入城饯君，君行而高安卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209655_comment'></div>在嘉州兼教授，月有食钱，积二岁一不取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209655_comment'></div>或诘其故，曰：「钱不足以赡诸生，可分以自润乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209655_comment'></div>士大夫高其义，争遣子弟从之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209655_comment'></div>外姑老矣，无子而孙甚贫，乃奉以入蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209655_comment'></div>及其亡也，多勉君火其柩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209655_comment'></div>君泣下曰：「忍为此耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209655_comment'></div>虽险远，距吾乡不过万里耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209655_comment'></div>竟护以归葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209655_comment'></div>居乡徒行，虽夜分必冠带，朋友止之，曰：「幽有鬼神，其可忽」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209655_comment'></div>接人无贤愚少长，谆谆曲尽诚意，外若无所不可，其中介不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209655_comment'></div>至今乡人时时道君作为，以警后生，至有追感而流涕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209655_comment'></div>歌诗杂文仅存二百篇，为一帙藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209655_comment'></div>两娶吴氏，前室生一男，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209655_comment'></div>一女，归贡士陈策，后君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209655_comment'></div>继室生二男，孝述、孝立，皆笃学自重，必能亢其宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209655_comment'></div>一女，归进士严知训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209655_comment'></div>孙女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209655_comment'></div>孝述等卜以崇宁五年十月乙酉葬君于晋陵县万安西乡姚野村之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209655_comment'></div>前事，持其内兄进士吴燮所为行状，且泣且拜请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209655_comment'></div>夫君盖乡先生也，安可辞，遂铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209655_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1209655'>谁为幽明，吾一贯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209655_comment'></div>谁为义利，吾一判之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209655_comment'></div>彼或言不足，吾裕然行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209655_comment'></div>贵富贱贫，谁其令之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209655_comment'></div>顺受其正，终身其宁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209655_comment'></div>子孙其承之，富禄其迎之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209655_comment'></div>不俟已日，君子信之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1209655_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　在常州。公自岭表归，即屏居，辟小圃，号曰道乡，学都称道乡先生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　在常州。有铭文。作品：夫人邹氏墓志铭(华直渊妻、鄒霖女)<div id='poem_1209673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夫人邹氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209673")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209673'>故寿州下蔡县主簿华君讳直渊之妻、夫人邹氏崇宁元年年八十有二，以闰六月癸亥终于常州之私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209673_comment'></div>其孙仲平等以十一月丙申祔藏于武进县怀德北乡下蔡之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209673_comment'></div>五年，追迹行实而为之状曰：夫人尚书都官郎中讳霖之长女，太常博士讳参之冢妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209673_comment'></div>其先杭州钱塘人，都官徙常之晋陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209673_comment'></div>夫人幼警慧，古今文章历耳辄成诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209673_comment'></div>都官未有子，夫人率其妹供子职甚谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209673_comment'></div>都官贤之，以归下蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209673_comment'></div>下蔡失所恃，弟妹多未龀，夫人一一调护，至于冠昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209673_comment'></div>门内之事，大者禀命，小者专达，靡不如太常意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209673_comment'></div>太常用是徇国忘家，以显名于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209673_comment'></div>下蔡既倦游，语夫人曰：「吾将归佚故乡，能安之否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209673_comment'></div>夫人曰：「君安，无不安者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209673_comment'></div>下蔡以故勇退就閒，逍遥声利之外，二十年如一日，未尝悔往慨不遇，惟训诲子孙而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209673_comment'></div>子男四人，申锡、峙、屿、申伯，皆举进士，申锡、峙尤以文学知名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209673_comment'></div>峙登第历官，一时公卿争挽致之，不克用以卒，终衢州西安县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209673_comment'></div>女三人，适进士李亘、胡元均、霍端辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209673_comment'></div>孙男十三人，平、寔、彦、宇、宙、完、寓、章、寅、宽、宰、宋，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209673_comment'></div>仲平登第，为高邮主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209673_comment'></div>寔以特起赐第郓州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209673_comment'></div>女十三人，长适进士周咸，次王临，次继咸室，次王履、邹语、周先，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209673_comment'></div>曾孙十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209673_comment'></div>夫人老矣，四子皆前逝，孙彦、宇亦夭逝，闻者不堪其忧，而夫人安之若命，泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209673_comment'></div>晚年不复省家事，惟岁时祭享，必纤悉阅视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209673_comment'></div>或以劝止，则曰「先实临之，安敢怠」，夫人贤德盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209673_comment'></div>状已，寔持以来，且曰：「夫人顾言曰『吾铭当属吾侄浩』，敢请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209673_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209673_comment'></div>浩之先君朝奉既不幸矣，姑尚无恙，可以慰罔极之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209673_comment'></div>今亦不幸矣，又属铭，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209673_comment'></div>于是雪涕而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209673_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1209673'>都官之女，太常之妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209673_comment'></div>媲德下蔡，卒为贤母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209673_comment'></div>八十有二，其身则寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209673_comment'></div>其子则否，不称其有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209673_comment'></div>不在其子，必在其孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209673_comment'></div>轩轩既翮，既翮而骞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209673_comment'></div>动惟时矣，聿傅于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209673_comment'></div>有丰其碑，有穹其龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209673_comment'></div>闯于高松，潜德光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209673_comment'></div>尚其有诗，配此铭词。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1209673_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　居家乡常州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年12月</a>　居家乡常州。有铭文。作品：胡子正墓志铭（胡元鈞）<div id='poem_1209656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>胡子正墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观元年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209656")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209656'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209656'>晋陵胡氏于东南最为名族，自文恭公贰枢府、修简公丞中台，其子孙昆弟以文学政事杰然见于世者踵相寻而起，入居台阁，出拥节旄，蔼蔼其盛未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209656_comment'></div>其或抱才而处，分老沈潜，则奉家法以周旋，终始无憾，庶几乎夫子所谓在家必达者，若君是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209656_comment'></div>君讳元钧，字子正，讳宗度之子，太常寺奉礼郎讳亶之孙，赠开府仪同三司、沂国公讳霖之曾孙，视文恭公为从祖，修简为从父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209656_comment'></div>自豫章徙而之晋陵，至君五世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209656_comment'></div>君既学，夙夜克励，期显亲，不幸失所怙，诸弟幼，奉礼君年高，聚族百口，无赢赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209656_comment'></div>慨然叹曰：「古人之学，孝友而已，奚必以仕进为哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209656_comment'></div>遂专力以任家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209656_comment'></div>奉礼君与母顾夫人无不意满以终其寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209656_comment'></div>抚诸弟至有家室，犹不以事劳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209656_comment'></div>有所入则付焉，不私一毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209656_comment'></div>故合居三十年，愉愉怡怡，乡邦称慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209656_comment'></div>迨今诸弟皆安富佚乐，君力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209656_comment'></div>岁大疫，族人有举家病者，死且过半，亲戚畏避，莫敢视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209656_comment'></div>君闻，亟往具棺敛、营药石，存亡咸不失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209656_comment'></div>同母兄俞氏夫妇亡，无子，君收育其孤女如己女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209656_comment'></div>当行，又择士以归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209656_comment'></div>乡人或系狱，计窘妄引，君欣然诬服，以脱其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209656_comment'></div>或贷其金不偿，辄折券不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209656_comment'></div>平居喜宾客，晚益饶裕，其子璿又能以君之所以奉亲者奉君，辟馆艺园，顺适君意，君乃不复事事，日与亲朋把酒笑谈而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209656_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209656_comment'></div>不有其身，以自奋于俯仰之间，既已说其祖、安其母而均及诸弟矣，又推是心以施乎乡党之人，同其忧乐，不但酬孝友之言而止，贤矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209656_comment'></div>大观元年七月五日，以疾终于家，享年七十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209656_comment'></div>初娶李氏，后娶华氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209656_comment'></div>子男五人，伯伦、伯强、伯玉、伯勤、璿，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209656_comment'></div>伯勤而上与女一人皆早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209656_comment'></div>孙男三人，迁、逵、逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209656_comment'></div>女四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209656_comment'></div>璿卜以其年十二月甲子葬君于晋陵县孝仁乡黄塘之原，同李夫人之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209656_comment'></div>前期，以通判处州、承议郎周君况之之状求铭于某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209656_comment'></div>某于君夫人华氏为内弟，又璿孝如此，其可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209656_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1209656'>孝于其亲，友于其弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209656_comment'></div>孰为古人，行之则是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209656_comment'></div>奋其一身，裕及三世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209656_comment'></div>内外卑尊，贯以诚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209656_comment'></div>居三十年，莫知其异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209656_comment'></div>爰逮宗党，爰逮闾里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209656_comment'></div>爰举斯心，有恩有义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209656_comment'></div>人之所难，独以为异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209656_comment'></div>是亦为政，何必从仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209656_comment'></div>尚其有承，以光受祉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1209656_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　居乡。有铭文。作品：砚铭　并跋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八四二《砚铭　并跋》题下注：“　大觀二年三月”）</span>宋子直墓志铭(宋靖)<div id='poem_1209658' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209658' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209658?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋子直墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观二年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209658")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209658_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209658'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209658'>通直郎、知温州平阳县事宋君讳靖，字子直，以大观元年七月疾革，顾其子澥、溥、泾而言曰：「彭城虽吾乡，然田荒屋坏，不可恃以久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209658_comment'></div>吾爱常州文物盛，又汝外氏所在，汝必葬吾于常而居焉，从舅学，吾死无憾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209658_comment'></div>俄以其月二十六日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209658_comment'></div>澥等奉遗命，得穴于晋陵县德泽乡冲浦之原，而以明年四月丙申克襄大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209658_comment'></div>初，君之疾也，平阳之民不复至庭下，曰须通直无恙，乃可辨曲直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209658_comment'></div>及君之卒也，虽重溪复岭之外，老扶幼挈，聚哭于门曰「通直竟舍我而逝耶」，语已又哭，观者亦哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209658_comment'></div>鳏寡孤独又绘像以祠焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209658_comment'></div>盖君爱民出天性，甫下车，罢胥徒之无名而巧挟文书以济其奸者三百人，令曰：「犹或窃扰吾民，亟执以告」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209658_comment'></div>自是绝迹，境内举安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209658_comment'></div>渔人夜半争鱼伤斗，捕者利赏，指为强劫，如其说，即当死者十八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209658_comment'></div>君原本情，杖之而已，以故得民心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209658_comment'></div>民数前令勤明廉洁，不以僻远改其度，如君比者才省记一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209658_comment'></div>呜呼，古所谓良吏者，君殆庶几乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209658_comment'></div>君叔涣嘉祐末登进士第为第三，声实暴耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209658_comment'></div>君慨然思慕以自励，乡先生中书舍人颜复、秘书省正字陈师道咸称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209658_comment'></div>初，用祖任为郊社斋郎，终父丧，调寿州司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209658_comment'></div>未几，丁祖母河东县君姚氏忧，又丁母夫人刘氏忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209658_comment'></div>服除，调濠州司法、应天府虞城尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209658_comment'></div>通四考，移同州冯翊冷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209658_comment'></div>代去，改宣德郎，磨勘转通直郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209658_comment'></div>在寿州，雪垂死者五人，法当改官，不以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209658_comment'></div>或诘其故，曰：「我不就赏，则失入者可以无罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209658_comment'></div>败人以自成，何心哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209658_comment'></div>在冯翊，以民苦转输，力与外台辨论，他邑亦赖以免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209658_comment'></div>居家孝友，父病，刲股涣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209658_comment'></div>子病心，护视深到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209658_comment'></div>胸中无畛畦，俸禄随手辄尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209658_comment'></div>享年四十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209658_comment'></div>曾祖说，卫尉寺丞，赠尚书工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209658_comment'></div>祖仲容，驾部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209658_comment'></div>父希元，宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209658_comment'></div>君娶予妹，五男五女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209658_comment'></div>长渤、第三汶皆夭逝，馀即澥、溥、泾，皆举进士，有立志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209658_comment'></div>长女适太原府祁县令姜思谦，次未行，次二亦夭逝，次尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209658_comment'></div>惟君高祖右谏议大夫惟干淳化中使陕西，首以高士种放、田诰、杨璞、万适闻于朝，咸被召擢，放尤光显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209658_comment'></div>夫知贤而不与立，孔子以为窃位不祥之实，孟子以为蔽贤者当之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209658_comment'></div>若谏议者固宜飨报，以大其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209658_comment'></div>然自子至孙四世矣，仕犹未达也，岂报之大者发迟耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209658_comment'></div>故因叙君遗事而追载之以待焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209658_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1209658'>环川原兮气秀，蔚松栝兮根深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209658_comment'></div>四方上下兮曷往，若来止兮容音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209658_comment'></div>自我民兮属耳，腾故邑兮讴吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209658_comment'></div>严奉尝兮兹始，久弥章兮君之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1209658_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年10月</a>　居乡。以八宝恩才授宣义郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　居乡。有铭文。作品：邹君墓志铭(邹扩)<div id='poem_1209673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夫人邹氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209673")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209673'>故寿州下蔡县主簿华君讳直渊之妻、夫人邹氏崇宁元年年八十有二，以闰六月癸亥终于常州之私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209673_comment'></div>其孙仲平等以十一月丙申祔藏于武进县怀德北乡下蔡之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209673_comment'></div>五年，追迹行实而为之状曰：夫人尚书都官郎中讳霖之长女，太常博士讳参之冢妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209673_comment'></div>其先杭州钱塘人，都官徙常之晋陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209673_comment'></div>夫人幼警慧，古今文章历耳辄成诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209673_comment'></div>都官未有子，夫人率其妹供子职甚谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209673_comment'></div>都官贤之，以归下蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209673_comment'></div>下蔡失所恃，弟妹多未龀，夫人一一调护，至于冠昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209673_comment'></div>门内之事，大者禀命，小者专达，靡不如太常意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209673_comment'></div>太常用是徇国忘家，以显名于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209673_comment'></div>下蔡既倦游，语夫人曰：「吾将归佚故乡，能安之否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209673_comment'></div>夫人曰：「君安，无不安者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209673_comment'></div>下蔡以故勇退就閒，逍遥声利之外，二十年如一日，未尝悔往慨不遇，惟训诲子孙而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209673_comment'></div>子男四人，申锡、峙、屿、申伯，皆举进士，申锡、峙尤以文学知名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209673_comment'></div>峙登第历官，一时公卿争挽致之，不克用以卒，终衢州西安县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209673_comment'></div>女三人，适进士李亘、胡元均、霍端辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209673_comment'></div>孙男十三人，平、寔、彦、宇、宙、完、寓、章、寅、宽、宰、宋，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209673_comment'></div>仲平登第，为高邮主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209673_comment'></div>寔以特起赐第郓州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209673_comment'></div>女十三人，长适进士周咸，次王临，次继咸室，次王履、邹语、周先，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209673_comment'></div>曾孙十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209673_comment'></div>夫人老矣，四子皆前逝，孙彦、宇亦夭逝，闻者不堪其忧，而夫人安之若命，泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209673_comment'></div>晚年不复省家事，惟岁时祭享，必纤悉阅视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209673_comment'></div>或以劝止，则曰「先实临之，安敢怠」，夫人贤德盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209673_comment'></div>状已，寔持以来，且曰：「夫人顾言曰『吾铭当属吾侄浩』，敢请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209673_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209673_comment'></div>浩之先君朝奉既不幸矣，姑尚无恙，可以慰罔极之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209673_comment'></div>今亦不幸矣，又属铭，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209673_comment'></div>于是雪涕而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209673_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1209673'>都官之女，太常之妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209673_comment'></div>媲德下蔡，卒为贤母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209673_comment'></div>八十有二，其身则寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209673_comment'></div>其子则否，不称其有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209673_comment'></div>不在其子，必在其孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209673_comment'></div>轩轩既翮，既翮而骞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209673_comment'></div>动惟时矣，聿傅于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209673_comment'></div>有丰其碑，有穹其龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209673_comment'></div>闯于高松，潜德光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209673_comment'></div>尚其有诗，配此铭词。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1209673_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　居乡。寻叙复宣德郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　居乡。是年，有与钱弱翁论春秋书。<div id='poem_1209430' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209430' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209430?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与钱弱翁论春秋书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209430")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209430_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209430'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209430'>浩愚且陋，且两窜炎荒，困于瘴疠之侵凌，曩时好书之心薾然怠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209430_comment'></div>比蒙上圣宥以生还，戴恩奉亲之外，得从乡先生长者游，庶几因此复自勉于万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209430_comment'></div>敢谓左右推与过当，不俟再见，即以所著《春秋传例》告焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209430_comment'></div>继宠以书，以《总例》五篇示之，使由此以知述作旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209430_comment'></div>不胜幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209430_comment'></div>不胜幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209430_comment'></div>夫经有《春秋》，犹天下之春秋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209430_comment'></div>天以春生，以秋成，而万物由之以各正性命，至于今未尝已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209430_comment'></div>《春秋》果废乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209430_comment'></div>世人之类多致疑于其书，而不知君君、臣臣、父父、子子自名分以来，莫或可紊者，乃是《春秋》之实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209430_comment'></div>左右独得孔子之志于意诚心正之中，操以验诸儒之说，其孰得孰失，既已判别如白黑在前，又从而去取，以辅成《传例》，且曰「天既不复再生孔子，《传例》虽成，岂敢必望有知我者」，是左右之所以自任者如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209430_comment'></div>又曰「未死之前，决须上进，未敢以全帙示人，恐贻不敬之讥」，且左右之所尊君者又如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209430_comment'></div>然则《春秋》大法之所在，左右非直言之，实行之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209430_comment'></div>浩何幸，乃获受赐于今日以自幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209430_comment'></div>本欲造门拜谢，偶亲宾继至，及少休，复苦足疮，以故悃愊之情不免藉毫楮以彻听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209430_comment'></div>惟高明亮之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1209430_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1110')">1109-1110年</a>　居乡。有铭文。作品：李季侔墓志铭(李畸)华世衡墓志铭(华仲平)德兴县君曾氏墓志铭(曾德克)<div id='poem_1209663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李季侔墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观三年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209663")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209663'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209663'>季侔，予友也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209663_comment'></div>熙宁中，今衢州西安县丞、文林郎詹抃成老方以通经为乡党师，予与季侔从焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209663_comment'></div>季侔尚少，已知夙夜自力，为起家之计，成老每每叹誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209663_comment'></div>闻者或谓季侔之亲轻财赴急，屡脱人于艰危，阴德所钟，其由此而显乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209663_comment'></div>予出游四方，久且三十年，而季侔布衣试有司犹弗偶，然其志益坚，其学益进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209663_comment'></div>购求群书，惟恐后时，所聚万馀卷，博览者资焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209663_comment'></div>尝曰：「遗子黄金满籯，不如一经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209663_comment'></div>亲既以是遗我，我复以是遗子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209663_comment'></div>子子孙孙，用之不竭，况万卷之多乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209663_comment'></div>庶知我之富者在此而不在彼也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209663_comment'></div>尝由族属达于里闾，周其窘穷而任其婚姻丧葬之事，往往讳不自言，尤为先生长者所称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209663_comment'></div>大观二年，年方四十七，奄以十一月丙辰卒于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209663_comment'></div>悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209663_comment'></div>季侔，字也，讳畸，实李氏，常州晋陵人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209663_comment'></div>曾大父振，大父宿，父选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209663_comment'></div>妻裴氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209663_comment'></div>男三人，长曰元善，尝中上舍选，盖将贡以入官以成先志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209663_comment'></div>次曰元美，曰元绍，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209663_comment'></div>女八人，长适登仕郎、辟雍直学施坰，次适登仕郎、婺州兰溪县主簿蒋璨，假将仕郎邵罴，太庙斋郎霍端本，次在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209663_comment'></div>其弟圳与元善卜以三年九月壬寅葬于晋陵县万安东乡之采菱埭，念所以诒后人者，乃泣以见属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209663_comment'></div>于是序而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209663_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1209663'>士方奋于庠序，孰蔽之弗使与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209663_comment'></div>世方跻于仁寿，孰啬之弗使久？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209663_comment'></div>尚其有书，充塞栋宇，承以勿忘，其昌孰御。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1209663_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华世衡墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观三年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209659")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209659'>君华氏，讳仲平，字世衡，常州武进人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209659_comment'></div>曾祖参，太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209659_comment'></div>祖直渊，寿州下蔡主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209659_comment'></div>父申锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209659_comment'></div>先世以来，积习为善，仕者多显于朝，居者能富其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209659_comment'></div>至君之父，益与诸弟问学有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209659_comment'></div>弟峙既登第寖用，则曰足以慰吾心矣，可以行吾志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209659_comment'></div>晨昏馀隙，教子以嗣其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209659_comment'></div>君退然季孟之间，似不能言者，然心敏力勤，日久功倍，遂登元符三年进士第，授广德军广德主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209659_comment'></div>就职未几，丁祖母夫人邹氏忧，服除，授将仕郎、高邮军高邮主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209659_comment'></div>郡守、部使者交荐，秩满，迁通仕郎、郑州荥泽令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209659_comment'></div>自京得疾，归数月而卒，大观二年八月五日也，享年四十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209659_comment'></div>娶丁氏，男耸尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209659_comment'></div>女四，长适进士沈执权，馀在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209659_comment'></div>母夫人陈氏老矣，方赖君以养而君卒矣，少妻幼子拥持夫人，相与恸哭，昼夜不休，吊者沾襟，闻者酸鼻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209659_comment'></div>越明年，弟章奉母夫人命，以十一月二十日葬于武进县怀德北乡郭庄之原下蔡墓之西北百馀步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209659_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1209659'>母发皤然，子形眇然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209659_comment'></div>君归九原，呜呼何言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1209659_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>德兴县君曾氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209674")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209674'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209674'>台州天台县令王君讳无咎之夫人德兴县君南丰曾氏，讳德克，字淑珍，赠太师、沂国公仁旺之曾孙，尚书户部郎中、直史馆、赠太师、密国公致尧之孙，太常博士，赠太师、鲁国公易占之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209674_comment'></div>既笄而嫁，嫁九年而嫠，嫠四十年，年六十九，大观二年五月乙丑终于润州其子之官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209674_comment'></div>以仲兄、丞相布之恩赐冠帔、封邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209674_comment'></div>子男二人：絪，通仕郎、杭州仁和县丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209674_comment'></div>缊，文林郎、润州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209674_comment'></div>女二人，长适朝奉郎、国子司业朱京，次适通仕郎、建昌军南丰县丞杨概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209674_comment'></div>孙男三人，女三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209674_comment'></div>夫人性庄重，又积习家法，故自处以至于行，自幼以至于老，内外宗党为女、为妇与为母者咸取则焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209674_comment'></div>丧父方八岁，哀慕已如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209674_comment'></div>及归王氏，能安其贫而相以义，天台用是弃官，潜心著书立言，为世大儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209674_comment'></div>天台没，四顾无所托，乃携诸子依于仲兄，训诲抚存，顷息弗怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209674_comment'></div>久之，男克登第，女得所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209674_comment'></div>男皆以文行知名，且将光显于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209674_comment'></div>王氏烝尝几绝矣，至是复继而滋丰，夫人力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209674_comment'></div>呜呼，贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209674_comment'></div>初，丞相与弟翰林学士肇居于润，皆久疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209674_comment'></div>俄而学士疾革，丞相闻之，一恸而薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209674_comment'></div>学士旋少间，闻丞相薨，亦一恸莫救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209674_comment'></div>相去裁一日，盖大观元年八月乙卯、丙辰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209674_comment'></div>识者固已叹二公友悌诚笃不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209674_comment'></div>后一年，夫人随其子官于润州，及境，亟往哭之，亦一恸不挟日而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209674_comment'></div>识者又知夫人之贤无愧乎兄弟如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209674_comment'></div>絪、缊卜以四年正月己酉葬于建昌军南城县可封乡松溪之原，相与泣血述夫人之行，属浩为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209674_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1209674'>曾氏之先，参游圣门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209674_comment'></div>门人三千，特以孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209674_comment'></div>由元逮西，有远其裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209674_comment'></div>笃于亲亲，岂惟男子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209674_comment'></div>猗欤夫人，自幼则然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209674_comment'></div>从而有行，咸以为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209674_comment'></div>既成其夫，亦显其嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209674_comment'></div>我心不忘，念我兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209674_comment'></div>一恸而绝，如弟如兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209674_comment'></div>与古列女，凛其同声。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1209674_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年2月</a>　居乡。公弟至明卒，公为志铭。作品：至明弟墓志铭(邹洞)<div id='poem_1209665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>至明弟墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209665")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209665'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209665'>君讳洞，字至明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209665_comment'></div>上世盖杭州钱塘人，曾祖随伯祖贾为广东转运使而卒，葬于荆门，先祖乃卜常州居焉，今为常州晋陵人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209665_comment'></div>先考有子六人，君次余为第二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209665_comment'></div>自儿童时即能致曲以事父母，少与余皆从师读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209665_comment'></div>予既出仕，诸弟游学，君遂不复应科举，曰：「我当专省定，以安兄弟之心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209665_comment'></div>故予与诸弟去亲侧久至四五年，近犹一二年，而君独未尝离左右，油油翼翼，声柔色怡，惟恐丝毫忤亲意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209665_comment'></div>予顷缘罪戾窜斥湖边，君时已感风痹二年矣，初不自忧，特为余深忧，发尽白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209665_comment'></div>其天性孝友盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209665_comment'></div>建中靖国元年，予方贰天官，遇郊祀恩，奏君为假承务郎，以疾不能赴调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209665_comment'></div>后八年，疾复作，奄忽而逝，实大观四年二月二十有一日，享年四十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209665_comment'></div>吾母安康郡太君张氏哭之甚哀，闻者泫然叹曰：「善人遽尔乎，乃俾高年之亲痛念至此耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209665_comment'></div>曾祖讳元庆，东头供奉官、阁门祗候，赠左屯卫大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209665_comment'></div>祖讳霖，尚书都官郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209665_comment'></div>考讳戬，广济军录事参军，赠朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209665_comment'></div>妻张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209665_comment'></div>男枢，举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209665_comment'></div>以其年四月五日葬君于晋陵县德泽乡之林庄先祖墓之东北二百步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209665_comment'></div>于是涕泣作铭，纳之圹中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209665_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1209665'>才也遏之，弗猷弗为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209665_comment'></div>寿也啬之，弗艾弗耆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209665_comment'></div>其谁已之，莫得而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209665_comment'></div>有子颀颀，奋于书诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209665_comment'></div>君子不亡，庶其在兹。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1209665_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年4月</a>　居乡。公有祭弟志明文。作品：祭至明弟。<div id='poem_1209699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭至明弟文<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209699")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209699'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209699'>维大观四年岁次庚寅四月己巳朔初四日壬申，兄具位某与弟洞、沼、况等，以清酌庶羞致祭于亡弟承务之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209699_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209699_comment'></div>先考弃诸孤，久已十五年，而痛念罔极，赖以自慰者，兄弟无故而已，孰谓尔奄忽至此极邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209699_comment'></div>老母在堂，左右奉承，方且兄弟同之，孰谓尔又遽不与邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209699_comment'></div>尔孝弟著于闺门，忠信推于朋友，恭谦和厚，见称于州闾，神宜听之，介以远福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209699_comment'></div>而乃位不正于九品，年不满于五十，果孰使之然邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209699_comment'></div>呜呼已矣，尚何言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209699_comment'></div>今日癸酉，将举尔柩葬于德泽乡林庄之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209699_comment'></div>前视先茔，裁二百步，惟祖惟考，尔其往从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209699_comment'></div>若夫尔之子，犹吾子也，教之诲之，以成尔志，以无忝于尔后，则吾以为己任焉，固可以无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209699_comment'></div>惟终天永诀，痛切心腑，不胜骨肉之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209699_comment'></div>尚享！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1209699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　居乡。有铭文。作品：姚君墓志铭(姚仲达)夫人臧氏墓志铭(姚棐忱妻)夫人葛氏墓志铭(葛瑜女、胡远妻)孙叔权墓志铭(孙握)寿昌县太君严氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1209661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209661?labeling=true' target='_blank'>姚君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209661")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209661_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209661'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209661'>元丰初，余与今通仕郎、新抚州金溪县令姚天迪棐忱同在太学，见其夙夜经史中，略不以家为念，问之则曰：「我弟仲达字子上，有才善干，顺适亲心无不至，我所以安于此者，以其足赖也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209661_comment'></div>后二十年，天迪尚未第，意其倦不复出，然方且汲汲科举如晚辈少年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209661_comment'></div>问之则曰：「欲罢数矣，仲达每涕泣而言：『独不念先人属兄以起家之意乎，奈何辄已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209661_comment'></div>家事无细大，仲达身任之，兄但努力为门户计』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209661_comment'></div>我以是不敢不勉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209661_comment'></div>又数年间，天迪登第，得目疾，甚异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209661_comment'></div>及见而问其故，即曰：「仲达缘家事数遭祸患，皆人所不能堪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209661_comment'></div>虽其心不以为苦，然我不胜痛愤，泣泪尽而致此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209661_comment'></div>今年春，天迪调官还，过常州，会余方遭仲弟丧，而天迪亦适闻其弟危疾，仓黄亟去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209661_comment'></div>既而书来，则曰到家仲达已前卒，实大观四年正月四日也，享年五十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209661_comment'></div>娶黄氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209661_comment'></div>子男三人，蒧、葵、策，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209661_comment'></div>女一人，归王邦宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209661_comment'></div>孙男、女四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209661_comment'></div>卜以其年九月十七日葬于剡金牛之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209661_comment'></div>念其平生以从兄奉亲故屡投身几死之地不惮，乡里叹以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209661_comment'></div>比年芝生于书楼，又生于堂庑，闻者皆以为孝友深笃所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209661_comment'></div>今不幸死矣，苟无以发扬，则何以慰泉下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209661_comment'></div>又念分好不以穷通改易，久而弥厚者莫如我友，乃不远千里走隶人，持行状踵余门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209661_comment'></div>余不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209661_comment'></div>惟姚氏世为越州剡县人，仲达之曾祖文玘、祖德荣、父延祐，皆有潜德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209661_comment'></div>延祐生三子，长曰仲堪，尝以文学荐，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209661_comment'></div>次即棐忱、仲达也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209661_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1209661'>瘠其身以肥家，残其身以成兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209661_comment'></div>岂其身不足顾惜乎，盖不敢忘先志而规自宁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209661_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209661_comment'></div>惟天矜之后人兴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1209661_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夫人臧氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209676")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209676'>夫人臧氏，世为越州山阴人，尝嫁而孀居，后乃归今通仕郎、新抚州金溪县令姚君棐忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209676_comment'></div>金溪有男七人，苄、薄、芝、华皆举进士，䔇、藙、苕尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209676_comment'></div>女三人，长适钱宋臣，次适陆宁，次适归宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209676_comment'></div>夫人各随其分，极意调护如己出，诸子安之，悉如前母无恙时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209676_comment'></div>金溪与弟仲达相视如左右手，父母既殁，同心协力，久益坚确。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209676_comment'></div>夫人奉此意以周旋，惟恐不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209676_comment'></div>仲达每窘于官，即出奁中物以脱其艰危，无吝色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209676_comment'></div>及其得疾以至不幸，适金溪赴调未归，所以处医药、办丧事、恤其娣而祔其孤，凡惊扰之际，男子所难勉者，靡不曲尽勤诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209676_comment'></div>金溪归，叹曰：「使我自竭，不过如此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209676_comment'></div>其家方赖以肃睦，而奄以大观四年九月十五日感疾卒，盖归金溪之四年也，享年三十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209676_comment'></div>将以其年九月十七日葬于剡之九里原，来求铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209676_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1209676'>甫闺门兮四年，俄兆域兮九里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209676_comment'></div>惟暂留兮亟往，果孰使兮如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209676_comment'></div>泽不泯兮杯棬，采复遵兮沼沚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209676_comment'></div>独冥冥兮难追，感夫子兮曷已！</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1209676_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夫人葛氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209675")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209675'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209675'>夫人葛氏，其先广陵人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209675_comment'></div>杨行密乱江淮，高祖徙居江阴，今为常州江阴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209675_comment'></div>曾祖鄘、祖惟则、父瑜，世以赀高一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209675_comment'></div>夫人生最盛时，而谨约柔顺，不啻寒家子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209675_comment'></div>年十四失所怙，事母张氏以孝闻，外祖光禄卿铸尤爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209675_comment'></div>会今朝散大夫致仕胡公远方择伉俪，于是夫人归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209675_comment'></div>舅正议公既殁，姑和义郡太君虞氏在堂，聚族众，贫甚，夫人罄奁中物以裕其谋，无吝色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209675_comment'></div>和义有痼疾，夫人侍左右十馀年，药饵不经心，手不以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209675_comment'></div>一日疾遽革，大夫随檄未还，夫人哀号之外，区处丧事，靡不周尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209675_comment'></div>长女甫嫁，大夫被旨出，婿自数千里来，势不得款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209675_comment'></div>时慈圣光献皇后山陵未祔，法家谓婚姻初无禁文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209675_comment'></div>夫人曰纵于文无害，理有未安，执不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209675_comment'></div>已而果有虞祭之限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209675_comment'></div>其遇事类如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209675_comment'></div>大夫自壮以至归，居家奉亲、友诸弟，当官夙夜不顾，和义退安里门，逍遥于风埃之表，五十年间，人无间言，繄夫人辅佐力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209675_comment'></div>诸子笃志学问，宣力郡邑，为士民叹誉，乡人称愿焉，亦夫人有以助成之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209675_comment'></div>大观三年冬得疾，十月十八日晏然而逝，享年七十一，以大夫恩封永康县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209675_comment'></div>子男五人：长曰聿，承直郎、知建昌军南城县事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209675_comment'></div>次曰津，通仕郎、行台州司法参军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209675_comment'></div>次曰𦘗，曰建，曰律，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209675_comment'></div>女四人，长适知荆门军当阳县丞黄熙，次适进士谢景平，次适西头供奉官、监磁州固镇杨应律，次适进士唐实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209675_comment'></div>孙男、女十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209675_comment'></div>卜以四年九月二十日葬于武进县怀德南乡之永安庄正议茔之西北二十步，大夫属其甥文林郎、知泗州录事参军张晬状夫人行实，而以浩辱在亲好，属为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209675_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1209675'>法度是循，鸤鸠其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209675_comment'></div>歌于《国风》，允为内则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209675_comment'></div>得之自天，聿追古昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209675_comment'></div>有如夫人，柔顺均一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209675_comment'></div>知进知止，克相以义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209675_comment'></div>或仕或处，率成以理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209675_comment'></div>令妻寿母，亶其受祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209675_comment'></div>我铭不诬，昭于曷已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1209675_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙叔权墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209662")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209662'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209662'>君孙氏，讳握，字叔权，世为常州晋陵人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209662_comment'></div>曾祖世南兄弟六人皆有声场屋，同时荐礼部者四人，自后子孙相继以进士起家，祖式独隐居不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209662_comment'></div>父谊，资州龙水县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209662_comment'></div>有四子，君为第三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209662_comment'></div>龙水捐馆，时君才十三岁，已能自立如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209662_comment'></div>外祖湖州德清县令徐良佐以能诗名江左，每过君家，有所咏歌，君辄私属其韵，德清叹誉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209662_comment'></div>及长，笃志问学，数试有司不偶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209662_comment'></div>或勉以不若治生事，君曰「奈何废箕裘之绪耶」，益自奋不怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209662_comment'></div>君天资沈静，未尝妄笑语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209662_comment'></div>居家事母，从兄友弟，与乡里亲朋周旋，靡不得其欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209662_comment'></div>当利害相摩之际，它人往往愤形色词，君独逊顺而已，众尤以为难及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209662_comment'></div>大观四年三月二十六日遇疾，二十八日卒于家，享年四十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209662_comment'></div>娶钱氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209662_comment'></div>三男，公发、公才、公美，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209662_comment'></div>四女，皆未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209662_comment'></div>卜以其年十月十四日葬于武进县后暑村先茔之右，其弟秉以母兄之意求予铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209662_comment'></div>予与叔权亲好甚厚，不相见才十许日而叔权逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209662_comment'></div>今乃为之铭，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209662_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1209662'>其容漠然，如不能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209662_comment'></div>其心皎然，不以利迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209662_comment'></div>后暑之原，奄从其先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209662_comment'></div>其后则延，何有穷年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1209662_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寿昌县太君严氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209678")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209678'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209678'>夫人严氏，其先成都人，后因宦游，徙贯姑苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209678_comment'></div>曾祖谏，尚书虞部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209678_comment'></div>祖颖，职方郎中、京东路转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209678_comment'></div>父孟坚，衡州军事判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209678_comment'></div>母甄氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209678_comment'></div>夫人甫笄，归毗陵张公次元，继其室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209678_comment'></div>公之父天章阁待制温之与其侄太常少卿铸同时以光禄卿老于里第，号为二卿，其族甚盛，然上下内外靡不以夫人为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209678_comment'></div>公自大理寺丞积官至朝请郎，自监楚州粮料历任至提点铸钱，出处进退，事多故矣，初不少贬，以追时好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209678_comment'></div>山阳徐先生积考公所尚，以谓有志于古之所谓刚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209678_comment'></div>夫人休戚同焉，盖三十年，未尝有一毫动公念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209678_comment'></div>公之姊妹皆丧夫，子幼，公取以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209678_comment'></div>夫人待遇之甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209678_comment'></div>家事禀而后行，择名士以嫁其女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209678_comment'></div>比夫人不幸，其女号赴，若丧所亲，曰恨无以报德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209678_comment'></div>判官既没，即迎继母张氏，竭力致养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209678_comment'></div>张临终曰：「吾死于此无憾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209678_comment'></div>提点既葬，携诸孤还里第问学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209678_comment'></div>有客造门，必询贤否，诚贤即纵从之游，促家人为具，笑语异常日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209678_comment'></div>喜《长庆集》，几成诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209678_comment'></div>爱泉石，不乐世荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209678_comment'></div>尝中秋为歌词示子孙，其所称慕，乃陶渊明、白乐天而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209678_comment'></div>元丰、元祐间，释氏禅家盛东南，士女纷造席下，往往空闺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209678_comment'></div>夫人闻之，戒家人曰：「苟尽妇道，即契佛心，安用从彼扰扰邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209678_comment'></div>疾革，命子孙诸妇环坐食芡实，既而曰：「且静，我当去」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209678_comment'></div>语绝瞑目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209678_comment'></div>子妇遽起呼问，则已逝矣，大观四年八月十六日也，享年七十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209678_comment'></div>初封华阳县君，后改封寿昌县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209678_comment'></div>子男八人，长基，通直郎，前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209678_comment'></div>次坚，通仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209678_comment'></div>次如晦、墀、垂、牧、埙、睿，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209678_comment'></div>女三人，长适进士方希纯，次适宣德郎吕切问，次适承事郎崔颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209678_comment'></div>孙男十二人，铎、鉴、錞、锡、銶、铢、锷、镈、钟、钺、锴、锜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209678_comment'></div>女七人，长适进士谢亮，次适假将仕郎周鉴，次许将仕郎毕知微，次许进士石公骐，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209678_comment'></div>曾孙男一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209678_comment'></div>以其年十月丁酉祔丧于滁州清流县昌城乡安仁村提点之兆，状其行属铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209678_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209678_comment'></div>夫人于外孙中眷浩特异，浩顷得罪窜岭表，亲戚朋旧不复顾省，甚者闻姓字而掩耳，过门巷而障面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209678_comment'></div>夫人独数数到吾家，拊存吾母，倍于平日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209678_comment'></div>又命诸子遗书问劳不绝，所以勤恤瘴疠窘穷之时，略不以祸福摇夺其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209678_comment'></div>疾且革矣，闻浩至前，犹忍呻吟之声，从容慰谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209678_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209678_comment'></div>无复报德之日矣，敢不勉次遗事而为之铭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209678_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1209678'>惟柔承刚严济恩，夫功显白子行称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209678_comment'></div>华阳寿昌袭光荣，䌽衣交焕兰膳馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209678_comment'></div>诜诜奕奕嬉曾孙，一方矜叹五福膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209678_comment'></div>可山环滁高且清，奄忽从公閟佳城，庆流厥后当弥兴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1209678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年11月</a>　郊赦改元，特复直龙图阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年11月20日</a>　居乡，有文。作品：跋陈居士传后。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《跋陈居士传》载：“居士本无求知于人，人自知之。宗子博士杨公中立又为之传以行于世，所以风劝來者，盖不但一乡而已也。大观四年十一月二十日，晋陵邹浩既篆其前已，因书此以见意云。”）</span><div id='poem_1209520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋陈居士传后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年11月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209520")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209520'>居士本无求知于人，人自知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209520_comment'></div>宗子博士杨公中立又为之传以行于世，所以风劝来者，盖不但一乡而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209520_comment'></div>大观四年十一月二十日，晋陵邹浩既篆其前已，因书此以见意云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1209520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1111')">1110-1111年</a>　居乡，有铭文。作品：孙明远墓志铭(孙邈)高平县太君范氏墓志铭(范仲温女、周师厚妻)<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》第一三一册--第一三二册卷二八四七题下注“政和元年十月”，此时作者已卒，记载似有误，谨系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1209660' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209660' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209660?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙明远墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209660")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209660_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209660'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209660'>晋陵孙姓多大族，居南郭之外者特以儒显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209660_comment'></div>自朝请伯仲以文学登科，子孙承之，益奋励为名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209660_comment'></div>君朝请长子也，天资庄重，甫五岁，对所尊言，必称名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209660_comment'></div>既学，即忘寝食寒暑，穷昼夜以自力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209660_comment'></div>每开卷，先盥手，净几格，正冠衣，俨然如侍圣贤而承训诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209660_comment'></div>自少至长，初不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209660_comment'></div>以故读书甚博，造理甚深，发为词章，咸有典则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209660_comment'></div>晋陵当熙宁改科之初，邵公刚试于南宫，余公中试于大廷，皆为第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209660_comment'></div>后者慕之，士风寖盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209660_comment'></div>迨绍圣乡举之秋，应诏而起者几二千人，君褎然为举者，誉问辉赫，乡先生有送以诗者，期君追继余、邵二公之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209660_comment'></div>然蹭蹬久不偶，乃以朝请谢事恩授太庙斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209660_comment'></div>试吏部高等，授将仕郎、湖州安吉主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209660_comment'></div>邑大事剧，君以廉恪协赞令治，部使者交荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209660_comment'></div>遇八宝恩，就迁通仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209660_comment'></div>秩满，监泗州军资库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209660_comment'></div>时朝请七十六岁矣，君方待次，日率子弟奉承左右，欢声协气，洋溢闺门，乡邦矜式焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209660_comment'></div>孙氏世多寿考，君又孝弟忠信，宜享远福，光显于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209660_comment'></div>大观三年，年方五十六，俄以其夏感疾，以五月九日卒于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209660_comment'></div>前卒一月，奉亲之外不与人接，但斋居焚香诵《华严经》而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209660_comment'></div>秩甫终而疾作，以至瞑目，亦异矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209660_comment'></div>有文集十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209660_comment'></div>君讳邈，字明远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209660_comment'></div>曾祖居约，祖宗修，赠朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209660_comment'></div>父扬休，见以朝请郎致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209660_comment'></div>母王氏，追封崇安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209660_comment'></div>继母施氏，见封德清县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209660_comment'></div>娶姑苏葛氏，子男五人，长曰瑰，常贡于礼部，以文行称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209660_comment'></div>次曰玮，曰琬，曰琰，曰珍，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209660_comment'></div>女四人，长适进士庄安上，次适进士虞颖，次前卒，次尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209660_comment'></div>孙男祖德卜以四年某月某日葬于某县某乡某处，朝请以铭属浩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209660_comment'></div>浩不获辞，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence'
