id='poem_sentence_30_1209660'>有才有志，学以充之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209660_comment'></div>迄于大成，可以有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209660_comment'></div>仕不及显，不行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209660_comment'></div>行于闺门，衣䌽而戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209660_comment'></div>既宁其亲，亦施其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209660_comment'></div>子子孙孙，率循于祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209660_comment'></div>五十有六，寿虽不长，不亡者存，嗣其隆昌。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1209660_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高平县太君范氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209677")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209677'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209677'>夫人范氏，世为苏之吴县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209677_comment'></div>太子中舍仲温之女，资政殿大学士、谥文正公仲淹之侄女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209677_comment'></div>中舍仕未显而逝，文正迎其嫂及诸孤以归，尤器爱夫人，曰异时当为择良婿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209677_comment'></div>其后文正薨，其家追用先意，以夫人嫁四明周公师厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209677_comment'></div>公自衢州西安令改官，由制置条例司即提举湖北常平，迁运判，易湖南，久之，乃通判河南府保州以卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209677_comment'></div>凡三十三年，夫人所以事舅姑、奉祭祀、治家教子，致公仕不顾私，殁无后虑，非特亲戚乡里之所称道，而士大夫籍籍闻之，固亦不可掩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209677_comment'></div>自元祐以来，从兄丞相纯仁、从弟右丞纯礼、龙图阁学士纯粹相继登用，婿陈瓘亦除谏官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209677_comment'></div>有以为夫人贺者，初无喜色，曰：「先文正笃于忠义，亲者尤服其训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209677_comment'></div>吾兄弟、吾婿必以是得之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209677_comment'></div>及皆窜逐，又或以告，夫人无忧色，曰：「吾妇人，不知外事，但各愿其无忘国恩而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209677_comment'></div>子锷尝擢为提举官，罢条一司敕令，未几，又以上书责监泉州税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209677_comment'></div>夫人年高疾久，不可远侍以去，锷不忍离左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209677_comment'></div>夫人戒之曰：「汝罪大责轻，朝廷岂终弃汝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209677_comment'></div>亟行，勿以吾为念」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209677_comment'></div>已而锷果蒙恩得真祠以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209677_comment'></div>居四年，夫人以大观三年八月十日卒于四明之里第，享年七十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209677_comment'></div>初封蓬莱县君，后改封高平县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209677_comment'></div>子男三人：长锷，承议郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209677_comment'></div>次铢，台州黄岩县尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209677_comment'></div>次慧印，从浮屠氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209677_comment'></div>女三人，长适监察御史俞伟，次适奉议郎毛濛，次适宣德郎陈瓘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209677_comment'></div>孙男、女十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209677_comment'></div>以政和元年十月八日葬于通远乡银山管金谷里，祔大夫之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209677_comment'></div>锷与浩亲厚，远以铭见属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209677_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1209677'>惟文正，笃忠义，忘乃身，徇国事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209677_comment'></div>习见闻，逮女子，施于家，率由是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209677_comment'></div>自其夫，暨后嗣，助成之，靡不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209677_comment'></div>要所存，似兄弟，若夫人，可无愧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1209677_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　居乡，瘴疾作，遂不起。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年3月</a>　居乡，有铭文。作品：何继文墓志铭(何武)<div id='poem_1209664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何继文墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209664")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209664'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209664'>前进士何升之将以政和元年三月壬申葬其父于江阴县凤戈乡之由里山，前期，走晋陵，且泣且拜，属某曰：「先人力教升之，冀有成立，崇宁二年春甫赐第，即以封事窜苏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209664_comment'></div>大观四年夏，蒙恩复入官，而先人弃诸孤已九月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209664_comment'></div>升之不孝罪大，惧无以自赎，惟是发扬潜德，为不朽计，尚庶几可以自竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209664_comment'></div>谨持乡丈人陈鼎所为行状请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209664_comment'></div>岂惟升之幸，所以慰冥冥甚厚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209664_comment'></div>浩受而读焉，曰：君讳武，字继文，世为金陵大族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209664_comment'></div>曾祖清，避李氏乱，徙居江阴，今为江阴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209664_comment'></div>祖亢、父咏皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209664_comment'></div>职方郎中徐申天圣中为江阴司理参军，闻咏贤，以妹妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209664_comment'></div>生子五人，君其长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209664_comment'></div>幼好学，能为诗，长益聪敏强记，自五经暨阴阳家说靡不该洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209664_comment'></div>或劝之应举，则曰：「我山林人耳，教子弟以绍先业足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209664_comment'></div>一日戒升之曰：「吾家积德久已累世，必有兴者，其在汝乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209664_comment'></div>勉之勿怠」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209664_comment'></div>升之游太学，较艺常列巍等，声名籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209664_comment'></div>间归省，君遽遣之曰：「勿以吾贫累汝志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209664_comment'></div>升之遂由上舍登进士乙科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209664_comment'></div>贺者盈门，君无喜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209664_comment'></div>及其得罪，唁者既至，君无戚容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209664_comment'></div>未几，恩释升之以归，君亦恬然自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209664_comment'></div>君孝友甚笃，信义甚著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209664_comment'></div>弟尝为姻家所讼，逮捕甚急，君亟诣县，请自对州狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209664_comment'></div>以高年冒大暑，留数月，直其弟而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209664_comment'></div>舅大理寺丞徐信宝卒，贫甚，其子远出，君赡给其家数年，略无倦意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209664_comment'></div>乡人争讼，多取决于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209664_comment'></div>以急难告者，必极力济之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209664_comment'></div>尝得卫生术，平居怡怡，惟以诗酒自适，故年虽高，貌若少壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209664_comment'></div>大观三年秋，忽作诗别家人，后三日而卒，实八月二十七日也，享年七十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209664_comment'></div>娶张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209664_comment'></div>子男三人，长升之，次申之，次仲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209664_comment'></div>女一人，未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209664_comment'></div>孙男、女二人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209664_comment'></div>噫，兹可铭也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209664_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1209664'>峨峨兮里山，渺渺兮江水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209664_comment'></div>兆龟食兮莫违，奄佳城兮在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209664_comment'></div>追厥美兮如纶，恩方来兮未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209664_comment'></div>曷既逝兮不忘，惟承家兮有子。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1209664_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年3月6日</a>　杨龟山先生来省疾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年3月9日</a>　卒于正寝。<br /></div>

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　公十八岁入太学，声誉赫赫然，试每在高等，议论挺特，不逐时好。<br /><a href="javascript: class='label1' id='7f53ce4c176848febe8cb8c3779881c0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7f53ce4c176848febe8cb8c3779881c0");'><span id='7f53ce4c176848febe8cb8c3779881c0_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　在京。赴吏部铨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年4月</a>　在京。有铭文。作品：先贤徐君墓碑记铭。<div id='poem_1209679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先贤徐君墓碑记铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐三年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209679")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209679'>按，先贤徐君与延陵吴季子笔之史者著矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209679_comment'></div>存而国家嗣立，雅道胥匡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209679_comment'></div>殁而生死交情，寤思弥笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209679_comment'></div>两君既往，而剑若长留，此皆千古不泯之人心为之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209679_comment'></div>延陵之北，地去七十里曰申浦，有吴季子墓，孔碑十字，掩映古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209679_comment'></div>延陵之东，地悬十里曰丁堰，亦有徐君墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209679_comment'></div>墓前有祠，祠前有井，井有亭，亭曰剑井亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209679_comment'></div>其后人志所思欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209679_comment'></div>而创立之世系，于今未获悉考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209679_comment'></div>余㦝然吊古，询乃耆英，究诸典册，兹一抔之土，是其始基，不得不为之纪载，贻厥后嗣，永昭世守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209679_comment'></div>从计之地广有三百七十步四尺，横计之有三百五十步，合计之叁亩有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209679_comment'></div>隧路山庭，俨与申浦季墓圣碑两相峙立，岂非天之不泯其迹而为之长存者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209679_comment'></div>又不特人心千古昭然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209679_comment'></div>抑徐君赐履彭城，乃徐州兆域堂皇，松楸郁蔼，而淮之泗州、兖之张秋，更复巍然华表，象冢开阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209679_comment'></div>讵徐氏之子孙繁衍，各宗所自而追崇之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209679_comment'></div>或者古帝王仙圣委席留衣，爪甲发毛封坟掩石？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209679_comment'></div>不可得而详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209679_comment'></div>故为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209679_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1209679'>灵剑常存，荣圭不掩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209679_comment'></div>拱树孤坟，天长地险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209679_comment'></div>帷堂野设，帐殿郊祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209679_comment'></div>土成黼黻，木影龙螭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209679_comment'></div>载拜兴思，如徐及泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209679_comment'></div>血食方来，碑阴永字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209679_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1209679'>元祐三年岁次戊辰清和之吉，延陵后学邹浩撰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209679_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1209679'>此文仅见于地方志，或非浩所作。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1209679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1209679'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_24_1209679_0'>⑴ 道光《武进阳湖合志》卷三四。又见康熙《武进县志》卷三四，康熙《常州府志》卷三六，光绪《武阳志馀》卷四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1209679_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='52aede15231a4615806404082c79a1aa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("52aede15231a4615806404082c79a1aa");'><span id='52aede15231a4615806404082c79a1aa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1093')">1092-1093年</a>，33-34岁</div><div id='52aede15231a4615806404082c79a1aa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年7月</a>　秩满，尚书右仆射苏颂荐除太学博士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年7月</a>　官太学博士。有记。作品：颍学题名记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八四一《颍学题名记》题下注“元祐七年七月”）</span><div id='poem_1209594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颍学题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209594")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209594'>熙宁初，神宗皇帝既以经术迪天下士，遂命学校之在大邦者皆设官教授，且自京东、西、河南、北、陕西五路始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209594_comment'></div>颍昌实京西一都会，于是设官又先于五路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209594_comment'></div>初委国子监推择以闻，又召其所当试者试于礼部，又诏侍从而上各举其所知，又朝廷自拔用其可者，二十年间，无虑四变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209594_comment'></div>诸州或以此阙员不补，独颍昌未尝无人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209594_comment'></div>仆秩满且去，客见属曰：「榱楹一新，简策并集，学者进德肃如也，頖宫制度备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209594_comment'></div>子继其后，盍追载前人之名氏，使久而不忘乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209594_comment'></div>自唐之殿最不行，而教授于群吏中号为无责，刺史莫之问，监司莫之顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209594_comment'></div>不幸官非其实，则偷岁月如传舍，视生徒如路人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209594_comment'></div>甚者忘其布衣之时，而己所不欲，一以施焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209594_comment'></div>士亦失其所习，以其靖恭笃实之姿，荡为轻薄子者有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209594_comment'></div>凡厥父兄，至以学校为不可游处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209594_comment'></div>噫，是果无责也，非邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209594_comment'></div>异日必有按子之所载以指而议者，曰『某人如此，可以为法』，曰『某人如此，可以为戒』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209594_comment'></div>日月逝矣，其得失是非炳炳耳目中，犹足以动来者之心，其为之毋忽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209594_comment'></div>仆竦然对曰：「若仆者，所谓可以为戒者也，然不敢巧自盖藏，以坠前人之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209594_comment'></div>有来者焉，傥因仆言以反诸其身，务称国家所以作人之意，则学者受赐多矣，尚庶几以此自赎于清议云」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209594_comment'></div>元祐七年七月初一日，晋陵邹某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1209594_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年4月</a>　出为襄州州学教授，有谢启。作品：谢改官启。<div id='poem_1209471' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209471' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209471?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢改官启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1093年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209471")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209471_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209471'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209471'>治遇日升，方严于核实；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209471_comment'></div>恩承天施，辄冒于迁官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209471_comment'></div>还视阙然，倍增惕若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209471_comment'></div>伏念某江湖冷族，冠剑鲰生，夙尘俊造之科，旋辱师儒之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209471_comment'></div>十年外部，专泮水以横经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209471_comment'></div>弥岁中都，分胶庠而授业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209471_comment'></div>空有惭于名教，初无补于人材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209471_comment'></div>宜触明刑，以惩尸禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209471_comment'></div>昨者乃缘异意，聿起烦言，致御史之交攻，动朝廷而耸听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209471_comment'></div>许还旧物，方仰戴于深仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209471_comment'></div>祸作私门，忽上延于所怙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209471_comment'></div>比终丧祭，偶尚生存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209471_comment'></div>顾亲养之弗充，敢里居而自必？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209471_comment'></div>勉扶羸惫，祗赴铨衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209471_comment'></div>矧逢休运之隆，丕复元丰之制，阶分既除于左右，次待仍革于期年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209471_comment'></div>苟逃指摘之严，极遂升选之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209471_comment'></div>岂伊品下，亦在数中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209471_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官道协圣神，勋昭夷夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209471_comment'></div>谓太平之急务，莫若登贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209471_comment'></div>付万有于公心，必先举类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209471_comment'></div>用笃一人之庆，永流四国之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209471_comment'></div>曾是吹嘘，误尝假借，遂致汪洋之泽，概沾蹇浅之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209471_comment'></div>敢不务对生成，力图报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209471_comment'></div>招不来而麾不去，或无歉于清时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209471_comment'></div>用则行而舍则藏，庶有几于吾道。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1209471_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='350b1f23ada34171a37e89b17341ecee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("350b1f23ada34171a37e89b17341ecee");'><span id='350b1f23ada34171a37e89b17341ecee_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1099')">1098-1099年</a>，39-40岁</div><div id='350b1f23ada34171a37e89b17341ecee' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年10月</a>　丁父保之公忧，解官居制。有铭文。作品：李府君墓志铭(李恕)<div id='poem_1209648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李府君墓铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣五年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209648")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209648'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209648'>赵郡李友直伯益与其弟友谅仲益、友闻季益皆以文雅知名，号为三益，余心向之有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209648_comment'></div>后与季益同登进士第，又与仲益同官于襄阳，始深得其为人，盖词学趋向荦荦可畏而不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209648_comment'></div>余虽未识府君，固知善庆之所钟，义方之所成，此其效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209648_comment'></div>是时季益奉府君为岳州沅江令，秩满，仲益迎侍以还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209648_comment'></div>余适祸归，不及见，但闻幅巾杖履，历防昔人之遗踪，上下山谷，步履轻疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209648_comment'></div>襄人初不知其为八十岁老人也，莫不叹仰，以为福禄未艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209648_comment'></div>然明年，绍圣四年四月丁酉，府君逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209648_comment'></div>诸孤护丧至杭州，卜以五年十月某日葬钱塘县钦贤乡之马鞍山，状其行属余铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209648_comment'></div>夫铭以信天下后世，大事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209648_comment'></div>仲益弟兄声称籍籍，所与游皆当世名卿大夫，不以是托焉而属于余，余曷敢辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209648_comment'></div>于是叙而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209648_comment'></div>君讳恕，字贯道，世为开封酸枣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209648_comment'></div>至君葬亲于白兆山，遂为安州安陆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209648_comment'></div>曾祖弼、祖德升皆晦迹丘园，以经术教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209648_comment'></div>考某始以进士起家，而守正不屈，阨于小官，最后为随州随县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209648_comment'></div>守将欲以荐状易其善马，毅然谢曰：「马久劳之，不忍中弃，迁官不愿也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209648_comment'></div>未几，投劾去以卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209648_comment'></div>君天资笃实，口无二言，其德似之，故能以终鲜之孤克成其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209648_comment'></div>方十许岁，族人有不得意于长上者规欲害其所爱之提孩，念莫能致，则以毒药授君曰：「夜卧，密置其口中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209648_comment'></div>君受药惟谨，比入门即弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209648_comment'></div>如是三四，族人验其不为用，引它事棰苦之，君终不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209648_comment'></div>它日，内外稍有知之者，相与叹曰：「是儿有阴德，讵可量耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209648_comment'></div>君少嗜学，于书无所不窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209648_comment'></div>既孤，不复事科举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209648_comment'></div>逮有子，秀拔绝人，顾可以成其志，即千里资遣以从师友，虽贫甚不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209648_comment'></div>已而二子相继登第，迎君宦游殆十五年，所以奉养甚适，人士荣之，且曰为善之报不在其身而在其子孙果如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209648_comment'></div>夫人朱氏，安州落雁太傅之裔，前君七年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209648_comment'></div>君今葬所，即其兆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209648_comment'></div>子男三人，即友直、友谅、友闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209648_comment'></div>友谅，宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209648_comment'></div>友闻，集庆军节度推官、知唐州湖阳县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209648_comment'></div>女二人，长适赠宣义郎刘兴宗，次适西头供奉官刘震，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209648_comment'></div>孙男十四人，彦开<span class='inlineComment2'>（馀无考）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209648_comment'></div>女十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209648_comment'></div>重孙男一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209648_comment'></div>君于五福备矣，可以无憾，惟潜德隐行不与耳目期者，世岂得而尽识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209648_comment'></div>然推其十许岁用心，则老而弥邵可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209648_comment'></div>故于其属纩也，言语气色如常日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209648_comment'></div>于其丧之至也，杭人识与不识为之咨嗟出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209648_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1209648'>曰高匪天，曰厚匪地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209648_comment'></div>方寸之间，天地所寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209648_comment'></div>有如府君，孰使而然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209648_comment'></div>受药即弃，见于童年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209648_comment'></div>笃于初心，以壮以老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209648_comment'></div>如有萌焉，至于合抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209648_comment'></div>天地知之，显相其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209648_comment'></div>其身弗有，蔚其后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209648_comment'></div>八十一年，数则有尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209648_comment'></div>有子如此，无穷之庆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1209648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　服阙，改宣德郎，召对，除右正言，具状谢。不允。作品：辞免右正言。<span class='inlineComment2'>（公为教授时，吕申公公著为守，命公撰乐语，不可。申公曰：“使教授他时作翰林学士，如之何？”答曰：“为翰林学士则可，为祭酒司业则不可。”吕后首荐之。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在右正言职。请审察壅蔽。作品：请审察壅蔽疏。<div id='poem_1209376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请审察壅蔽疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209376")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209376'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209376'>臣闻君尊如天，臣卑如地，天地之气交然后足以全万物之生，君臣之情通然后足以隆四海之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209376_comment'></div>臣伏睹皇帝陛下躬揽机政以来，自左右辅弼之外，其因职而请对、因举而赐对者悉皆从容访问，尽其所言，君臣之情固已通而无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209376_comment'></div>然过是以往，窃虑其间不得上达尚多有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209376_comment'></div>臣愿陛下审察壅蔽之端，推广听纳之路，使四方万里之远无以异于一堂之上，则天下幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209376_comment'></div>天下幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1209376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在右正言职。请令在京官司被受续降条贯指挥，关报门下中书后省。<div id='poem_1209377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请官司被受条贯关报门下、中书后省疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209377")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209377'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209377'>伏以设官之方，虽台官主于纠劾，谏官主于献纳，大率皆是以言为职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209377_comment'></div>然而谏官比之台官，除省曹依条合行关报事件外，其馀并不预闻，虽或闻之外议，又缘取索诸处文字不得，无由考实，难以论列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209377_comment'></div>臣窃见御吏台昨因奏乞在京官司被受朝旨并依元丰四年以前指挥关报本台，至元符元年八月五日奉圣旨，依所见立法施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209377_comment'></div>伏望睿慈特赐详酌，令在京官司今后被受一司续降条贯及一时指挥，亦依关报御史台法关报门下、中书后省谏官案，所贵事得周知，可以论列，上副陛下虚怀听纳之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1209377_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在右正言职。有铭文。作品：华元吉墓志铭（华申锡）<div id='poem_1209649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华元吉墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209649")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209649'>君华氏，讳申锡，字元吉，世为常州武进人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209649_comment'></div>曾大父宏，赠大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209649_comment'></div>大父参，故太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209649_comment'></div>父直渊，故寿州下蔡县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209649_comment'></div>下蔡君有子四人，君其长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209649_comment'></div>禀赋纯笃，表里一如，自其童幼，即喜问学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209649_comment'></div>既长，博通深造，为流辈所推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209649_comment'></div>熙宁以来，朝廷作新人材，尊用经术，炳然与三代同风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209649_comment'></div>而吾乡之士继踵兴起以显赫乎当世者，视天下为最盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209649_comment'></div>君于此时乃累诏不偶，人颇咨惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209649_comment'></div>君不为动，曰：「我知修己而已，以此绍箕裘之业而为子孙亦足矣，它复何憾」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209649_comment'></div>下蔡君久疾卧家，其仲子申甫方擢第仕四方，叔季又从师友读书，独君朝夕侍左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209649_comment'></div>凡可以顺承其意者，虽劳苦之事，勇前不懈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209649_comment'></div>下蔡君既捐馆，母夫人邹氏年益高，君奉养尤竭力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209649_comment'></div>君殁久矣，夫人或事不如意，则必玄然叹曰：「吾儿在，宁有是耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209649_comment'></div>娶陈氏，故尚书屯田郎中傅之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209649_comment'></div>子三人，齐、彦、章，皆笃学有立志，而彦早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209649_comment'></div>君年四十有一，元祐二年五月十五日，以疾卒于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209649_comment'></div>后十有三年，元符元年八月某日，始克葬于武进县怀德北乡某村之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209649_comment'></div>其孤谓予与君亲好隆厚，属铭君墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209649_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1209649'>学以诚其身，孝以悦其亲，谓当获于上以充其志，而迄不伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209649_comment'></div>呜呼已矣，利其后人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1209649_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在右正言职。有行状。作品：故登州防御推官华君行状。<div id='poem_1209644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故登州防御推官华君行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209644")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209644'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209644'>君华氏，讳峙，旧名申甫，元祐初避高鲁王讳改焉，字元翰，世为常州武进人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209644_comment'></div>君天资豪爽，初就外傅诵书，日记数千言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209644_comment'></div>年十四，课试六论，词旨如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209644_comment'></div>既长西游，必与名士为友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209644_comment'></div>会熙宁初罢制举，专以经术取士，君不远数千里谒王文公于金陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209644_comment'></div>公称异之，授以经义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209644_comment'></div>退归，不复茹荤，杜门自饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209644_comment'></div>如是三年而学成，遂登九年进士第，调高州电白县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209644_comment'></div>未赴任，今户部侍郎吕公提举中都市易务，辟为监门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209644_comment'></div>未几免归，丁父忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209644_comment'></div>至元丰八年，神宗山陵，今翰林学士承旨蔡公为顿递使，辟君管城县顿事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209644_comment'></div>事已，调环州通远寨主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209644_comment'></div>方待次外台，选权奉天县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209644_comment'></div>奉天故乾州，为陕右剧邑，前令类以不职去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209644_comment'></div>君至，擿奸吏之已甚者绳其一二，而民以服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209644_comment'></div>他郡邑虽远数百里，至有请君以听其讼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209644_comment'></div>甫留七月，邑以大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209644_comment'></div>部使者奏终其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209644_comment'></div>会亲嫌，并罢通远，又法当远仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209644_comment'></div>久之，调端州四会县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209644_comment'></div>明年，部使者奏移广州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209644_comment'></div>广州蕃汉错居，狱讼纷纠，率由译者变乱其言，以致失实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209644_comment'></div>君察见弊端，每有所治，必先穷竟译者，自是人无冤声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209644_comment'></div>囚方在系，日躬视其饮食沐浴之事，使悉如所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209644_comment'></div>一旦遇赦，出囚于州门之外，其肤发充泽，殆非囹圄中人也，见者感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209644_comment'></div>秩满，调登州防御推官，知衢州西安县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209644_comment'></div>以疾卒于都城，实绍圣五年三月十有七日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209644_comment'></div>享年五十，娶周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209644_comment'></div>子男八人，实、宇、宙皆举进士，以学行知名，而宇卒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209644_comment'></div>馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209644_comment'></div>女七人，长适进士周咸，早卒，许以第三女继其室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209644_comment'></div>次适进士王临，四适进士王履，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209644_comment'></div>孙男二人，女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209644_comment'></div>君怀慷慨，喜功名，才出仕即遇神宗厉精治道之日，拔用人才不以次序，又一时知己在显途，力挽致君，且有以馆阁荐者，然君免归矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209644_comment'></div>及元丰末，西鄙用兵，单骑走寨上，究观形胜，得边防措置十二事以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209644_comment'></div>未报，而神宗弃天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209644_comment'></div>三十年间，负其志气，落落不合，卒穷以死，其命也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209644_comment'></div>君为学不泥章句，为文辩博俊伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209644_comment'></div>平居凛凛若无所屈，一闻人善，则靡然归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209644_comment'></div>苟不可意，虽在势者面折不避也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209644_comment'></div>其孤卜以元符元年八月一日葬君于武进县怀德北乡萧塔村之原，念所以发扬潜美，非得当世大贤君子知君之深者一言以信之，则无以垂示无穷，于是属某状其行以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209644_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1209644_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年10月</a>　在右正言职。请牵复绍圣以来责降言官，论三经义出题试士。作品：请牵复绍圣以来责降言官疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三〇《请牵复绍圣以来责降言官疏》题下注“　元符元年十月”）</span><div id='poem_1209378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209378?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请牵复绍圣以来责降言官疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209378")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209378'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209378'>伏见绍圣以来，言官缘论事不当责降差遣者久未牵复，切恐中人以下因此以言为戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209378_comment'></div>今来大礼，泽及万方，无物不荷至恩，所有绍圣以来责降言官，亦望圣慈详酌情理，牵复施行，不惟可见公朝未尝以言废人，抑足以作天下敢言之气。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1209378_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年11月</a>　在右正言职。以郊祀覃恩，父保之肥赠通直郎，母张氏封仁寿县太君，夫人沈氏封崇德君。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年12月</a>　在右正言职。请申饬西边将帅。作品：请申饬西边将帅疏。<div id='poem_1209380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请申敕西边将帅疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209380")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209380'>伏睹泾原路招降、擒到西夏统军、监军并大小首领及人口、孳畜等万数不少，普天之下莫不称贺，以谓先帝之志而陛下成之，经所谓「天子之功」，传所谓「惟断乃成」，不足为陛下道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209380_comment'></div>然兵家未胜，则以决胜为难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209380_comment'></div>既胜，以持胜为难，惟其时而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209380_comment'></div>徒知决胜于其前，而不知持胜于其后，将有弃前功而招后患者矣，可不戒哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209380_comment'></div>臣恐将帅之臣狃于屡胜，不知所以持之，得志而志怠，忽事而事生，无以释朝廷西顾之远虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209380_comment'></div>伏惟圣慈密赐申敕，益务谨重，图惟厥终，岂但边鄙幸甚，实天下幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1209380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在右正言职，论蕃官殿前呈试弓马。<div id='poem_1209381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论蕃官殿前呈试弓马疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209381")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209381'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209381'>伏睹近者陛下御延和殿引见归明蕃官，令于殿前呈试弓马等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209381_comment'></div>夫以陛下威德广被，莫不革心，固无他虑，但戎人外臣，引见之初亦宜过防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209381_comment'></div>兼自今以往，归明者渐众，窃恐此事既传，其间不无阴怀两端之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209381_comment'></div>若令呈试，显属未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209381_comment'></div>伏望圣慈深赐省察，今后引见蕃官，即罢呈试弓马等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1209381_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在右正言职。奏论章惇。作品：论章惇疏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年12月</a>　在右正言职。奏论执政大臣不和。作品：论执政大臣不和疏。<div id='poem_1209382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论执政大臣不和疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年末）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209382")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209382'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209382'>臣伏自供职以来，夙夜靡宁，思报万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209382_comment'></div>顾天下之事可论者虽多，然其本原悉在于朝廷之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209382_comment'></div>传曰「正朝廷以正百官，正百官以正万民，正万民以正四方」，四方正，远近莫敢不一于正，此最今日之急务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209382_comment'></div>臣观执政大臣不务同心同德以称陛下登用之意其日久矣，而莫甚于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209382_comment'></div>故事无利害，人无忠邪，但某以为可者，某必以为不可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209382_comment'></div>某以为不可者，某必以为可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209382_comment'></div>可不可之论相持于上，而公是公非悉蔽于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209382_comment'></div>夫是非者，万事之本原，不可蔽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209382_comment'></div>一蔽于私而失其实，则末流之弊殆有不胜虑者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209382_comment'></div>陛下虽有求贤之诚，真贤何由而尽用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209382_comment'></div>陛下虽有听言之诚，忠言何由而尽闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209382_comment'></div>陛下虽有爱育元元之诚，仁恩德泽何由而尽达？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209382_comment'></div>是其为害岂不大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209382_comment'></div>况陛下操威福之柄以驭普天，虽远在四方万里之外，莫不欲其令之则从，禁之则止，有以明好恶之所在而不敢违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209382_comment'></div>而执政大臣近在左右，乃不能体国，如此岂陛下之威福独不可行于左右之近乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209382_comment'></div>夫威福不行于左右之近，而欲四方万里之外无不行焉，臣窃以为难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209382_comment'></div>且其不和之心既已发于声形，动于天地，为水为旱，为民物之灾矣，失今弗图，后必滋甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209382_comment'></div>抑恐四夷闻之，必有以轻议中国者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209382_comment'></div>此正朝廷所以为今日之急务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209382_comment'></div>臣望陛下留神听察，断以至公大义而力图之，实宗庙社稷无疆之休！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1209382_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年1月7日</a>　官右正言。正月，论郭时亮。作品：论郭时亮疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三〇《论郭時亮疏》题下注“元符二年正月七日”）</span><div id='poem_1209383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论郭时亮疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年正月七日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209383")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209383'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209383'>致治莫先于用人，用匪其人，民受实弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209383_comment'></div>臣窃见朝廷开封府界郭时亮自到本任，不务宣导朝廷德泽，惟以掊克凌暴为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209383_comment'></div>去年积雨，陛下所亲见而天下所共知，畿甸之内，鲜不被患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209383_comment'></div>凡人户以水诉者，时亮一切痛抑之，诸县顺承，惟恐不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209383_comment'></div>间有官吏不忍百姓实无所出，力为检放，即怒骂捃摭，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209383_comment'></div>民之怨嗟，闻者感动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209383_comment'></div>夫畿甸者，诸路之首，近在陛下耳目之前，至易察也，而时亮敢尔，略不以罔上损下为恤，又况远在千里之外者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209383_comment'></div>今来不惟未治其罪，方且擢为河东转运副使，一时公议，拂然惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209383_comment'></div>抑恐诸路监司见时亮本合得罪而反蒙迁擢，其奉法爱民者将解体而莫劝，违法殃民者将率意而莫惩，则远方赤子殆有困苦无告甚于畿甸之内者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209383_comment'></div>是由失赏刑于时亮一身之微，而致天下元元不得实受陛下仁厚之赐，此尤不可不虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209383_comment'></div>伏望睿断，罢时亮新命，追正其罪，以谢畿甸之民，以释公议之惑，以示惩劝于天下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1209383_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年2月</a>　在右正言职。论曾旼。作品：论曾旼疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三〇《论曾旼疏》题下注“元符二年二月”）</span><div id='poem_1209384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209384' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209384?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论曾旼疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209384")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209384_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209384'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209384'>臣伏闻曾旼往界首接伴北使，与之纷争累日方决，终不能夺北使之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209384_comment'></div>臣以得于外论，无由备见本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209384_comment'></div>若果有之，所系不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209384_comment'></div>盖彼我纷争，不过是非两端而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209384_comment'></div>谓旼等所争为是，则终不能夺北使之议，是舍是而从非也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209384_comment'></div>谓旼等所争为非，则安用纷争累日方决，是以非而为是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209384_comment'></div>舍是从非，则必为北使所屈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209384_comment'></div>以非为是，则必为北使所窥，二者必有一焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209384_comment'></div>旼等曾不审处于未见北使之前，而乃轻发于已见北使之后，此何谓也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209384_comment'></div>又况泛使实与常使不同，既未知其的为何求而来，正赖接伴豫以道理处之，使不能妄有生事之渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209384_comment'></div>而乃无故启其争心，尤为可罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209384_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降指挥，推究旼等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209384_comment'></div>如委有上项事迹，乞重行黜责，以为后人之戒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1209384_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年2月</a>　在右正言职。论刘定。作品：论刘定疏。<div id='poem_1209385' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209385' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209385?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论刘定疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209385")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209385_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209385'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209385'>伏闻新知庐州刘定前知陈州日恣为贪污不法等事，近因臣僚奏论，已降指挥，差官根治去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209385_comment'></div>其刘定虽未即正典刑，委是有罪戾难赦之人，岂宜更合冒赴新任，以辱兵民重寄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209385_comment'></div>伏望圣慈详依贾青罢知河中府近例，先次放罢，听候朝旨施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1209385_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年3月</a>　在右正言职。论蹇序辰。<div id='poem_1209387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论蹇序辰疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209387")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209387'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209387'>伏闻蹇序辰奉命使辽，颇失使事之体，为辽人所慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209387_comment'></div>除改例受绢既已施行外，其宴于客省及饮酒辄拜等行见行取问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209387_comment'></div>臣窃以使事所系，实为朝廷重轻，故虽一言一语之间，犹必致谨而不敢忽，况有大于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209387_comment'></div>今序辰乃宴非其所，拜不以道，曾不思故事当循，而惟辽人之命是从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209387_comment'></div>辽虽无知，岂不萌轻中国之心乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209387_comment'></div>孔子曰：「使于四方，不辱君命，可谓士矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209387_comment'></div>士且不可辱命，而序辰为尚书，反辱命如此，宜典刑之所先而不赦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209387_comment'></div>然序辰善事执政，世所共知，窃虑早晚供到文字进呈之时，执政必有多方致力，为序辰之助者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209387_comment'></div>万一此计得行，有所宽贷，则不惟无以惩戒后人，兼恐彼中自此指为故事，永不可改，其耻不小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209387_comment'></div>伏望圣慈深赐省察，出自独断，重行黜责，以慰天下公议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1209387_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年3月</a>　在右正言职。请廷集百官询访辽使事宜。作品：请廷集百官询访辽使事宜疏。<div id='poem_1209386' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209386' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209386?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请廷集百官询访辽使事宜疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209386")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209386_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209386'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209386'>伏见辽国人使已于今月十三日朝见，外议以为非泛使不至中国久矣，今此叩廷，决不虚发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209386_comment'></div>若非本朝自有所请，则必为羌人请命而至，此实大事，尤在审详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209386_comment'></div>窃庙谋已有成算，足以为国家长久之利，然臣伏观祖宗以来，每有大事，虽庙谋素定，亦必谋及在廷之臣，以参用其智，盖所以致戒于未然之前，而不至遗患于已然之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209386_comment'></div>臣今欲乞依祖宗故事，廷集百官，或只侍从，示以辽意，曲加询访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209386_comment'></div>其爱君虑国之心既非一日，宜必有至计远略，可备采择，以为万一之助者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209386_comment'></div>伏望圣慈详酌，特降指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1209386_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年4月</a>　在右正言职。论永裕陵买土利便。<div id='poem_1209389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>言永裕陵买土利便疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209389")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209389'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209389'>伏闻补治永裕陵沟井所见今买土已见利便，但以河南、河阳、颍昌、汝、郑五州府二十九县顾到人夫入役，已有定数，故于买土不能无限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209389_comment'></div>窃缘民间既知卖土实有厚利，莫不相率，纷然而集，势亦难遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209389_comment'></div>兼访闻河南等州人夫虽名和顾，颇有科配及去役处有至数程以上者，比之情愿卖土之人，显是利害不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209389_comment'></div>欲乞应系愿卖土之人不限人数，尽令收买，仍将买价增添钱数应几，不日益加纷集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209389_comment'></div>其河南等州县人夫即乞自远至近以次减放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209389_comment'></div>不惟官中省得顾钱，民间不妨农事，实于元料功役极有减助，可以速见成效，此又国家无穷莫大之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209389_comment'></div>伏望圣慈详酌，特降指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1209389_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年4月</a>　在右正言职。请选河北帅臣。<div id='poem_1209390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请选河北路帅臣疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209390")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209390'>臣闻河北路州军多是城壁不完，器械不利，士卒不足，训练不精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209390_comment'></div>陛下威德远加，必无意外之虑，然有备无患，亦前圣所不敢忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209390_comment'></div>近者朝廷虽已节次检举施行，缘积习已久，骤然为之，或启敌人疑心，前日霸州修桥之事可验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209390_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈应系河北路帅臣并选素有器识、众所信服之人，密以方略授之，使于岁月间修城壁、治器械、招士卒、谨训练，委任而责成功，不至动人耳目而武备饬矣，实万世安疆之计。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1209390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年4月</a>　在右正言职。请疏放滞狱。作品：请疏放滯狱疏。<div id='poem_1209391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请疏放滞狱疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209391")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209391'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209391'>伏惟京城久愆雨泽，兼闻诸路亦颇旱乾，窃恐农事失时，向去民间阙食，军储边计所系者大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209391_comment'></div>昔汉东海郡特以孝妇一狱不实，致枯旱三年，后因于公辨直其事，天立大雨，岁以丰熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209391_comment'></div>臣观陛下丕承先烈，钦恤庶狱，诚尧舜之用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209391_comment'></div>然中外攸司未必人人悉能推广德惠，匹夫匹妇一有枉滥，未足以感复至和，又况囚系淹延，追逮纷扰，多失其所者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209391_comment'></div>望降睿旨申饬中外，分委监司亟行疏放，庶几狱无滞冤，必有感格，上副陛下忧恤元元之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1209391_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年5月</a>　在右正言职。请下河北路安抚转运等司相度水患。作品：请下河北路安抚转运等司相度水疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三一《论台员旷缺疏》题下注“元符二年五月”）</span><div id='poem_1209392' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209392' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209392?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请下河北路安抚转运等司相度水患疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209392")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209392_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209392'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209392'>伏闻北京城内自开贯御河以来，民庐僧舍为水所浸，见已不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209392_comment'></div>若万一河流涨溢，即必为北京大患，事理无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209392_comment'></div>兼闻本处大姓已有迁居县镇，豫为避水之计者，人心危虑，不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209392_comment'></div>欲乞下河北路安抚转运等司疾速相度，务令一方永远无虞，上副朝廷兴利除害之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209392_comment'></div>伏望圣慈详酌，特赐指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1209392_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年5月</a>　在右正言职。请回徙御河。作品：请回徙御河疏。<div id='poem_1209393' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209393' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209393?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请回徙御河疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209393")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209393_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209393'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209393'>臣近以北京城内御河浸溃为患，乞赐指挥，下河北路安抚转运等司相度处置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209393_comment'></div>臣续访闻得河北去年大水之时，北京几殆者数矣，赖救护官司急将御河塞断，以故水不入城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209393_comment'></div>今来若只疏畎积水以纾目前之患，不惟河高城卑，疏畎之后依旧浸溃，其患犹在，实恐将来秋水暴集，因缘御河引注入城，涨溢难防，为患必大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209393_comment'></div>惟是回徙御河行于城外，庶几一方永无他虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209393_comment'></div>兼闻北京城外旧有河道，虽久堙废，自可兴复，以成御河之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209393_comment'></div>但御河系李仲所开，仲方为本路提刑，故官吏无敢言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209393_comment'></div>然而一方生灵之害，岂可因人而忽之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209393_comment'></div>况今迫近秋水涨溢之期，尤不可缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209393_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降指挥，令河北路不干碍官司疾速相度，回徙御河，自北京城外通行，以绝后患。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1209393_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年5月</a>　在右正言职。请戒励边臣。<div id='poem_1209394' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209394' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209394?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请戒励边臣疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209394")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209394_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209394'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209394'>伏见近者北敌遣使为羌人请命，已蒙圣恩，开以自新之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209394_comment'></div>既而曲赦陕西、河东，又以息民偃革形于德音，普天之下，鼓舞相贺，以为羌人罪大势穷，灭在旦夕，陛下遂赦不问者，直以生灵为念故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209394_comment'></div>然敌使之还，德音之布亦云久矣，而边臣犹或以经画为事，喧传外议，莫不惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209394_comment'></div>夫朝廷之所以示天下者，信而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209394_comment'></div>信不可无，犹大车不可以无輗，小车不可以无軏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209394_comment'></div>故虽州里之微，非信且不可行，而况天下乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209394_comment'></div>今来边臣乃不能上体至意，未忘经画，窃虑因此外则为朝廷失信于外国，内则为朝廷失信于陕西、河东之民，别致生事，不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209394_comment'></div>伏望睿慈特降指挥，严行戒励，庶几边臣谨于遵奉，有以副陛下深念生灵之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209394_comment'></div>不胜幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1209394_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年5月</a>　在右正言职。论台员旷缺。<div id='poem_1209395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论台员旷阙疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209395")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209395'>臣伏以台谏者，人主耳目之官，所恃以除壅闭而广聪明者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209395_comment'></div>一有旷阙，则蔽之所由生将有不胜虑者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209395_comment'></div>《书》曰「无旷庶官，天工人其代之」，又况耳目之官乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209395_comment'></div>然而自昔以来，备置台谏，使奋不顾身以交修厥职，殆非朝廷用事者之所乐，故必在人主独断而已，不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209395_comment'></div>臣窃见御史台除不置大夫外，由中丞而下有侍御史，有殿中侍御史，有监察御史，共八员，今止三员；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209395_comment'></div>两省谏官除不置散骑常侍外，由谏议大夫而下有司谏，有正言，共六员，今止有一员，旷阙之多，于兹为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209395_comment'></div>仰惟陛下躬揽威柄，延见群臣，而天鉴所加，莫不洞判，其间以身许国、无所阿徇、可以上当圣意者宜多有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209395_comment'></div>伏望断自宸衷，早赐选备，庶几言路不至久阙，相与尽忠献纳，少助陛下博览兼听之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1209395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年6月</a>　在右正言职。论增设水磨。作品：论增设水磨疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三一 《请抚存陕西等路被水去处疏》题下注“元符二年六月”）</span><div id='poem_1209396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论增设水磨疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209396")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209396'>伏见元丰年修置水磨，变磨茶末出卖，止是在京及开封府界诸县，未尝行于外路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209396_comment'></div>今既追复旧法，自合尽依元丰事体，而都提举汴河堤岸司乃于京西路郑、滑州、颍昌府，河北路澶州一例施行，近日又更差官前去京东路济州山口措置水磨等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209396_comment'></div>除郑州旧系府界县分，可以依旧施行外，其颍昌府、澶、滑州、山口皆元丰旧法所无，而今辄行之，果何谓也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209396_comment'></div>若谓颍昌既有水磨，可以就便出卖，济州山口置磨以后亦可出卖矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209396_comment'></div>若谓澶、滑系与畿县相邻可以出卖，即凡与畿县相邻去处亦可出卖矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209396_comment'></div>若谓山口当清河之冲，可以因水置磨，即凡通水去处亦可置磨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209396_comment'></div>既行之郑、滑，又行之澶州，又将行之济州，皆以为可，即一路一州，自此通彼，辗转相因，何所不至？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209396_comment'></div>虽朝廷遵奉前例，不敢辄有增损，而本司乃以机变之巧阴肆滋蔓，臣恐岁月之后，遂遍天下，而茶商衣食之源尽为本司所榷，不得措其手足，其弊可胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209396_comment'></div>伏望圣慈深赐照察，特降指挥，只令一依元丰旧法施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209396_comment'></div>所有济州山口措置水磨并其馀非元丰所行事件并一切寝罢，庶几不失先朝立法为民之意，上副陛下继志述事之孝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1209396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年6月</a>　在右正言职。论两浙路丁盐勘当。作品：论两浙路丁盐勘当疏。<div id='poem_1209397' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209397' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209397?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论两浙路丁盐勘当疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209397")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209397_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209397'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209397'>伏见两浙路察访司体究到本路人丁盐钱利害，乞将人户见催过丁盐钱通一路移补旧额，将见欠盐钱并与除放，并遇阙盐，依官卖盐价蠲免其钱，蒙送户部勘当，本部称已有朝旨，难议施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209397_comment'></div>臣窃详降旨之初，盖为两浙路转运副使胡宗哲止陈其利而隐其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209397_comment'></div>今来既缘臣僚上言，付察访司体究得自转运司催理以来，民力不堪，委实有害，户部自合依实勘当，申取朝廷指挥，却自称已有朝旨，难以施行，失仁圣恤民之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209397_comment'></div>伏望慈睿详酌，特降指挥，依察访司所奏事理施行，庶几一路元元实被德泽甚厚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1209397_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年6月</a>　在右正言职。请抚存陕西等路被水去处。作品：请抚存陕西等路被水去处疏。<div id='poem_1209398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209398?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请抚存陕西等路被水去处疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209398")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209398_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209398'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209398'>伏闻大河水势日近暴涨，凡在冲注，漂荡一空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209398_comment'></div>如三门、白波，则其害尤甚，盖数十年以来所未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209398_comment'></div>道路相传，无不骇叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209398_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞应系陕西、京东、河北等路被水冲注去处，并申饬逐路监司，或自朝廷委官前去，躬布惠泽，厚加抚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209398_comment'></div>庶几漂荡之馀生者得以自全，而死者不至暴露，以伤太平之和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209398_comment'></div>伏望圣慈详酌，速降指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1209398_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年6月</a>　在右正言职。论水旱相继消息宜谨。作品：论水旱相继消息宜谨疏。论水旱相继消息宜谨。<div id='poem_1209399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论水旱相继消复宜谨疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209399")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209399'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209399'>伏见去年河北、京东等路大水，为害甚于常时，上赖圣恩抚存，百姓方幸全复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209399_comment'></div>而今年之水又非去年可比，盖自陕西、京西以至河北，其间州县当水冲者皆漂荡民人，毁坏庐舍，至不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209399_comment'></div>仰惟朝廷申饬监司，举行诏条，所以宣导德泽甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209399_comment'></div>然而频年以来，水旱相继，虽盈虚之数所不可逃，而消复之方，尤宜致谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209399_comment'></div>《书》曰「惟先格王，正厥事」，正厥事而已，不以为数之当然，此消复之实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209399_comment'></div>臣愚伏观陛下清静以承天休，寅畏以谨天戒，惟恐一物失所，无以当上天爱育之意，固已应天有其实矣，尚虑政令施设之间，人才进退之际，有未足以释公议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209399_comment'></div>伏望睿慈深赐照察，以尽「格王正厥事」之义，不胜幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1209399_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年6月</a>　在右正言职。论盐司妄奏雨泽。<div id='poem_1209400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论监司妄奏雨泽疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209400")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209400'>伏见诸路监司率以本路雨泽沾足、秋成有望奏闻朝廷，然天道高远，难以豫知，若后雨泽过多，或时雨不继，为水为旱，决不可逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209400_comment'></div>缘监司既尝奏陈，不惟本司务掩前言，兼所属州县互相观望，虽行检放，亦非实数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209400_comment'></div>甚者公然抑勒，不令申诉灾伤，民间窘无所出，重以威势督之，遂至质卖妻孥，委弃父母，转徙沟壑，无以自存，为害甚大，不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209400_comment'></div>伏望圣慈严降指挥，敕戒诸路监司及州县长吏，如敢似此害及百姓，并重行黜谪，庶几今后莫不警惧，上副陛下恻怛爱民之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1209400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年7月</a>　在右正言职。论陆师闵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年7月</a>　在右正言职。再论陆师闵。作品：论陆师闵第二疏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年7月</a>　在右正言职。三论陆师闵。作品：论陆师闵第三疏。<div id='poem_1209403' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209403' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209403?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三论陆师闵疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209403")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209403_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209403'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209403'>臣近以陆师闵黜谪未久，骤然褒复，累具事理奏论，乞赐详酌施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209403_comment'></div>至今多日，未奉指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209403_comment'></div>臣固当体朝廷之意，不复论列，然区区愚忠，不能自已者，诚以公议未安故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209403_comment'></div>夫以公议上达圣听，恭俟采择，是乃臣之职分，敢不罄竭以闻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209403_comment'></div>臣观自古以来，帝王御世之术本末先后虽不一端，其要在务明赏罚而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209403_comment'></div>盖赏罚明故惩劝行，惩劝行故官吏肃，官吏肃故纪纲正而朝廷尊，此务明赏罚所以为操术之至要也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209403_comment'></div>师闵之事，其可忽乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209403_comment'></div>若以师闵为无罪，则忽罢户部侍郎，差知小郡，在前日为误罚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209403_comment'></div>若以师闵为有罪，则骤复宝文阁待制、知河南府，在今日为误赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209403_comment'></div>二者并用，是岂明赏罚之道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209403_comment'></div>臣窃惟朝廷不过急于得人任使，且谓师闵所坐情为可宥，及不欲追改已行之命，故虽师闵到任才二十一日，便行褒复，不以为疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209403_comment'></div>然而皆有可论者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209403_comment'></div>若急于得人任使，则臣前奏论之已详，已尘天览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209403_comment'></div>若谓师闵情为可宥，则文案具存，其情可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209403_comment'></div>按钟传奏讨荡画谋办事尽出师闵，数日间合力干办，乞特推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209403_comment'></div>既是讨荡谋画办事尽出师闵，数日间合力干办，即传以一百九十七级为三千五百三十级，师闵岂不预其事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209403_comment'></div>借令不知传妄冒之情，岂不知传乞为推恩之奏乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209403_comment'></div>不以自明，此何意也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209403_comment'></div>及六月十四日承受朝旨，妄冒人限一月许自首免罪，直至十八日方出榜施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209403_comment'></div>却于奏状内称寻行出榜，岂有奏以寻行出榜而施行乃在得旨四日之后乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209403_comment'></div>身为从官，优被宠寄，略不尊惮朝廷，公肆欺妄，迹状甚著，而遂谓其情为可宥，恐非所以示天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209403_comment'></div>公议未安，尤在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209403_comment'></div>若不欲追改已行之命，则言路所闻，无不在已行之后，傥以追改为难，即言职殆将废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209403_comment'></div>伏望圣慈曲赐照察，出自威断，追寝师闵前命，以释天下公议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1209403_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年7月</a>　在右正言职。奏请振济河北。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年7月</a>　在右正言职。论编类章疏。<div id='poem_1209405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论编类章疏疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209405")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209405'>伏睹近降指挥，令六曹诸司依臣僚上言，各将元丰八年四月以来应本司及所属申请勘当更改法度言涉附会讥讪文书尽检阅，随事编类，并著所任官姓名，具册申纳三省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209405_comment'></div>臣窃契勘自元丰八年四月以来，曾任六曹诸司及所属职事人数极多，除言涉附会讥讪文书已行编类外，其不为时事所屈，而尊君奉法，挺然如初，见于申请勘当之际者，亦必有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209405_comment'></div>欲乞依前降指挥行亦检阅，别作一项编类成册，具姓名申纳以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209405_comment'></div>所有盗匿弃毁、增减隐落及漏泄等事，亦乞依编类章疏已得朝旨施行，庶几特立自重之人终为圣明所察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1209405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年7月</a>　在右正言职。论看详诉理轻重。<div id='poem_1209406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论看详诉理轻重疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209406")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209406'>伏见看详诉理文字所节次看详过文字进呈，已蒙朝廷施行了毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209406_comment'></div>臣契勘元降看详指挥系分两等，一谓语及先帝，一谓语言过当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209406_comment'></div>除语及先帝之人外，其馀所诉虽情犯不齐，大率皆以官司锻炼致罪，抱负冤抑，得遇朝廷清明，辨雪矜贷为词，只是语言过当一等而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209406_comment'></div>而今所施行，则有勒停者，有降官者，有降官及差遣者，有远小处监当者，有罢知州与宫观者，有送吏部与合入差遣者，有罚铜三十斤者，有罚铜十斤者，一时公议，竟莫知其所以异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209406_comment'></div>又况诉理之语初亦难辨，有可以为轻，亦可以为重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209406_comment'></div>有可以为重，亦可以为轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209406_comment'></div>若可以为重，则语言过当者直谓之语及先帝可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209406_comment'></div>若可以为轻，则虽语及先帝者但谓之语言过当可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209406_comment'></div>然而典刑之所加，则不同日而语矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209406_comment'></div>夫因其近似难辨之迹而典刑轻重随以上下，是乃陛下威福之操柄下移于近臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209406_comment'></div>《书》所谓「惟辟作福，惟辟作威」者，正在此也，可不谨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209406_comment'></div>臣今据臣所知已行遣过事件等第节录如后：一、勒停谢愔诉雪父景初罪犯状内称「非今日朝廷清明，何以雪幽冤于泉下」等语言，自邓州职官勒停<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十二月二十一日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209406_comment'></div>一、降官韩忠彦、王存等奏雪谢景初罪犯劄子内称「朝廷专置官局，辨理枉横，景初不幸身没，不能自直」等语言，其韩忠彦自大中大夫降授中大夫，王存自右正议大夫降授通议大夫<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符二年正月十七日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209406_comment'></div>一、周之道诉雪本身罪犯状内称「天下之冤，无如臣比，若不仰告公朝，臣无路伸理」等语言，自朝散大夫降授朝奉大夫<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符二年五月一日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209406_comment'></div>一、阎令诉雪本身罪犯状内称「有罪之人，于格不应除雪者，苟情涉可矜，类蒙宽减，圣恩旷大，千载一时，况臣无辜，义当自直」等语言，自朝奉大夫降授朝请郎<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年五月二十六日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209406_comment'></div>一、马诚诉本身罪犯状内称「朝廷专差制使置狱劾问，虽明知傅致锻鍊，不敢以冤滥愬陈，恐重得罪」等语言，自奉议郎降授通直郎<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十月十四日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209406_comment'></div>一、降官及降差遣任公裕诉雪本身罪犯状内称「刑部一概以特旨，遂称难议施行，以此排天下之幽冤，使不得伸理」，及称「制勘院附会锻鍊，抑勒虚招，致臣久负冤抑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209406_comment'></div>今睹圣慈伸理天下冤滞，伏望察臣非辜」等语言，自朝请大夫、权发遣江淮等路发运副使降授朝散大夫、充发运判官<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年九月二十六日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209406_comment'></div>一、远小处监当宋乔年诉雪本身罪犯状内称「朝廷明恤冤抑，乔年之滥罚，亦冀获伸，庶获情法相应，冤抑得雪」等语言，令吏部与远小处监当差遣<span class='inlineComment2'>（未见月日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209406_comment'></div>一、罢知州与宫观叶涛诉雪本身罪犯状内称「蔡确、舒亶、何正臣、李定以兴造刑狱为事，故罗织及臣，抱赃污之至冤，废处江海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209406_comment'></div>今者伏值皇帝陛下、太皇太后陛下废黜奸恶，登用正士，矜恤民隐，薄敛时使，前日之吏多以微过被罪，今方命有司覆理而出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209406_comment'></div>苟臣不以片言自别，则自满堂取乐而已，犹自向隅，众皆望天而戴盆不已」等语言，自知明州差主管江宁府崇禧观<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十二月一日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209406_comment'></div>一、送吏部与合入差遣周邠诉雪本身罪犯状内称「前日非辜冤抑，幸得伸诉于今日大公之朝，倘蒙昭雪，则臣之元降一官庶有望于还复」等语言，罢知吉州，送吏部与合入差遣<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符二年正月二十四日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209406_comment'></div>一、罚铜吴居厚诉雪本身罪犯状内称「今遇朝廷推广恩惠，凡有罪戾之人，尽蒙宽贷湔洗，人情莫不悦豫」等语言，罚铜三十斤<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十二月十七日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209406_comment'></div>一、蒋之奇奏雪李萃罪犯状内称「今来冲替，显是太重」等语言，罚铜十斤<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十二月五日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209406_comment'></div>伏望圣慈深赐省察，以为来事之鉴，不胜幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1209406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年7月</a>　在右正言职。论选用水官。作品：论选用水官疏。<div id='poem_1209407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论选用水官疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209407")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209407'>伏睹近降指挥，令郑佑等相度燕家河，若开浚后不能行夺北流，虚费人工物料，逐官并重行朝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209407_comment'></div>自非圣明照见本末，岂及于此，不胜幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209407_comment'></div>然今来所用水官尽是主张东流，缘此转官擢任之人虽已重行朝典，豫严戒敕，窃虑各官势须力护前失，规为身谋，不免虚费人工物料等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209407_comment'></div>待其事败然后黜谪，则人工物料之费，其害已不赀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209407_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降指挥，令条具内外官曾任水事而不专主东流之议者，选用其人，使与见今水官相参措置施行，庶几利害得实，不至重有劳民蠹国之弊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1209407_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年8月</a>　在右正言职。请黜责水官妄作。<div id='poem_1209408' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209408' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209408?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请黜责水官妄作疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209408")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209408_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209408'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209408'>伏见都水监及外丞司官昨缘河事迁转官秩、升擢任使，其数不少，自去年以来，堤防屡次兴筑，曾不足以捍御涨水，而公私被患，上轸圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209408_comment'></div>则是前日以为有功者，非特不足恃而已，又适因其逆障水势，驯致大害，至于此极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209408_comment'></div>就令百姓所失衣食之具，官司所放税赋之物，朝廷所支赈济之费，虽以千百万计，无足恤者，然数千里生灵性命，岂不重可念哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209408_comment'></div>水官方且安享禄位，俛仰自如，一时公议，莫不惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209408_comment'></div>若但赏之于虚利未效之前，而不谪之于实害已形之后，亦何恃以为劝沮乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209408_comment'></div>伏望睿慈特诏有司条具都水监及外丞司官昨因河事转官擢任，而今已见其罪状者，出自睿断，并行黜谪，以谢河北之民，以惩妄作之吏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1209408_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年8月</a>　在右正言职。论国子监解额许开封府举人就试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在右正言职。论看详诉理轻重。作品：论看详诉理轻重疏。<div id='poem_1209406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论看详诉理轻重疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209406")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209406'>伏见看详诉理文字所节次看详过文字进呈，已蒙朝廷施行了毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209406_comment'></div>臣契勘元降看详指挥系分两等，一谓语及先帝，一谓语言过当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209406_comment'></div>除语及先帝之人外，其馀所诉虽情犯不齐，大率皆以官司锻炼致罪，抱负冤抑，得遇朝廷清明，辨雪矜贷为词，只是语言过当一等而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209406_comment'></div>而今所施行，则有勒停者，有降官者，有降官及差遣者，有远小处监当者，有罢知州与宫观者，有送吏部与合入差遣者，有罚铜三十斤者，有罚铜十斤者，一时公议，竟莫知其所以异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209406_comment'></div>又况诉理之语初亦难辨，有可以为轻，亦可以为重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209406_comment'></div>有可以为重，亦可以为轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209406_comment'></div>若可以为重，则语言过当者直谓之语及先帝可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209406_comment'></div>若可以为轻，则虽语及先帝者但谓之语言过当可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209406_comment'></div>然而典刑之所加，则不同日而语矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209406_comment'></div>夫因其近似难辨之迹而典刑轻重随以上下，是乃陛下威福之操柄下移于近臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209406_comment'></div>《书》所谓「惟辟作福，惟辟作威」者，正在此也，可不谨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209406_comment'></div>臣今据臣所知已行遣过事件等第节录如后：一、勒停谢愔诉雪父景初罪犯状内称「非今日朝廷清明，何以雪幽冤于泉下」等语言，自邓州职官勒停<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十二月二十一日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209406_comment'></div>一、降官韩忠彦、王存等奏雪谢景初罪犯劄子内称「朝廷专置官局，辨理枉横，景初不幸身没，不能自直」等语言，其韩忠彦自大中大夫降授中大夫，王存自右正议大夫降授通议大夫<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符二年正月十七日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209406_comment'></div>一、周之道诉雪本身罪犯状内称「天下之冤，无如臣比，若不仰告公朝，臣无路伸理」等语言，自朝散大夫降授朝奉大夫<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符二年五月一日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209406_comment'></div>一、阎令诉雪本身罪犯状内称「有罪之人，于格不应除雪者，苟情涉可矜，类蒙宽减，圣恩旷大，千载一时，况臣无辜，义当自直」等语言，自朝奉大夫降授朝请郎<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年五月二十六日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209406_comment'></div>一、马诚诉本身罪犯状内称「朝廷专差制使置狱劾问，虽明知傅致锻鍊，不敢以冤滥愬陈，恐重得罪」等语言，自奉议郎降授通直郎<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十月十四日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209406_comment'></div>一、降官及降差遣任公裕诉雪本身罪犯状内称「刑部一概以特旨，遂称难议施行，以此排天下之幽冤，使不得伸理」，及称「制勘院附会锻鍊，抑勒虚招，致臣久负冤抑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209406_comment'></div>今睹圣慈伸理天下冤滞，伏望察臣非辜」等语言，自朝请大夫、权发遣江淮等路发运副使降授朝散大夫、充发运判官<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年九月二十六日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209406_comment'></div>一、远小处监当宋乔年诉雪本身罪犯状内称「朝廷明恤冤抑，乔年之滥罚，亦冀获伸，庶获情法相应，冤抑得雪」等语言，令吏部与远小处监当差遣<span class='inlineComment2'>（未见月日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209406_comment'></div>一、罢知州与宫观叶涛诉雪本身罪犯状内称「蔡确、舒亶、何正臣、李定以兴造刑狱为事，故罗织及臣，抱赃污之至冤，废处江海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209406_comment'></div>今者伏值皇帝陛下、太皇太后陛下废黜奸恶，登用正士，矜恤民隐，薄敛时使，前日之吏多以微过被罪，今方命有司覆理而出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209406_comment'></div>苟臣不以片言自别，则自满堂取乐而已，犹自向隅，众皆望天而戴盆不已」等语言，自知明州差主管江宁府崇禧观<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十二月一日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209406_comment'></div>一、送吏部与合入差遣周邠诉雪本身罪犯状内称「前日非辜冤抑，幸得伸诉于今日大公之朝，倘蒙昭雪，则臣之元降一官庶有望于还复」等语言，罢知吉州，送吏部与合入差遣<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符二年正月二十四日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209406_comment'></div>一、罚铜吴居厚诉雪本身罪犯状内称「今遇朝廷推广恩惠，凡有罪戾之人，尽蒙宽贷湔洗，人情莫不悦豫」等语言，罚铜三十斤<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十二月十七日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209406_comment'></div>一、蒋之奇奏雪李萃罪犯状内称「今来冲替，显是太重」等语言，罚铜十斤<span class='inlineComment2'>（元符元年十二月五日。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209406_comment'></div>伏望圣慈深赐省察，以为来事之鉴，不胜幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1209406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在右正言职。论编类章。作品：论编类章疏。<div id='poem_1209405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论编类章疏疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209405")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209405'>伏睹近降指挥，令六曹诸司依臣僚上言，各将元丰八年四月以来应本司及所属申请勘当更改法度言涉附会讥讪文书尽检阅，随事编类，并著所任官姓名，具册申纳三省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209405_comment'></div>臣窃契勘自元丰八年四月以来，曾任六曹诸司及所属职事人数极多，除言涉附会讥讪文书已行编类外，其不为时事所屈，而尊君奉法，挺然如初，见于申请勘当之际者，亦必有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209405_comment'></div>欲乞依前降指挥行亦检阅，别作一项编类成册，具姓名申纳以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209405_comment'></div>所有盗匿弃毁、增减隐落及漏泄等事，亦乞依编类章疏已得朝旨施行，庶几特立自重之人终为圣明所察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1209405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年9月</a>　在右正言职。上疏劾章惇。作品：论章惇第二疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三一《论章惇第二疏》题下注“元符二年九月”）</span><div id='poem_1209409' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209409' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209409?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论章惇第二疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209409")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209409_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209409'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209409'>陛下之所以用惇者，为其不负先帝也，而今则负先帝之迹已彰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209409_comment'></div>陛下之所以用惇者，为其能尊朝廷也，今则尊朝廷之心何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209409_comment'></div>方司马光用事，惇虽显与光异，而阴实助之，故欲变先帝保甲之法，则与连名抗疏，指以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209409_comment'></div>夫惇在先帝时既位居二府，于朝廷政事无不可议者，果知保甲不便，言于先帝而罢之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209409_comment'></div>安忍先帝陵土未乾，遽指以为非乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209409_comment'></div>不因编类章疏，世亦无由知其负先帝如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209409_comment'></div>伏自委官编类章疏及看详诉理文字以来，凡厥语言上及先朝、有伤陛下继述之孝者莫不行遣，所以正臣子之分义而惩其奸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209409_comment'></div>惇每敷奏，必曰某罪重，当窜远方，某罪轻，当削夺官职，不知几日而几人矣，曾不自思亦有前项章疏语及先帝，当如之何而定罪乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209409_comment'></div>日惟面谩，无复畏惮，其不尊朝廷又如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209409_comment'></div>谋身欺世，心迹甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209409_comment'></div>光既追正典刑，其馀章疏文字亦行遣殆尽，不应惇者独相如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209409_comment'></div>又况惇蒙先帝擢二府，蒙陛下擢为宰相，恩礼隆厚，无与比伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209409_comment'></div>乃敢傲然肆为不忠，尤难与众犯之人一概定罪。</div><div
