id='poem_sentence_12_1209409_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年9月</a>　在右正言职。上疏谏立刘后，除名勒停，送新州羁管。作品：谏哲宗立刘后疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（初，邹浩召还，入对，帝首及谏立后事，奖叹再三，询谏草安在。对曰：“焚之矣。”退告陈莹中瓘，莹中曰：“祸其在此乎！異日奸人妄出一缄，则不能复辨矣。”至是蔡京用事，使其党内侍协防随属馆客伪公疏。于是朝廷大怒，于是责授衡州别驾，永州安置。《全宋文》卷二八三〇《 諫哲宗立劉后疏》题下注“元符二年九月”）</span><div id='poem_1209372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏哲宗立刘后疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209372")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209372'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209372'>臣闻《礼》曰：「天子之与后，犹日之与月，阴之与阳，相须而成者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209372_comment'></div>「天子理阳道，后治阴德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209372_comment'></div>天子听外治，后听内职」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209372_comment'></div>然则立后以配天子，安得不谨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209372_comment'></div>今陛下为天下择母，所立乃贤妃刘氏，一时公议，莫不疑惑，诚以国家自有仁祖故事，不可不遵用之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209372_comment'></div>盖皇后郭氏与美人尚氏争宠致罪，仁祖既废后，不旋踵并斥美人，所以示公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209372_comment'></div>及至立后，则不选于妃嫔，必选于贵族，而立慈圣光献，所以远嫌也，所以为天下万世法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209372_comment'></div>陛下以罪废孟后，与废郭后实无异焉，然孟氏之罪未尝付外杂治，果与贤妃争宠而致罪乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209372_comment'></div>世固不得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209372_comment'></div>果不与贤妃争宠而致罪乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209372_comment'></div>世亦不得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209372_comment'></div>若与贤妃争宠而致罪，则并斥美人以示公，固有仁祖故事存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209372_comment'></div>若不与贤妃争宠而致罪，则不立妃嫔以远嫌，亦有仁祖故事存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209372_comment'></div>二者必居一于此矣，不可得而逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209372_comment'></div>况孟氏罪废之初，天下孰不疑立贤妃以为后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209372_comment'></div>及读诏书，有「别选贤族」之语，又闻陛下临朝慨叹，以废后为国家不幸，又见宗室有立妾之请，陛下怒其轻乱名分，重赐谴责，于是天下始释然不疑陛下立后之意在贤妃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209372_comment'></div>今果立之，则天下之所以期陛下者皆莫之信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209372_comment'></div>载在史册，传示万世，不免上累圣德，可不惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209372_comment'></div>可不惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209372_comment'></div>且五伯，三王之罪人也，其葵丘之会，载书犹首曰「无以妾为妻」，况陛下之圣，高出三王之上，其可忽此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209372_comment'></div>万一自此之后，士大夫有以妾为妻，臣寮纠劾以闻，陛下何以处之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209372_comment'></div>不治则伤化败俗，无以为国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209372_comment'></div>治之则上行下效，难以责人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209372_comment'></div>孔子曰：「名不正则言不顺，言不顺则事不成，事不成则礼乐不兴，礼乐不兴则刑罚不中，刑罚不中则民无所措手足」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209372_comment'></div>夫名之不正，遂至民无所措手足，则其害可胜道哉，尤不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209372_comment'></div>臣伏观陛下天性仁孝，追奉休烈，惟恐一毫不当先帝之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209372_comment'></div>然先帝在位，动以二帝三王为法，斥两汉以下不取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209372_comment'></div>今陛下乃引自汉以来有为五伯之所不为者以自比，是岂先帝之意乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209372_comment'></div>是岂继志述事所当然者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209372_comment'></div>此尤公议之所未谕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209372_comment'></div>臣观白麻内再三言之者，不过称贤妃有子，及引永平、祥符立后事，以为所咨之故实，臣请论其所以然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209372_comment'></div>若曰有子可以为后，则永平中贵人马氏未尝有子也，所以立为后者，以德冠后宫故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209372_comment'></div>祥符中德妃刘氏亦未尝有子也，所以立为后者，以钟英甲族故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209372_comment'></div>又况贵人之系，实为马援之女；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209372_comment'></div>德妃之时，并无废后之嫌，其与贤妃事体，迥然不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209372_comment'></div>若曰贤妃德冠后宫，亦如贵人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209372_comment'></div>钟英甲族，亦如德妃，则何不于孟氏罪废之初，用立慈圣光献故事，便立之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209372_comment'></div>迁延四年，以待今日，果何意邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209372_comment'></div>必欲以此示天下果信之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209372_comment'></div>兼臣闻顷年冬享景灵宫，贤妃实随驾以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209372_comment'></div>是日雷作，其变甚异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209372_comment'></div>今又宣麻之后，大雨继日，已而飞雹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209372_comment'></div>又自告天地祖宗社稷以来，阴霪不止，以动人心，则上天之意盖可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209372_comment'></div>陛下事天甚谨，畏天甚至，尤宜思所以动天而致然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209372_comment'></div>考之人事既如彼，求之天意又如此，安可不留圣意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209372_comment'></div>夫成汤，圣君也，仲虺不称其无过，称其改过不吝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209372_comment'></div>高宗，贤君也，傅说不告以拒谏，而告以从谏则圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209372_comment'></div>臣虽至愚，不足以方古谏者，常念唐太宗犹有耻君不及尧舜之臣，况真可为尧舜如陛下之圣，而于身亲见之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209372_comment'></div>是以不敢爱身，冒犯天威，图报陛下亲自识拔大恩之万一，而区区血诚，尽于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1209372_comment'></div>惟陛下俯从而改之不以为吝，则万世之下，所以仰陛下之圣者，亦将在成汤、高宗之上矣，岂不美哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1209372_comment'></div>岂不美哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1209372_comment'></div>伏望圣慈深赐照纳，不以一时改命为甚难，而以万世公议为足畏，追停册礼，别选贤族，如初诏施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1209372_comment'></div>庶几上答天意，下慰人心，为宗庙社稷无疆之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1209372_comment'></div>不胜幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1209372_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ababe8839e8b4cc7a2bb1072c92875fc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ababe8839e8b4cc7a2bb1072c92875fc");'><span id='ababe8839e8b4cc7a2bb1072c92875fc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1102')">1100-1102年</a>，41-43岁</div><div id='ababe8839e8b4cc7a2bb1072c92875fc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年3月</a>　三月，复除右正言，三具状辞，不允。作品：乞辞右政言疏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年3月</a>　在右正言职。乞如神考故事诏侍从言事。作品：乞如神考故事诏侍从言事疏。<div id='poem_1209415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞如神考故事诏侍从言事疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209415")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209415'>臣伏见神考尝诏侍从官言事，其略曰：「《传》曰：『近臣尽规，以为荣耻休戚与上同也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209415_comment'></div>今在此位者，视朕过失与朝廷政事之阙，默而不言，乃或私议窃叹，若以其责不在己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209415_comment'></div>夫岂习见成俗以为当然，其亦有含章怀宝，待倡而发者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209415_comment'></div>宜令侍从官自今视朕与朝廷政事之阙，无有巨细，各具章极言无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209415_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209415_comment'></div>言善而不用，朕有厥咎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209415_comment'></div>道之而弗言，尔为不恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209415_comment'></div>朕将用此考察在位所以事君之寔而明黜陟焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209415_comment'></div>夫自五帝以来，神圣超卓，如我神考，可谓群臣莫能及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209415_comment'></div>然犹咨访阙失，不敢忽如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209415_comment'></div>今陛下宠待近臣甚厚，是亦神考之用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209415_comment'></div>顾近臣未必皆能上体圣意，敢以所见，极言无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209415_comment'></div>欲望如神考故事，特降诏书，谕以至怀，庶几人人思自罄竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209415_comment'></div>陛下从而览之，岂唯兼收博采，坐以无事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209415_comment'></div>而臣下忠邪得失之情，亦因以灼知而尽见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209415_comment'></div>此要道也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1209415_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在右正言职。状乞给假归常州迎侍，不允。作品：乞给假归常州迎侍状。<div id='poem_1209351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞给假归常州迎侍状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209351")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209351'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209351'>窃念臣母年高，素苦风眩，臣昨过岭，以家贫路远，迎侍不得，见居常州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209351_comment'></div>臣既被召旨，又不敢迂程归省，及至国门，闻臣母自臣得罪以来，日夕忧惧，旧疾增加，人子之心，实难安处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209351_comment'></div>陛下方以仁孝治天下，臣虽不获辞禄就养，欲望圣慈曲赐矜恤，特许给假，令臣暂归常州，迎侍老母前来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209351_comment'></div>不胜区区犬马之情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1209351_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在右正言职。疏请察为学之本。作品：请察为学之本疏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在右正言职。疏论向族子弟，乞密加训敕。作品：论士大夫交结向族子弟疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三二《论士大夫交结向族子弟疏》题下注云：“元符三年六月”）</span><div id='poem_1209412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论士大夫交结向族子弟疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209412")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209412'>臣伏见陛下即位之初，皇太后权同听政，所以协济艰难，为宗庙社稷无穷之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209412_comment'></div>本朝故事，惟慈圣光献皇后垂帘之日，与章献明肃皇后、宣仁圣烈皇后事体稍异，然犹久之，方始复辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209412_comment'></div>今皇太后乃深自退托，不敢引三后为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209412_comment'></div>初降手书，期以祔庙礼毕，不复与政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209412_comment'></div>既又不候祔庙，亟践初言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209412_comment'></div>自古以来，方册所载母后之美，未有如皇太后功德如此之盛者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209412_comment'></div>《易》曰：「进退不失其正者，其唯圣人乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209412_comment'></div>皇太后可谓不失其正矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209412_comment'></div>普天之下，虽三尺童子尚知歌舞称颂，况忠义有识之士哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209412_comment'></div>陛下天性仁孝，思所以报功德者甚切，是以向宗回等以次超擢，莫不曲尽其厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209412_comment'></div>虽非陛下以此为私，而宫禁之间，所以奉皇太后之欢心者无所不至，盖可推此而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209412_comment'></div>今士大夫或不深惟陛下厚待母族之意，往往奔走其门，务相交结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209412_comment'></div>甚者阴使腹心密致诚款，似欲因缘势力，以为进身固位之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209412_comment'></div>一时公议，颇亦疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209412_comment'></div>然臣闻旧来向族子弟所为稍有不善，皇太后必遣使切责，以此人人畏惧，唯务寡过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209412_comment'></div>而向宗回等又素以修饰见称于时，纵使士大夫切于自谋，决不为之改操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209412_comment'></div>但恐向族子弟至多，其间岂无思虑不审之人，万一为士大夫所误，不能远嫌，以动公议，臣寮有以闻者，不知陛下何以处之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209412_comment'></div>若不行，则无以正祖宗之法度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209412_comment'></div>若行之，则无以慰慈闱之至念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209412_comment'></div>不唯陛下难处，在皇太后处之亦甚难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209412_comment'></div>且陛下之立也，大臣固有异议者，赖皇太后以宗庙社稷为心，断然不摇，大计以定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209412_comment'></div>而陛下既立之后，天地协应，人心自归，六合之间，尽为和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209412_comment'></div>故虽蛮夷戎狄，远在声教之外，亦莫不稽首面内，幸不世出之遭遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209412_comment'></div>是则皇太后之功德，又孰得而形容之邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209412_comment'></div>功德如此，皇太后乃委而弗居，深自退托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209412_comment'></div>虽帝尧之克逊，大禹之不伐，何以复加！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209412_comment'></div>方且含饴弄孙，尊享太平之福，与陛下同之，如天长地久，安可使难处之事辄有闻于天下乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209412_comment'></div>臣愚伏愿陛下于从容省侍之际，密以此事禀皇太后，乞自皇太后密加觉察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209412_comment'></div>若外议无实则已，果有其实，乞自皇太后密加训敕，以杜其渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209412_comment'></div>庶几外则不废祖宗之法度，内则不动慈闱之至念，使天下咸仰陛下奉亲之圣孝，咸仰皇太后立子之功德，永永万年，无有穷已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209412_comment'></div>而向族子弟保其令名，亦有无穷之显，岂不美欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209412_comment'></div>臣昨以罪远窜，分死瘴乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209412_comment'></div>蒙恩生还，复以旧职，实在陛下即位之初，皇太后垂帘之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209412_comment'></div>今身体发肤皆陛下、皇太后之所再造，所以图报大恩，尤非其馀臣寮之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209412_comment'></div>若于此时有所见闻，噤不启口，至它日臣寮有奋不顾身而言者，然后亦从而言之，则臣之罪大矣，敢不豫以奏陈？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209412_comment'></div>伏望圣慈赦其狂妄而纳其愚忠，不胜幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209412_comment'></div>不胜幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1209412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1209412'><span class='label'>按：</span>此篇及以下三篇《道乡集·补遗》所录文不全，今改以《诸臣奏议》为底本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1209412_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在右正言职。论帝王为学之本。作品：论帝王为学之本疏。<div id='poem_1209417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论帝王为学之本疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209417")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209417'>臣窃观自昔才智之君固有务学以为先者，然而学非其本，失所以学，终不足以成帝王之高致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209417_comment'></div>《记》曰：「欲明明德于天下者，先治其国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209417_comment'></div>欲治其国者，先齐其家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209417_comment'></div>欲齐其家者，先脩其身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209417_comment'></div>欲脩其身者，先正其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209417_comment'></div>欲正其心者，先诚其意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209417_comment'></div>欲诚其意者，先致其知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209417_comment'></div>致知在格物」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209417_comment'></div>此学之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209417_comment'></div>又曰：「物格而后知至，知至而后意诚，意诚而后心正，心正而后身脩，身脩而后家齐，家齐而后国治，国治而后天下平」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209417_comment'></div>此所学之效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209417_comment'></div>扬子曰：「学之为王者事，其已久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209417_comment'></div>尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武，汲汲夫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209417_comment'></div>尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武，皆万世所仰，以为帝王之师者也，尚汲汲于学而不敢怠，为人君者，其可以忽此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209417_comment'></div>恭惟陛下天资圣神，群臣莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209417_comment'></div>方且延纳名儒，入侍讲读，招来谠论，用广总明，固已卓然知所务矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209417_comment'></div>所以为学之本，更望深赐察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209417_comment'></div>虽处宫闱之间，常若对乎天地，则知人安民，自如帝尧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209417_comment'></div>能察迩言，自如帝舜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209417_comment'></div>身为法度，自如大禹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209417_comment'></div>不迩声色，自如成汤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209417_comment'></div>卑服即康功田功，自如文王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209417_comment'></div>垂拱而天下治，自如武王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209417_comment'></div>其事岂不至约，而其功岂不博乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209417_comment'></div>陛下不以臣愚而废其言，不胜幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1209417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在右正言职。乞如仁宗故事。作品：乞如仁宗故事疏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在右正言职。诏侍从言事。作品：诏侍从言事疏。<div id='poem_1209415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞如神考故事诏侍从言事疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209415")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209415'>臣伏见神考尝诏侍从官言事，其略曰：「《传》曰：『近臣尽规，以为荣耻休戚与上同也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209415_comment'></div>今在此位者，视朕过失与朝廷政事之阙，默而不言，乃或私议窃叹，若以其责不在己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209415_comment'></div>夫岂习见成俗以为当然，其亦有含章怀宝，待倡而发者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209415_comment'></div>宜令侍从官自今视朕与朝廷政事之阙，无有巨细，各具章极言无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209415_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209415_comment'></div>言善而不用，朕有厥咎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209415_comment'></div>道之而弗言，尔为不恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209415_comment'></div>朕将用此考察在位所以事君之寔而明黜陟焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209415_comment'></div>夫自五帝以来，神圣超卓，如我神考，可谓群臣莫能及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209415_comment'></div>然犹咨访阙失，不敢忽如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209415_comment'></div>今陛下宠待近臣甚厚，是亦神考之用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209415_comment'></div>顾近臣未必皆能上体圣意，敢以所见，极言无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209415_comment'></div>欲望如神考故事，特降诏书，谕以至怀，庶几人人思自罄竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209415_comment'></div>陛下从而览之，岂唯兼收博采，坐以无事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209415_comment'></div>而臣下忠邪得失之情，亦因以灼知而尽见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209415_comment'></div>此要道也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1209415_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年7月</a>　在右正言职。请申敕太史无讳天象。作品：论天象乞申勅太史無有讳避疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（论天象乞申勅太史無有讳避疏。）</span><div id='poem_1209414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论天象乞申敕太史无有讳避疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209414")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209414'>臣闻天人之应，捷于影响，苟知其故而豫处之，则转祸为福，斯不难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209414_comment'></div>神宗皇帝尝谓辅臣曰：「事之将兆，天常见象，但人不能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209414_comment'></div>彗孛示人事甚直，犹如语言，顾今无深晓天道之人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209414_comment'></div>古人能知之，则能消伏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209414_comment'></div>又曰：「事将萌而天象先见，盖人事在下，气积于上，积众人之气而先见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209414_comment'></div>犹人之五脏有疾病，而气色见于面矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209414_comment'></div>非神宗皇帝至神至圣，岂能及此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209414_comment'></div>此人主之所宜遵用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209414_comment'></div>臣愚欲望睿慈申敕太史，无有讳避，悉以所占密具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209414_comment'></div>从而察之，以正厥事，以为曲突徙薪之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209414_comment'></div>天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1209414_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年9月</a>　改起居舍人，两具状辞，不允。作品：辞免起居舍人状。<div id='poem_1209352' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209352' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209352?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免起居舍人状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209352")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209352_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209352'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209352'>臣窃见祖宗以来，推择左右秉笔之臣，尤为至严，所以厉庶工而尊朝廷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209352_comment'></div>陛下方遵奉成宪，以尽《春秋》谨始之义，名器所属，必时望人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209352_comment'></div>而越使记言，乃误超擢，臣虽不学，岂不自省非其分乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209352_comment'></div>闻命惊惶，莫知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209352_comment'></div>伏望圣慈俯昭诚悃，追寝褒除，改用豪英，庶协公议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1209352_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年9月</a>　任起居舍。有奏。作品：上徽宗乞先恤公议而后谨独断疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三一 《上徽宗乞先恤公议而后谨独断疏》题下注“元符三年九月”）</span><div id='poem_1209410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上徽宗乞先恤公议而后谨独断疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209410")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209410'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209410'>臣尝读《孟子》，见其「左右皆曰贤，未可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209410_comment'></div>诸大夫皆曰贤，未可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209410_comment'></div>国人皆曰贤，然后察之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209410_comment'></div>见贤焉，然后用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209410_comment'></div>左右皆曰不可，勿听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209410_comment'></div>诸大夫皆曰不可，勿听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209410_comment'></div>国人皆曰不可，然后察之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209410_comment'></div>见不可焉，然后去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209410_comment'></div>如此然后可以为民父母」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209410_comment'></div>于是知公议不可不恤，独断不可不谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209410_comment'></div>人君之所急务，尤在于此焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209410_comment'></div>盖左右非不亲也，然不能无交结之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209410_comment'></div>诸大夫非不贵也，然不能无恩雠之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209410_comment'></div>至于国人皆曰贤，皆曰不可，则所谓公议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209410_comment'></div>夫公议之所在，既已察之矣，必待见贤焉然后用之，见不可焉然后去之，则所谓独断也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209410_comment'></div>惟恤公议于独断未形之前，惟谨独断于公议已闻之后，则人君之所以致治者，又安有不善乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209410_comment'></div>二帝之所以帝，三王之所以王，未有不出于此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209410_comment'></div>臣愚伏见朝廷之事，窃疑近日以来颇有异于陛下即位之初者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209410_comment'></div>参听人言，往往有嗟叹不平之语，非若前日之无不和悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209410_comment'></div>且今去陛下即位之初，才半年有馀耳，然遽已如此，不知自今以往，又将如之何也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209410_comment'></div>况祔庙既毕，普天之下莫不延颈拭目以徯初政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209410_comment'></div>而初政者，乃人君谨始以正其本者也，尤宜省察，正在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209410_comment'></div>臣愿陛下深思孟子之言，务使公议先达于上，然后断以独智，庶几有为，悉协天下之望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1209410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1209410'><span class='label'>按：</span>此疏《道乡集·补遗》引录《宋史·邹浩传》之节文，不及《诸臣奏议》之全，今改以后者为底本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1209410_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　除通直郎，试中书舍人，仍改赐章服，两具状辞，不允。作品：辞免中书舍人。辞免中书舍人第二状。谢中书舍人启。<div id='poem_1209355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免中书舍人第二状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209355")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209355'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209355'>闻命震惊，莫知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209355_comment'></div>窃以代言之任，擢自右史，虽故事具存，然必学识文词过人远甚，乃协公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209355_comment'></div>如臣孤陋，一无所长，秉笔殿坳，日月未几，免试弗获，废黜为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209355_comment'></div>敢谓殊私，亟此褒用，在臣分义，尤极难安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209355_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降指挥，追还恩奖，庶几名位不为虚受，以严一时多士之劝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1209355_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢中书舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209458")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209458'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209458'>秉笔螭坳，未知报称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209458_comment'></div>演纶凤阁，亟此超踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209458_comment'></div>既成命之莫回，跼微躬而增腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209458_comment'></div>窃以隆社稷之福者，莫先乎求士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209458_comment'></div>为邦家之光者，尤在乎得贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209458_comment'></div>矧居侍从之官，仍处深严之地，预闻机要，参掌命书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209458_comment'></div>苟非四海之豪英，曷副一时之公议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209458_comment'></div>询谋至慎，今昔攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209458_comment'></div>如某者才慊中流，学惭上达，徒以遭逢之异，尝叨供奉之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209458_comment'></div>蝼蚁何知，尚有君臣之义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209458_comment'></div>驽骀虽钝，岂无刍粟之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209458_comment'></div>勉自罄于愚忠，竟莫裨于至治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209458_comment'></div>分甘遐外，望绝生全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209458_comment'></div>属圣仁之勃兴，脱瘴氛而收用，未逾一岁，忽已五迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209458_comment'></div>敢期清切之除，更冒褒扬之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209458_comment'></div>靖言侥倖，厥有夤缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209458_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官公天下以为心，妙环中而应物，曲尽上臣之道，用纾侧席之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209458_comment'></div>众正之路既开，太平之基自立，致兹凡陋，躐厕高华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209458_comment'></div>某敢不思所以然，务其大者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209458_comment'></div>初心固在，虽没齿而不移：来效可图，誓捐躯而必往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209458_comment'></div>庶无愧怍，少答生成。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1209458_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在中书舍人职。疏乞至诚终始纳谏。作品：乞至诚终始纳谏疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三二 《乞至诚终始纳谏疏》题下注“元符三年四月”）</span><div id='poem_1209416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞至诚终始纳谏疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209416")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209416'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209416'>臣伏读《虞书》，见舜命群臣作股肱耳目而戒之曰：「予违汝弼，汝无面从，退有后言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209416_comment'></div>夫面从以成其违者，是谀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209416_comment'></div>后言以指其违者，是谤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209416_comment'></div>二者非事君之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209416_comment'></div>有虞之臣皆大贤，岂不知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209416_comment'></div>舜且以此戒焉，是知拂心忤意，非人臣之所乐，在于人君有以导之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209416_comment'></div>此帝舜之圣所以为万世法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209416_comment'></div>臣愚切观陛下即位以来，宪天聪明，首辟言路，旋因日食，亟降诏书，咸使纳忠，无有忌讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209416_comment'></div>言果当理，欣然听从，增秩赐官，风动天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209416_comment'></div>故虽疏远刍荛之贱，莫不鼓舞遭遇，思日罄竭，以补初政之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209416_comment'></div>而况股肱耳目之寄，又安有不尽其忠者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209416_comment'></div>帝舜之圣，今复见于陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209416_comment'></div>然臣观唐太宗乃近古明君，魏郑公且曰：「陛下贞观之初，导人使谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209416_comment'></div>三年以后，见谏者悦而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209416_comment'></div>比一二年，勉强受谏而终不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209416_comment'></div>质以其详，悉有据验」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209416_comment'></div>太宗悟曰：「非公，无能道此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209416_comment'></div>人苦不自觉耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209416_comment'></div>于是知纳谏固难，而谨终尤为难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209416_comment'></div>子思曰：「诚者，物之终始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209416_comment'></div>不诚无物」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209416_comment'></div>伊尹曰：「终始惟一，时乃日新」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209416_comment'></div>彼太宗闻之而悟，真大过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209416_comment'></div>顾不能持以至诚，日新无敝，使郑公不得而窥焉，则其去舜也远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209416_comment'></div>陛下方稽古以御今，如太宗之事，亦愿取以为鉴，以隆太平之伟绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209416_comment'></div>臣又伏思，上书之人所言不一，其泛论大体，指陈邪正，如此类者，自可留之禁中，以备观览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209416_comment'></div>至于陈述利害，事干有司者，即乞降付政府，委官看详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209416_comment'></div>有可施行，旋具闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209416_comment'></div>此则圣诏之出，不为空文，施之国家，固非小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209416_comment'></div>唯陛下留听。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1209416_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在中书舍人职。疏请继述五朝善政。作品：请继述五朝善政疏。<div id='poem_1209411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请继述五朝善政疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209411")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209411'>陛下善继神宗之志，善述神宗之事，孝德至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209411_comment'></div>尚有五朝圣政盛德，愿稽考而继述之，以扬七庙之光，贻福万世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1209411_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在中书舍人职，有铭文。作品：提点刑狱崔君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1209650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>提点刑狱崔君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209650")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209650'>元符三年春，天子既嗣位，妙简畯良，助隆初政，而朝奉郎嘉兴崔君遹孝立实由江南西路提点刑狱召为尚书户部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209650_comment'></div>道病，十月四日次常州无锡而卒，享年五十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209650_comment'></div>母寿光县太君沈氏垂老，子传世尚幼，三女皆未行，诸弟举进士未第，弟之子以贡贺奉表沾恩未出官，上下内外赖君以济，而君逝矣，闻者悲焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209650_comment'></div>其家以建中靖国元年某月某日葬于杭州临安县灵凤乡某所之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209650_comment'></div>其弟适，太学名士也，以君行状来求铭，曰：「君讳仁授之曾孙，国子监丞讳伸之孙，歙州婺源主簿、赠朝散郎讳敏中之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209650_comment'></div>初学即崇义理，不务词章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209650_comment'></div>会神宗以经术取士，遂登乙科，调宣州宣城主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209650_comment'></div>朝廷方选教官，委国子监考所业以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209650_comment'></div>君进《诗说》十卷，丞相王文公称之，擢为夔州教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209650_comment'></div>夔险远，难侍亲以行，辞不赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209650_comment'></div>赴宣城，用荐者迁杭州于潜令，又用荐者改宣德郎、知袁州分宜县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209650_comment'></div>寻丁朝散忧，服阕，知颍昌长社县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209650_comment'></div>户部奏留为校法官，又留驱磨文字，就除干当公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209650_comment'></div>会哲宗复遣常平使者，遂使淮南西路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209650_comment'></div>主义者怼不向己，降通判定州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209650_comment'></div>久之事明，除广南东路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209650_comment'></div>辞以母老，改江南西路，就除提点刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209650_comment'></div>再娶皆殿中侍御史钱公顗之女，长赠德化县君，季封德清县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209650_comment'></div>君侍亲孝，友弟睦，行己待人，一本于义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209650_comment'></div>朝散贫甚，乡有高其节者出缗钱数百千助毕婚嫁，其名虽贷，其实非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209650_comment'></div>君既终丧，乃力自俭约，月储半俸偿之，必其受而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209650_comment'></div>少年登科，声动辇下，公卿争欲妻之以子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209650_comment'></div>不就，曰：『以贵富偶贫贱，肯屈意事吾亲哉』！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209650_comment'></div>钱公方斥监秀州税，乃自请婚焉，又取其季以继其室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209650_comment'></div>诸弟试有司不利，往往连日咨慨，若无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209650_comment'></div>至其绌为通判，则怡然修职如州县时，在宣城复圩田，在于潜去猾吏，民到于今怀其赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209650_comment'></div>绳奸不避要权，荐士必先寒远，与人交久而益固，闻人善不啻如己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209650_comment'></div>有自宣德郎再迁至承议郎，不磨勘者八年，或问其故，曰：『尝梦官至朝奉，母老矣，幸少延以奉甘旨』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209650_comment'></div>已而覃恩自迁其官，乃泫然叹曰：『终于此乎』！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209650_comment'></div>后数月，果不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209650_comment'></div>其生平可知者如此，其惟恐人知与人不得而知者可以推此概见也，念非铭得所托则无以信后世，敢请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209650_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209650_comment'></div>若孝立者，殆庶几所谓躬行君子，仰不愧于天，俯不怍于人者欤，某何足以铭之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209650_comment'></div>然某不敏，孝立取以为友有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209650_comment'></div>去年北归过赣上，相见惊喜，且曰：「自子窜瘴乡，吾母日诵佛书，祝子无恙」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209650_comment'></div>然则孝立虽不可作，所以慰其母夫人无穷之哀思者，敢不勉为铭耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209650_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1209650'>孰不戴天，孰不比人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209650_comment'></div>孰无愧怍，以立其身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209650_comment'></div>安于躬行，是谓君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209650_comment'></div>将圣不亡，我知其与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209650_comment'></div>显岂在位，传岂在嗣，昭如列星，庶其在此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1209650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年3月</a>　疏论论太学生不当以言事殿举。作品：论太学生不当以言事殿举疏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八三二《论太学生不当以言事殿举疏》题下注“建中靖国元年三月”）</span><div id='poem_1209413' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209413' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209413?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论太学生不当以言事殿举疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209413")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209413_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209413'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209413'>臣准中书省刑房送到录黄一道，为太学生张寅亮等妄言裁减皇太后园陵浮费，各殿一举事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209413_comment'></div>臣寻观寅亮等所上书，其言狂谬，固当惩戒以示天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209413_comment'></div>缘士大夫已在选擢而详练滋久者，尤有不能体悉朝廷用意之深，况山野一介布衣之贱乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209413_comment'></div>陛下察其无知，特从轻典，又且追改屏出学、押出门指挥，则是寅亮等固已在所矜容矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209413_comment'></div>止殿一举，诚不为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209413_comment'></div>但近年以来，言路壅塞，为时大弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209413_comment'></div>自陛下劝奖开导，始克通达，世以相贺，获仰太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209413_comment'></div>今寅亮等若未免殿举，窃恐自此以后人复畏避，不敢献言，天下之事，无由周知，亦圣政所当深虑者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209413_comment'></div>《传》不云乎：「乌鸢之卵不毁，而后凤凰集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209413_comment'></div>诽谤之罪不诛，而后良言进」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209413_comment'></div>臣愚亦愿陛下以此赦之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209413_comment'></div>所有录黄，臣未敢签书行下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1209413_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　秋，赐三品服，差同修神宗国史，三具状辞，不允。作品：辞免同修国史奏状。辞免同修国史第二状。辞免同修国史第三状。<div id='poem_1209358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209358?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免同修国史奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209358")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209358'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209358'>闻命惊惶，莫知所处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209358_comment'></div>臣窃观神宗皇帝升遐久已十有七年，而一代信书至今未就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209358_comment'></div>陛下圣孝，既深以为念，必慎择史官，付之论撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209358_comment'></div>岂臣疏贱，所敢参预！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209358_comment'></div>况今英俊布满台阁，其才行学识，率居臣右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209358_comment'></div>改而命之，不惟臣分获安，实足以副陛下显扬先烈之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1209358_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免同修国史第二状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209359")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209359'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209359'>臣虽至愚，既荷圣恩，曲加任使，自当奋厉，求称万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209359_comment'></div>又况神宗皇帝改科造士，臣实执经太学，继蒙赐第，擢为教官，因缘遭逢，以至今日，果于大典可以助致涓埃，亦自当罄竭夙夜，图报长育之恩，岂敢重于辞避？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209359_comment'></div>缘自开院以来，不知所更者几人，所历者几时，而所见不同，互有笔削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209359_comment'></div>近虽已降指挥，兼用新旧《实录》，及《实录》之所不载而明有稽据可参相照者，并听详考事实，书之国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209359_comment'></div>然是非取舍，纷错无绪，必欲相与折衷，以成万世不刊之书，此非臣至愚所能任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209359_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣诚心，特与辞避，以安分愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209359_comment'></div>不胜天地生成之赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1209359_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209360' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209360' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209360?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免同修国史第三状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209360")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209360_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209360'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209360'>恳诚虽至，俞旨未颁，不免倾输，仰祈矜察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209360_comment'></div>窃以文字之职，儒者所荣，擢寘史官，尤更宠异，在臣侥倖，岂可胜言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209360_comment'></div>但臣志学以来，以资质驽钝，痛自刻厉，遂得心疾，每思虑过当，即怔忪不宁，发为口疮，寝食几废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209360_comment'></div>今来修史，惟神宗皇帝盛德大业如青天白日，尚容窥仰万一，其馀群臣事实，皆揉于爱憎，未知所辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209360_comment'></div>正赖心力有馀之人区别是非，以严褒贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209360_comment'></div>而臣所苦，适难勉强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209360_comment'></div>倘因愦乱，取舍失当，则凡厥所书，必至乖戾，传示万世，其害无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209360_comment'></div>此尤臣之所大惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209360_comment'></div>臣荷陛下生成之恩，不啻天地父母，是以辄忘诛戮，冒渎再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209360_comment'></div>敢望圣慈赦其罪而允其请，庶不致以疾缪上误大典。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1209360_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　除依前通直郎，试尚书吏部侍郎，仍赐对衣金带，具状辞，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　除依前通直郎，试尚书吏部侍郎。有铭文。作品：神龙卫四厢都指挥使宁州刺史贾公墓志铭（賈嵒）<div id='poem_1209652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>神龙卫四厢都指挥使宁州刺史贾公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209652")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209652'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209652'>元符初元，哲宗皇帝躬揽之六年也，延见文武之士，殆无虚日，拔其尤者，以隆治功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209652_comment'></div>于是皇城使、威州刺史贾公自权发遣河东路兵马钤辖召对，大合旨，超授神龙卫四厢都指挥使、宁州刺史、权管当侍卫亲军马军司公事、旧城里都巡检使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209652_comment'></div>一时将帅，翕然耸慕，以为遭遇之异有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209652_comment'></div>三年春，哲宗升遐，选为山陵都护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209652_comment'></div>时公疾殆矣，不辞而行，遂以三月二十九日卒于河南永安之宁神院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209652_comment'></div>天子闻之，恻然嗟悼，遣内东头供奉官宋某护丧以归，且敕葬事官为应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209652_comment'></div>特赠雄州防御使，官其二子，又擢其长子为閤门看班祗候，录其季女之夫为三班借职，常赙外加赐白金千两、绢七百，所以恩恤甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209652_comment'></div>其孤以明年，建中靖国元年八月二十五日葬于开封祥符马店村，而承议郎、前权通判兰州军州事俞君次夔状其生平曰：公讳岩，字民瞻，世为开封人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209652_comment'></div>曾大父真、大父信皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209652_comment'></div>父顺，以公贵赠左屯卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209652_comment'></div>母李氏，追封安康郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209652_comment'></div>继母李氏，追封淮安郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209652_comment'></div>公生而警颖，不为儿童事，父母异之，谓必能起家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209652_comment'></div>读书略通其义，酷好弓矢击刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209652_comment'></div>未冠，已志如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209652_comment'></div>一日，慨然叹曰：「大丈夫当自奋立，不然，何以显亲扬名于天下」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209652_comment'></div>遂勉从戎，以骑射称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209652_comment'></div>不数年，迁行门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209652_comment'></div>元丰初，神宗皇帝临轩选才武，遂换内殿承制，为庆州荔源堡兵马都监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209652_comment'></div>泸州夷獠叛，朝廷委环庆路副都总管林广经制其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209652_comment'></div>广首辟公为先锋将，深入蛮徼，通江门，取隘口，粮道无阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209652_comment'></div>讨荡巢穴，几得乞第，斩获三百八十级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209652_comment'></div>帝嘉其劳，特转西京左藏库副使，仍以袍带、介胄、枪牌、茶药赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209652_comment'></div>除河东第三将，未行，权京西第一将，留驻于环庆路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209652_comment'></div>久之，赴河东，任河外准备，牵制兰会贼马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209652_comment'></div>逢西贼于明堂川，俘馘甚众，就除第八将，转庄宅副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209652_comment'></div>哲宗登极，覃恩转右骐骥使，改西京作坊使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209652_comment'></div>今大丞相曾公以龙图阁学士帅太原，奏充准备将领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209652_comment'></div>从副都总管李浩行，逢西贼于满满浪舒啰逻易，击走之，复为第三将，改第七将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209652_comment'></div>从知府州，又充行统制，入界至横水川青鱼河，斩获七十九级，转内园使，就迁权本路兵马都监兼第一将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209652_comment'></div>绍圣初，转东作坊使再任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209652_comment'></div>入界至青冈岭、越祖平、埋迎三岔，斩获四十级，特转宫苑使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209652_comment'></div>寻总领先锋，至橐驼巷左监军司，逢西贼，力战，斩获一百七十级，焚荡族帐、器械、仓廪尤多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209652_comment'></div>四年春，西贼数万围麟州神堂寨甚急，公亟拥骑四百出援，且令汉蕃士卒曰：「国家无事时不惜厚禄畜养尔辈，正以待一旦仓卒之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209652_comment'></div>今虽众寡不敌，岂可坐视而不救？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209652_comment'></div>吾誓以死报国」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209652_comment'></div>莫不感激，奋励争前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209652_comment'></div>径由屈野河川、杨家墓行五里许，回视河西沙堰子、染拔谷、青草会，则贼骑已不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209652_comment'></div>公因念韩信背水阵以取胜，乃据北栏道坡岭上，使四无所向，人人用命，自旦至暮，相持不决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209652_comment'></div>公矢一发中酋领，应弦而倒，众即遁去，重围遂释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209652_comment'></div>是日微公，神堂破矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209652_comment'></div>帝闻而嘉叹，亟以袍带、枪牌、弓矢、茶药赐之，特转皇城使，又加威州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209652_comment'></div>援筑葭芦寨，至吐浑河，掩袭真卿流、贺罗峰、没宁流，斩获三十二级，牛马橐驼千数，葭芦遂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209652_comment'></div>又挠耕至桑泊，逢西贼，力战，贼败遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209652_comment'></div>追至啰没王河，斩获七十级，生擒伪钤辖乜香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209652_comment'></div>元符初，就除权发遣本路兵马钤辖兼第一将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209652_comment'></div>既入对对，首谕「神堂功久在朕听」，公惶恐称谢，且条奏边事甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209652_comment'></div>帝深器之，遂擢管库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209652_comment'></div>是岁郊礼，管当法驾、卤簿、仪仗、兵队，以整肃闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1209652_comment'></div>今天子登极，覃恩转濠州围练使，迁侍卫亲军步军都虞候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1209652_comment'></div>既受命为都护，促行，家人以疾久，力劝止之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1209652_comment'></div>公叱曰：「吾本一介行伍，蒙国厚恩，未有毫发补报，可辞行耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1209652_comment'></div>力疾上道，以至于卒，享年五十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1209652_comment'></div>娶席氏，封普安郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1209652_comment'></div>子男五人：长曰诜，右班殿直、閤门看班祗候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1209652_comment'></div>次曰说，曰咏，曰谌，曰详，皆右班殿直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1209652_comment'></div>女六人，长适右班殿直边公绰，次适进士高建一，次适进士折可畏，次适右班殿直彭鉴，次适进士李孝纯，次许嫁三班借职袁思永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1209652_comment'></div>公天姿特挺，沈毅有谋，望之凛凛不可犯，天下奇男子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1209652_comment'></div>事继母如嫡，人不知其为异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1209652_comment'></div>在河外时，或欲率其子入界，公曰：「吾子技未精，果行，不免冒赏以欺朝廷，吾不忍为」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1209652_comment'></div>将兵二十年，战未尝北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1209652_comment'></div>士卒中伤，必载以归，躬自抚视，完复乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1209652_comment'></div>与人周旋，惟恐不尽，轻财乐施，家无馀蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1209652_comment'></div>每公退，即延儒者讲论书史，教诸子以忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1209652_comment'></div>巨公名卿荐之者踰六十人，尤为今大丞相曾公所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1209652_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1209652_comment'></div>孰谓弗克寿考以享富贵之盛而止矣，宜有铭以告后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1209652_comment'></div>其孤遂以状来求铭，予尝闻俞君言其先公天章阁待制充帅环庆时，力荐公于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1209652_comment'></div>天章没，公画像祠之，岁久益虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1209652_comment'></div>盖不忘俞公如此，宜其忠于报国虽出万死而不顾也，是诚有过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1209652_comment'></div>于是序而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1209652_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_1209652'>赫赫神宗，文武生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1209652_comment'></div>作新多士，以大有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1209652_comment'></div>士患不才，才亟用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1209652_comment'></div>智信仁勇，各适其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1209652_comment'></div>惠此中国，服彼四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1209652_comment'></div>天高地厚，孰得以窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1209652_comment'></div>于时贾公，拔自行伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1209652_comment'></div>何以况之，如罴如虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1209652_comment'></div>帝曰汝才，协济吾武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1209652_comment'></div>夙夜行门，非汝宜处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1209652_comment'></div>往事兵戎，往勤捍御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1209652_comment'></div>我有成军，今兹将汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1209652_comment'></div>开迹泸南，继踵河东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1209652_comment'></div>干戈所向，未尝不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1209652_comment'></div>敌谁为坚，贼谁为雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1209652_comment'></div>奋不旋顾，必摧其锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1209652_comment'></div>尤卓异者，神堂之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1209652_comment'></div>如古将帅，凛凛英风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1209652_comment'></div>简在哲庙，虽久不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1209652_comment'></div>趣其入对，有谋而藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1209652_comment'></div>帝益嘉叹，擢护岩廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1209652_comment'></div>恩殊秩峻，耸动多方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1209652_comment'></div>念德莫报，陵役是当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1209652_comment'></div>忽其逝矣，天子恻伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1209652_comment'></div>今天子圣，绍隆先帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1209652_comment'></div>卧鼓灭烽，蛮夷慕义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1209652_comment'></div>将臣熙熙，雅歌自喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1209652_comment'></div>同我太平，长守富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1209652_comment'></div>公独胡为，未老而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1209652_comment'></div>尚其子孙，不坠厥世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_100_1209652_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年8月</a>　除依前通直郎，试尚书吏部侍郎。有文。作品：封还陈瓘出外录黄疏。<div id='poem_1209418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>封还陈瓘出外录黄疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209418")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209418'>瓘素以声闻推重一时，今到都司，曾未逾月，遽令出外，恐非所以示天下而慰公议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209418_comment'></div>伏望收还新命，以全朝廷待士之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209418_comment'></div>所有录黄，未敢签书行下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1209418_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年9月</a>　在依前通直郎，试尚书吏部侍郎职。有铭文。作品：中大夫直龙图阁知青州军州事王公墓志铭（王说）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八四五《中大夫直龙图阁知青州军州事王公墓志铭（王说）》题下注“建中靖國元年九月”）</span><div id='poem_1209653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中大夫直龙图阁知青州军州事王公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209653")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209653'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209653'>公王氏，讳说，字岩夫，其先自太原徙真定，又徙洛阳，今为洛阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209653_comment'></div>曾大父彬，赠太师、中书令兼尚书令、崇国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209653_comment'></div>大父化基，礼部尚书，赠太师、中书令兼尚书令、魏国公，谥惠献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209653_comment'></div>父举正，太子少傅致仕，赠太师，中书令兼尚书令、祁国公，谥安简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209653_comment'></div>公家自魏公始大，祁公继之，皆辅政忠清亮直，达于三朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209653_comment'></div>公世贵，幼喜学问自修，虽以荫得官，竟取进士第，自太常寺太祝迁光禄寺丞，著作佐郎，秘书丞，太常博士，尚书屯田、都官、职方员外郎，屯田、都官郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209653_comment'></div>官制行，改朝散大夫，转朝请、朝议、左中散大夫，拜中大夫，加直龙图阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209653_comment'></div>勋上柱国，爵河南郡开国侯，食邑一千三百户，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209653_comment'></div>历管当在京马军粮料院、马步军专计司，西京、陕府、河阳、郑州提辖收捉私盐，通判滑州、相州，知卫州、常州、临江军、晋州、徐州，尚书仓部郎中，知密州、泾州，尚书祠部郎中，知相州、太府少卿，知郑州、荆南府、澶州、河阳、河中府、邓州，兼京西南路安抚使，青州，兼京东东路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209653_comment'></div>建中靖国元年十六日，终于青州治所，享年七十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209653_comment'></div>初为卫州，年甫三十，适天下久无事，法度寖弛，吏袭欺罔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209653_comment'></div>顾公甚少，裕然儒者，易之，抱案却立，视公所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209653_comment'></div>公徐为裁决，皆中几要，时有纵舍，不可摇夺，吏始畏服，旋以治闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209653_comment'></div>常州士喜学，公为延致名儒临川王安国平甫教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209653_comment'></div>平甫时虽布衣，义甚高，非贤有礼弗就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209653_comment'></div>既从公游，士人慕乡，自远而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209653_comment'></div>未几，朝廷改科，专用经术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209653_comment'></div>常之士试开封、礼部及策于廷皆第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209653_comment'></div>已而相属为从官、郎吏、二千石者甚众，世益以为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209653_comment'></div>临江介于虔、吉，俗喜斗，多诞谩，富室子杀人，赂人代之，狱具辞服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209653_comment'></div>公顾谓曰：「汝顾利许人以死，独不为父母妻子计乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209653_comment'></div>囚色动，具以情告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209653_comment'></div>民安于习俗，吏恬不加察，公以一言得之，远近欢颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209653_comment'></div>晋人朴厚，尤乐公简易，力请于朝，为留五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209653_comment'></div>常有调发兴作，聚民于庭，喻以利害，戒以期信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209653_comment'></div>民相先从之，未尝告劳，至被玺书褒谕，劳赐金帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209653_comment'></div>徐得巨盗，久讯不承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209653_comment'></div>及公至，专以恩信为治，囚闻之，泣曰：「我曹幸当平世，何苦如此，不过吏迫之急耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209653_comment'></div>今幸得公，虽不获自新，复忍欺之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209653_comment'></div>愿抵罪无恨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209653_comment'></div>由是盗益销靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209653_comment'></div>相州洪福寺火，逻卒救止，因有所攘，连逮颇众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209653_comment'></div>公曰：「始需其功，旋治其罪，后有警，何以使人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209653_comment'></div>且及无辜，吾不忍也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209653_comment'></div>乃令自陈，坐者无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209653_comment'></div>后公从子行境中，夜半车乘相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209653_comment'></div>或谓其徒前此能如是乎，从子问之，曰：「吾境多寇夺，为行旅患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209653_comment'></div>今郡守以诚置人腹中，奸偷不忍挠之，因得夜行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209653_comment'></div>从子以告，公曰：「兹适岁丰耳，岂吾所能哉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209653_comment'></div>郑当元丰时，地狭民贫，不能输役，废为县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209653_comment'></div>后复为州，且更用差役法取办境内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209653_comment'></div>绍圣初复免役，诏以八事，尤先裕民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209653_comment'></div>公会属邑令议于州，择其善者奏行之，岁弛缗万有奇，民尤以为德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209653_comment'></div>湖北兵与湖南并将，因更戍岭外，涉横、钦、廉、象四州之境，多死亡者，以故难于招募，且乏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209653_comment'></div>公谓广西被边之地，移兵于其境内，则习瘴疠，无甚惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209653_comment'></div>湖南北兵交驻潭、桂，则近戍而不劳，又控扼衡、荆，缓急可用，仍不畏死，乐于应募，有五利焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209653_comment'></div>条列以闻，朝廷嘉纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209653_comment'></div>大河东流，新堤始完，主者惧力怯冲垫，阴决下流以杀其势，水泛溢平野，澶州、清德军皆被害，州县顾望，莫敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209653_comment'></div>公即奏曰：「吏畏罪过甚，乃移患于民，愿亟察之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1209653_comment'></div>朝廷遂遣使相视，塞决口，民以安堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1209653_comment'></div>河阳夹河为城，会秋雨甚水大至，城不没者数板，州人惴恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1209653_comment'></div>时公已年七十馀，曰：「吾为守，与城存亡者也，虽老，敢自爱」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1209653_comment'></div>即率寮属，躬为顾指，得其要害，冒雨督治，逮暮不少休，众益安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1209653_comment'></div>治逾二年，无犯死刑者，有芝生于厅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1209653_comment'></div>今天子即位之初，公自河中移邓州，请入觐，对称旨，擢拜太中大夫、知青州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1209653_comment'></div>议者谓太中仪物视从官，不当叙迁，公亦坚辞，改直龙图阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1209653_comment'></div>公素康强，未尝卧疾，一日会亲族燕饮，言笑自如，夜分安坐而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1209653_comment'></div>公到青才半月，然民已怀公，为罢歌乐屠宰者累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1209653_comment'></div>公性宽大浑厚，不见圭角，明白洞达，内外如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1209653_comment'></div>遇人无贵贱皆为之尽礼，虽欺罔诞谩，一以诚报之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1209653_comment'></div>闻人之善，惟恐不及，至过恶，则为掩覆芘护，虽亲密不以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1209653_comment'></div>尝有所厚，虽或负公，益不忍伤其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1209653_comment'></div>故虽悍戾偷薄之士，始见之而肆，中则愧，终则畏服而敬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1209653_comment'></div>平居怡然，能自娱适，毁誉休戚不以干虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1209653_comment'></div>视宗族极恩，专荫补多及疏远，与交游终始无穷达之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1209653_comment'></div>其为政以忠厚仁恕为本，扶善抑恶，销绝奸慝，不喜近功小效，搜摘隐微，悦可人意，不饰繁文末节，驰声誉，苟进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1209653_comment'></div>僚吏能否，皆因任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1209653_comment'></div>既各尽其材，又为之揄扬荐达，期于成就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1209653_comment'></div>或阽于罪戾，必反覆戒谕，终不废逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1209653_comment'></div>告以善则欣然从之，如自己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1209653_comment'></div>有所为，后有言其非是者，亟为改易，无愧词吝色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1209653_comment'></div>前后守十五州、历五朝，政治损益尤多，平心一意，无所观望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1209653_comment'></div>仕皆循次，未尝骤进，亦终身不挂吏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1209653_comment'></div>然所临皆要藩剧郡，当天下全盛之际，人物阜蕃，兵革销弭，各因其俗，治以无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1209653_comment'></div>出入休显，垂四十年，康宁寿考，为世荣观，近世名卿未之及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1209653_comment'></div>自魏、祁相继显用，公复与兄诲、子瑜并以器能进擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1209653_comment'></div>其使大辽，实兄弟相先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1209653_comment'></div>其在相州，瑜适守滑，夹河相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1209653_comment'></div>长婿为枢密直学士，更践要剧，亦复与公同时，时论美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1209653_comment'></div>公喜学，晚而不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1209653_comment'></div>有文集二十卷，诗集十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1209653_comment'></div>娶钱氏，河南郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1209653_comment'></div>李氏，河内郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1209653_comment'></div>薛氏，河东郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1209653_comment'></div>子男三人：瑜，朝奉大夫、京东路转运使，先公而卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1209653_comment'></div>琮，知相州录事参军、河北路盐事司干办公事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1209653_comment'></div>璆，太庙斋郎，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1209653_comment'></div>女八人，长适枢密直学士孙览，次适承议郎李去盈，次适通直郎杨彦章，早卒，次适承议郎陈扶，次适瀛州防御推官许子卿，馀并早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1209653_comment'></div>孙男四人，良冶郊社斋郎，良史、良质并假承务郎，良式尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1209653_comment'></div>孙女三人，长适承议郎、尚书比部员外郎周绅，次适颍昌府观察判官孙俟，一尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1209653_comment'></div>曾孙男大伦，郊社斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1209653_comment'></div>曾孙女一人，未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1209653_comment'></div>其孤既以其年九月十五日葬于河南府洛阳县大樊村行茔之次，属尚书礼部员外郎荣君辑状公行事，求铭于浩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1209653_comment'></div>浩为颍昌府教授，时公之子瑜提点刑狱，辱知甚厚，又与公之孙良冶友好，盖尝闻公居家历官安于为善，绝口不以语人，故虽子孙亦莫得而知其详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1209653_comment'></div>然自其所可知以推其所不可知，信贤矣哉，乃为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_94_1209653'>孰不从仕，仕或谋身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1209653_comment'></div>孰不为善，善或近名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1209653_comment'></div>有贤王公，中道是循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1209653_comment'></div>弗屈乎己，弗异乎人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1209653_comment'></div>孰险孰易，孰疏孰亲，五朝四方，一以其诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1209653_comment'></div>身名从之，迄用有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1209653_comment'></div>其闻显矣，其心则纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1209653_comment'></div>不见有物，为吾死生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1209653_comment'></div>安坐而逝，世益公贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1209653_comment'></div>安简之子，惠献之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1209653_comment'></div>亘千万年，俨其如存。</div><div id='poem_sentence_104_1209653_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年11月</a>　郊礼覃恩，父保之公赠朝奉郎，母张氏封安康郡太君，夫人沈氏封蓬莱县君，奏弟泂假承务郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　是年国是纷更，蔡京起用，故公与游定夫先生相继乞外补。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在京，有铭文。作品：孙君墓志铭（孙惟吉）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八四五 《孙君墓志铭（孙惟吉）》题下注“崇宁元年正月”）</span><div id='poem_1209651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209651")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209651'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209651'>君讳惟吉，字正之，远祖潜五代时为武进令而卒，子孙因家焉，遂为武进人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209651_comment'></div>自曾大父以来，皆传一子，且不寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209651_comment'></div>君之父幼孤而贫，外氏欲嫁其母，毅然止之，力修子职，以成其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209651_comment'></div>君甫数岁，知父孝如此，于是以家事自任曰：「岂宜复累吾亲哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209651_comment'></div>比长，赀益饶裕，所以致其养者无不如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209651_comment'></div>迄于寿终，与人通财，虽嫠妇稚子，未尝一毫非义，曰：「人纵可欺，如吾心何」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209651_comment'></div>里有急难，赖君以济不知几人，初无德色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209651_comment'></div>视子孙可教者悉遣之学，辟馆聚书，宾延高士以充养其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209651_comment'></div>故其子溪以文学行义名于东南，贡于礼部，且将显用于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209651_comment'></div>其馀若孙皆刻厉有立志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209651_comment'></div>晚奉释氏甚笃，苟可以致其诚者无不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209651_comment'></div>一日，忽不食，条处后事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209651_comment'></div>后三日，沐浴，戒诸子曰：「五鼓寺钟鸣，亟告我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209651_comment'></div>及期，索水盥手，合掌而坐，良久就枕，则逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209651_comment'></div>实建中靖国元年六月十有九日也，享年七十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209651_comment'></div>娶符氏，前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209651_comment'></div>子男五人，长即溪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209651_comment'></div>次豁、裕、谹、谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209651_comment'></div>女六人，适谈渊、潭元康、江通、蒋中美、张郛、陈中行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209651_comment'></div>孙男七人，蒙亨、谦亨、丰亨、焕亨、知微、知彰、知柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209651_comment'></div>孙女五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209651_comment'></div>溪等卜以明年，崇宁元年正月四日葬于县之怀德北乡平冈村夫人符氏之茔，走京师求予铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209651_comment'></div>予与溪友善，不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209651_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1209651'>不恤其身，以安其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209651_comment'></div>不专其利，以其义成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209651_comment'></div>有丰其报，其子则贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209651_comment'></div>君为不亡，以永其传。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1209651_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　官试尚书兵部侍郎。有谢表。作品：改除兵部侍郎谢表。<div id='poem_1209341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209341?labeling=true' target='_blank'>改除兵部侍郎谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209341")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209341_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209341'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209341'>臣浩言：伏奉敕命，特授依前通直郎、试尚书兵部侍郎，差遣、赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209341_comment'></div>易以兵曹，便其史职，载惟优渥，第切兢荣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209341_comment'></div>伏念臣资禀至愚，仕逢昌运，荷上圣并容之异，预清朝委任之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209341_comment'></div>比自西垣，擢居选部，所掌适司于右列，其繁尤倍于他曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209341_comment'></div>惟专夙夜之勤，方称铨衡之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209341_comment'></div>而臣猥兼笔削，甫历秋冬，顾用志之难分，惧收功之弗逮，敢图昭察，亟赐迁除！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209341_comment'></div>虽故事之具存，实殊恩之曲被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209341_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下仁如天覆，明并日升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209341_comment'></div>凫短鹤长，均受生成之造；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209341_comment'></div>越南燕北，悉蒙临照之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209341_comment'></div>是致驽材，亦叨器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209341_comment'></div>臣敢不益坚宿愿，勉跂前修，庶殚犬马之劳，少效涓埃之报。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1209341_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　春，复具状乞外补。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　夏，充宝文阁待制、知江宁府兼管内劝农使，充江南东路兵马钤辖，仍加武骑尉，封文安县开国男，食邑三百户，赐如故。公具状辞免职名，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年3月</a>　在京城。有铭文。作品：真淡先生唐公墓誌銘（唐既）<div id='poem_1209654' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209654' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209654?labeling=true' target='_blank'>真淡先生唐公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209654")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209654_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209654'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209654'>唐氏远矣，世不乏人，惟晋昌、太原、京兆、秦州、北海五族最显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209654_comment'></div>天复中，建威军推官名希颜者避地钱塘，生仁恭，为盐铁判官，赠太子太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209654_comment'></div>太保生谓，为通儒院学士，从忠懿归本朝，出守秭归，因家江陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209654_comment'></div>终职方郎中，赠太子太傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209654_comment'></div>今江陵、钱塘之族皆出自北海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209654_comment'></div>太傅生极，才气爽拔，与孙何齐名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209654_comment'></div>弱冠登甲科，又与寇莱公为忘年交，丁晋公为布衣旧，略不为之屈，以故仕不脱州县，弃官去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209654_comment'></div>其后谢公绛判流内铨，疏其节以闻，特转大理寺丞，迁殿中丞致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209654_comment'></div>生一子，是为处士愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209654_comment'></div>处士尚幼，慨贫无以养，乃捐书力穑，亟成其家，以适亲意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209654_comment'></div>先生处士第四子也，母某氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209654_comment'></div>先生讳既，字潜亨，又取水一火二，号真淡翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209654_comment'></div>先生始生，殿中君仰观而占曰：「水躔翼轸，楚分也，法主文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209654_comment'></div>吾孙骨相异，其有以亢吾宗乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209654_comment'></div>初学，即与其兄子思寝食自励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209654_comment'></div>子思亦先生流亚也，乡人以此庆处士有子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209654_comment'></div>稍长游太学，同舍老生对之歛容，不敢惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209654_comment'></div>伯父质肃公介方参大政，爱叹以为类己，奏试主簿于将作监，锁其厅中，别试异等，声动场屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209654_comment'></div>丁处士忧，服除，不复赴礼部，山林独往之意于是萌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209654_comment'></div>亲友勉之，调渝州巴县尉，非其好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209654_comment'></div>未几谢去，筑室于汉水之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209654_comment'></div>居且完，顾书籍犹假于人，遂走吴、粤，悉售以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209654_comment'></div>掩关却扫，凡二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209654_comment'></div>始也日有所为，以若干为准，虽寒暑风雨不废，以为积小致高大当如此，故于书无所不读，于事无所不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209654_comment'></div>而终也自守其约，于象数之外，不药不卧，不箑不纩，草衣藿食，往往辟谷，日诵《易》、《老子》、《黄庭》一过而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209654_comment'></div>尝曰：「在《易》之《泰》，后以财成天地之道，辅相天地之宜，以左右民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209654_comment'></div>君子体之，则亦财成辅相，以左右身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209654_comment'></div>吾非悦生而恶死，所以尊生者，上以报生我之施，下以善吾死耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209654_comment'></div>人有疑其不置像设者，曰：「覆载俯仰，皆神明也，岂像设所能尽耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209654_comment'></div>吾事之以道，自谓勤香火者无以过也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209654_comment'></div>其所养盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209654_comment'></div>吏部尚书彭公汝励按刑京西，时就见之，自以为弗及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209654_comment'></div>左司谏孙公谔为淮安守，闻且过郡迎谒归心焉，至阖城扉留之，画其像以慰其别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209654_comment'></div>自馀名人豪士有获际者，睹其貌庞眉頍颡，天庭骨隐起如径寸珠，听其言纵横无滞輆，若决积水于千仞之溪，靡不罔然自失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209654_comment'></div>以故通经者服其得先儒未决之秘，博古者服其贯方册所载之详，修真者服其造一气未形之先，善书者服其妙八角垂芒之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209654_comment'></div>下至百工众技，亦皆服其巧出意表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209654_comment'></div>然先生初不以此自多也，遇人有所不及，人自服之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209654_comment'></div>或曰：「此特往而不能返者，奚为哉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209654_comment'></div>及观其语学者，则曰：「古之人身包形器，物来则任以形器之所宜，固有历聘以观其可不可与有行者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209654_comment'></div>若合不合，则归于道之兴废焉，或运天下如反掌，或准天下以言行，其致一也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209654_comment'></div>又尝因诏求言，欲令其子条列复井田、修废官之说以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209654_comment'></div>彼以为往而不能返者，果知先生也邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209654_comment'></div>门人魏倚取孔子所谓「隐居以求其志，行义以达其道」者概之，几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209654_comment'></div>教子务充其德性，且曰：「良能富于己，何得为贫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209654_comment'></div>识者皆贵之，何得为贱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209654_comment'></div>此天下真富贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209654_comment'></div>汝能自立足矣，馀听命可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209654_comment'></div>惇叙姻族，尤有恩义，贫不给者衣食之婚嫁之，死则哭之寝门，以尽其礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209654_comment'></div>将逝之年，玩《易》不去手，每有所得，必肃衣冠，北向稽首，以为目中了然见六十四卦定位于天地之间，庶几不为仁智所域，与昔日以意致之有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1209654_comment'></div>但神机不可轻以告人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1209654_comment'></div>一日，忽屏人，独居家，人意其不快，呼医，遽止之曰：「吾无苦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1209654_comment'></div>然谆谆赞《易》，以为道之至数，孔子言之，妙不违则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1209654_comment'></div>天且有则，况其凡乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1209654_comment'></div>老子言道，大体而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1209654_comment'></div>默推此语，殆于数之至神者先受之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1209654_comment'></div>后十日，命汎扫道室，听医诊脉，平不异他日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1209654_comment'></div>俄而正坐，妻子环侍，了无一语，俨若假寐然逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1209654_comment'></div>自启手足至大歛，体温如平生，实元符三年九月二十日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1209654_comment'></div>前此，昼有白星陨道室前，乃先生生日八月八日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1209654_comment'></div>越月而逝，异矣夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1209654_comment'></div>享年五十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1209654_comment'></div>娶陈氏，左中散大夫习之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1209654_comment'></div>知书，有贤德，能佐先生立其家而成其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1209654_comment'></div>子男长曰愗，次曰悊，习举进士，修身慎行，似先生者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1209654_comment'></div>先生流泽，其由此而光乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1209654_comment'></div>幼男节与二女皆早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1209654_comment'></div>文稿十五卷，《邦典》二卷，《易论》三卷，门人集所闻为《说约》十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1209654_comment'></div>其家卜以崇宁元年三月甲申葬先生于襄阳县隆山之东原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1209654_comment'></div>前期，愗持魏倚状走京师属铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1209654_comment'></div>呜呼，先生于浩厚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1209654_comment'></div>尝谓知其心者，天下一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1209654_comment'></div>前年九月，浩以谏官论事狂妄窜新州，先生留荆门待焉，诲告纤悉，无所不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1209654_comment'></div>既别，明日又追路语曰：「我昨夕深念尚有某事未竟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1209654_comment'></div>浩窃疑之，先生宝练神气，面有孺子色，而浩方且穷处瘴氛必死之地，不复相见决矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1209654_comment'></div>孰谓未一年，浩偶蒙恩生还，而先生奄忽与化俱耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1209654_comment'></div>浩教授襄阳时，见先生本《周官》以释《春秋》，谓之《邦典》，因劝尽释诸经，以发吾覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1209654_comment'></div>先生约五十五岁成之，又孰谓五十四而先生逝耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1209654_comment'></div>庄子曰「死生无变于己」，而况利害之端乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1209654_comment'></div>先生平日齐家与检身等，教子与正心等，固未尝顷刻置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1209654_comment'></div>而将逝之际，乃独不留一语，盖不知所以忘而忘焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1209654_comment'></div>至矣乎，非死生无变于己而能若是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1209654_comment'></div>使其家不以铭见属，独当自以文字发潜德之幽光，矧其子不远千里，匍匐踵门，哀诉如此其勤乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1209654_comment'></div>于是掇其遗事，论次而为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1209654_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_1209654'>其传有书，其似有子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1209654_comment'></div>其不可得而泯者，无所终穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1209654_comment'></div>其五十有四者，数而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1209654_comment'></div>光莫隆乎日月，大莫外乎天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1209654_comment'></div>万物各正性命于其间，孰能妙无己以为己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1209654_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1209654_comment'></div>亘千古而常今，先生其在此。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_1209654'></div><div id='poem_sentence_89_1209654_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　改知杭州未赴，寻改知越州。六月八日，出京。作品：改除越州谢表。<div id='poem_1209339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>改除越州谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209339")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209339'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209339'>清华内阁，表率名藩，并冒殊私，不胜至幸<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209339_comment'></div>伏念臣姿惟固陋，运偶昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209339_comment'></div>神宗推道德以育材，窃处师儒之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209339_comment'></div>哲庙揽乾刚以述事，叨为耳目之官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209339_comment'></div>逮上圣之继兴，躐群英而骤用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209339_comment'></div>恩深骨肉，固已绝于身谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209339_comment'></div>义迫威颜，乃重陈于亲意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209339_comment'></div>侵寻半载，冒昧累章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209339_comment'></div>荷鸿造之曲成，俾便乡而出守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209339_comment'></div>曾未几日，就更两州，皆二浙之上游，为一时之盛选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209339_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下道遵尧舜，治越成康，广形孝弟之风，丕变华夷之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209339_comment'></div>天慈所被，物愿毕从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209339_comment'></div>是致愚诚，获蒙睿察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209339_comment'></div>臣敢不深惟遭遇，勉企循良！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209339_comment'></div>昔侍燕闲，既奉宽仁之训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209339_comment'></div>今居屏翰，誓殚宣布之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209339_comment'></div>庶有见于抚绥，以无惭于报塞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1209339_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年6月8日</a>　六月八日，出京，有诗。作品：追思去岁此日出京。<div id='poem_516488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_516488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/516488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追思去岁今日出京有作<span class='inlineComment2'>（癸未六月八日作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年6月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_516488")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_516488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_516488'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_516488'>解船东下出都门，倏已弥年讵可论。<div id='poem_sentence_0_516488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_516488'>圣主只应怜旧物，归欤朝夕被深恩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_516488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_516488'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_516488_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title

-----title
扬州
-----detail
