<div class='label1' id='23509ff0ed4c4c2ba9f8da9ae609c93d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("23509ff0ed4c4c2ba9f8da9ae609c93d");'><span id='23509ff0ed4c4c2ba9f8da9ae609c93d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1087')">1084-1087年</a>，25-28岁</div><div id='23509ff0ed4c4c2ba9f8da9ae609c93d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年8月</a>　到扬州任。有文。作品：祭苏丞相颂文。<div id='poem_1209695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209695?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭苏丞相文<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年闰六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209695")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209695'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209695'>惟崇宁元年岁次壬午闰六月甲寅朔，具位邹某谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于故丞相、司空苏公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209695_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209695_comment'></div>惟先祖都官与先公太师同登天禧三年进士第，分好深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209695_comment'></div>公以其故，待某甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209695_comment'></div>爰自甲子仲秋，初见公于持丧广陵之际，迨至庚辰孟冬再别，今于归老丹阳之后，十七年间，公既教诲之，使学通古今；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209695_comment'></div>又品题之，使名闻于时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209695_comment'></div>又陶冶而成就之，使获遇于圣明之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209695_comment'></div>某虽愚不肖，窃冀进不负君，退不辱亲，不为名教罪人，以答恩德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209695_comment'></div>然久之未能也，而公逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209695_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209695_comment'></div>公由馆阁隮侍从，至于宰相，其于书无所不记，于事无所不能，为朝廷蓍龟，为海宇模楷，盖虽三尺童子，莫不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209695_comment'></div>若其运动枢极，绥靖华夷，智必用乎几先，功每收乎形外，天下阴受其赐而莫睹其迹，则虽贤士大夫有不知也，某亦安能言之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209695_comment'></div>然某尝闻公之绪言矣，学至于绝学，心至于忘心，消息盈虚，自与时会，世虽欲亲疏利害之，不可得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209695_comment'></div>然则公之所以出处，其本于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209695_comment'></div>不然，何扬历五朝，备更万事，而从容终始，一归于正耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209695_comment'></div>虽然，在公为无足言者，姑以荐诚意、侑奠觞而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209695_comment'></div>公骑箕尾，宁来歆鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209695_comment'></div>尚享！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1209695_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　在扬州任。与吕公著交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　在扬州任。有文。作品：四柏赋。谢吕运使启。<div id='poem_1209146' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209146' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209146?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四柏赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209146")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209146_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209146'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209146'>广陵学官厅尝为夫子庙，今所居之堂即其殿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209146_comment'></div>庭植四柏，皆凛凛合抱，爱之而赋云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209146_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1209146'>瞻广陵之寂历兮，直高堂之峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209146_comment'></div>薙蔓草以如拭兮，伟四柏之亭亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209146_comment'></div>叶委盖以固覆兮，干耸崒以上征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209146_comment'></div>根盘薄而石老兮，皮皴皵以龙惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209146_comment'></div>俨相揖以成列兮，何意气之不可凌！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209146_comment'></div>岂商山逸叟见邀于子房兮，将以翼储君而经营？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209146_comment'></div>抑康庐胜友自得于莲社兮，方且傲当世而洁清？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209146_comment'></div>想昔日之巍然广殿兮，对先圣以交荣，如子路、曾晰、冉有、公西华之侍坐兮，垂绅端拱，各控其素志之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209146_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209146_comment'></div>余德至陋，缪膺教职，获与柏而相值，如亲炙夫盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209146_comment'></div>讲习之馀，将迎之隙，既弗嗜于杯盘，又兼忘于射奕，必往来柏阴，吟哦其侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209146_comment'></div>绵日月以居多，豁聪明而有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209146_comment'></div>其朝暮也，蔼瑞露以冥冥，驻归云而凝碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209146_comment'></div>其四时也，谢群芳之争妍，憩薰风而暑释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209146_comment'></div>筛蟾光之十分，封雪霜而玉皪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209146_comment'></div>若乃琼花兮一本，芍药兮千畦，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1209146", 1209146, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>蕙兰</span>馥郁乎亭槛，锦绮焜煌乎涂泥，上由刺史，爰逮黔黎，咸择地而置酒，纷踵继以车驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209146_comment'></div>曾此柏之不顾兮，其青青固自若也，岂以此自少而遂衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209146_comment'></div>及夫时运遄往，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1209146", 1209146, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>木帝</span>无为，骤雨滂沱以涤荡，狂飙奔腾而折摧，昔蕃鲜兮何在，今寂寞兮空枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209146_comment'></div>使当年之好事，惨搔首以兴悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209146_comment'></div>独此柏之不变兮，其青青固自若也，亦岂以此自多而增奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209146_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209146_comment'></div>柏之所以为柏兮，其常德若兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209146_comment'></div>仆幸得之而深兮，胜老马以为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209146_comment'></div>允蹈贤圣所期于学者，死而后已兮，肯以穷达异其毫釐！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209146_comment'></div>庶几无愧乎柏之常德兮，不为君子之弃而小人之归。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1209146_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209433' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209433' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209433?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢吕运使启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209433")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209433_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209433'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209433'>抱虚承乏，曾唐最之蔑闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209433_comment'></div>容众匿瑕，荷祢章之漫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209433_comment'></div>恩随幸至，感与惭并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209433_comment'></div>伏念某抱犊陋资，羹藜微族，早惧沉沦于流俗，常思髣髴于英躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209433_comment'></div>周王作人，丕变辟雍之制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209433_comment'></div>汉关弃传，猥从俊乂之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209433_comment'></div>欲成器以未能，忽文科而误中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209433_comment'></div>主民书于吴会，未展寸长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209433_comment'></div>董教法于泮宫，继叨试可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209433_comment'></div>轩然师席，固片善之匪宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209433_comment'></div>蕞尔鲰生，庶相长之多益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209433_comment'></div>况维扬之乡校，实淮甸之贤关，简编鳞袭而几无孑遗，岁月驹驰而似不我与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209433_comment'></div>誓以将迎之暇，不荒讲习之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209433_comment'></div>群经之所以幽深，诸史之所以博洽，爰逮颛门之学，纷如百子之书，悉皆口诵而心惟，冀或月将而日就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209433_comment'></div>道德性命，造默默之忘言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209433_comment'></div>治乱兴衰，究寥寥之已事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209433_comment'></div>用居今日，不愧古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209433_comment'></div>虽自处以迪兹，顾当官而何补？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209433_comment'></div>岂如他职，号曰亲民，各戮力于猷为，能有功于州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209433_comment'></div>以是相准，益见无堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209433_comment'></div>宜其推毂之弗加，重以守株之太拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209433_comment'></div>非礼勿动，未尝摇尾以乞怜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209433_comment'></div>在邦必闻，每戒枉寻而直尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209433_comment'></div>忘怀白论，第顾清谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209433_comment'></div>奈何迂疏，辄当鉴拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209433_comment'></div>不求而得，克昭特达之知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209433_comment'></div>曷为其然，时乃大公之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209433_comment'></div>伏惟某官天资忠厚，人物优隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209433_comment'></div>果益振于家风，动有称于圣世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209433_comment'></div>霜雪既降，坚一节而不渝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209433_comment'></div>金玉其相，掩群材而尤异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209433_comment'></div>辄自中都之佐，荐膺外寄之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209433_comment'></div>彻民隐于九重，荐可而替否；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209433_comment'></div>布君仁于一路，解娆而除苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209433_comment'></div>老奸胆落而潜以自新，良士颜开而喜于托庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209433_comment'></div>苟见其善，忘贵贱之是分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209433_comment'></div>必论于朝，俾滞淹之获振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209433_comment'></div>越惟堕弱，尤溢分涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209433_comment'></div>初无鬷蔑之一言，特辱法真之独与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209433_comment'></div>邹术奋而吹律，寒谷逢春；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209433_comment'></div>伯乐过而回眸，疲驽增价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209433_comment'></div>某敢不饬前言而永践，致术业以大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209433_comment'></div>见于云为，或发胸中之蕴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209433_comment'></div>期于异日，上酬门下之恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1209433_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　在扬州任。长子柄生，字德久。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　在扬州任。是年有诏以孟子与颜子并配孔子，又追封荀况、扬雄、韩愈从祀庙庭。有文。作品：祭告先圣先师文。<div id='poem_1209682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭告先师文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209682")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209682'>昔者圣人以四科差群弟子，而公独以德行冠焉，斯可谓盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209682_comment'></div>后世豪杰之士，如孟轲、荀况、扬雄、韩愈，莫不想馀风而颂誉之，或曰具体而微，或曰智而穷于世，或曰得其所行，或曰确乎不拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209682_comment'></div>其言虽不同，要之皆为知公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209682_comment'></div>此亦潜心圣人之道，与公一趣而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209682_comment'></div>今天子以义起礼，咸秩无文，而四人者皆追封焉，俾列公侧以祠于庙，以为先儒之报，而有司将塑绘其像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209682_comment'></div>既得令日，何敢不前期以告。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1209682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　在扬州任。有文。作品：奉安先圣兖国公邹国公文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　官扬州。有上王左丞书。<div id='poem_1209421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上王左丞书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209421")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209421'>伏闻左丞由建康移镇维扬，客有知浩详、爱浩至者前揖而贺曰：「子之父前此二十年为池州贵池县主簿，今左丞王公方抑首于其州之掾曹，分朋好也，视同寮为特厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209421_comment'></div>子今乃获指令于公之节钺之下，公将善必子称，罪必子宥，庇子不浅矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209421_comment'></div>浩窃应之曰：「客虽不浩贺，浩固已自贺若不胜者，但非客之所谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209421_comment'></div>夫扬为东南一都会，頖宫萃四方之学者，旦暮讲习，纷如他州，所设师儒悉皆命自朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209421_comment'></div>朝廷非不惓惓也，刺史更加意焉，霁威俛首接之而厚其仪，养之而厚其财，以风动一方之俗，使勇发而为善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209421_comment'></div>父诫其子，兄诏其弟，妇勉其夫，长帅其幼，朋友相切偲而不怠，以承嘉惠，以称盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209421_comment'></div>贤能成器，惟恐不先，冥顽悛恶，唯恐居后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209421_comment'></div>则民之化之，或观或感，浸寻乎仁义廉耻之风，而黄堂日以无事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209421_comment'></div>《记》曰：『化民成俗，其必由学』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209421_comment'></div>此之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209421_comment'></div>扬之建学，为日固久，刺史加意于此者，远则惟魏国韩公，尝增其田畴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209421_comment'></div>近则惟秀国陈公，尝新栋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209421_comment'></div>且钜公名卿，由廊庙侍从之贵，拥节钺而镇是邦相踵也，或以此为不急之务，而莫之谁何；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209421_comment'></div>或有其意而车未停骖，坐未暖席，遽被命去，而不得为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209421_comment'></div>是以旷数十年间，无与陈、韩二公并者，况欲绍复鲁僖蜀文之盛乎，是可为太息也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209421_comment'></div>浩闻王公之贤，小之剖符守一州，而一州享其利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209421_comment'></div>大之辅佐理四海；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209421_comment'></div>而四海受其赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209421_comment'></div>谈士颂之，文士纪之，志士畏慕而法之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209421_comment'></div>今其来也，必举化民成俗之言，绍复鲁僖蜀文之盛，不俾韩、陈二公擅美誉于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209421_comment'></div>浩之自贺，实在于此，非客之所谓也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209421_comment'></div>客曰：「然仆固失之，子亦未为得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209421_comment'></div>子不闻王公之为人乎，处艰剧如简易，临苍黄如平日，才至大也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209421_comment'></div>事无纤而不该，理无幽而不烛，识至明也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209421_comment'></div>彼方戢舌而独抗其议，彼方缩手而独致其身，气至刚也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209421_comment'></div>与六合而争衡，纳万物而犹裕，量至广也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209421_comment'></div>为小官时已如此矣，譬松柏才拱把而磥砢，节操已有高耸千寻、大合百围之势，识者率以宰辅目焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209421_comment'></div>至其尹上京而登政府也，辨匿姓之书而全百千之命于危疑之际，止徙墓之请而安亿万之魂于冥漠之间，以至宽市易之逋，措曲狱之刑，下膏泽于旱暵可忧之时，排奸邪于根本难拔之地，其他盖不可以悉数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209421_comment'></div>是其才识气量能使普天之下无一夫不获者明效矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209421_comment'></div>匪朝伊夕，入秉鸿钧，弼亮圣主，比隆时雍，其又将不止于此，岂区区敛其施于一頖宫哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209421_comment'></div>况督府千里之内，官吏待之而裕其职业，农夫待之而裕其耕耨，百工待之而裕其斲削，商旅待之而裕其阜通，非特頖宫之士愿深而望切焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209421_comment'></div>子之所言，何异楚人亡弓，楚人得之，犹有楚国之限者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209421_comment'></div>浩窃复曰：「客前之所贺浩者，出于私情，故专在一身而遗頖宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209421_comment'></div>今之所以辟浩者，归于公议，故博及天下而略頖宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209421_comment'></div>浩虽鄙人，亦粗晓于斯二者，独以頖宫为言，则庶几所谓思不可出其位之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209421_comment'></div>孟子谓公孙丑曰：『子诚齐人也，知管仲晏子而已矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209421_comment'></div>浩承乏于扬之頖宫者也，知頖宫而已矣，不亦可乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209421_comment'></div>客既退，浩因记其言，今辄书以叩将命者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209421_comment'></div>恭惟知府左丞资政矜其愚而恕其罪，不独浩之幸也，一方多士之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209421_comment'></div>浩属以职贱拘文，不敢越境外，谨遣诸生持书前迎台旆，干冒钧严，浩下情无任背汗肌慄之至。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1209421'></div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1209421_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1087')">1086-1087年</a>　官扬州。有铭文。作品：都曹墓志铭（曹处厚）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八四四 《都曹墓志铭（曹处厚）》题下注“元祐元年十二月”）</span>蓬莱县君狄氏墓志铭(狄遵礼)<div id='poem_1209646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨都曹墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209646")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209646'>永康军录事参军杨君既卒之十有五年，元祐元年也，其兄无为军无为县令处愿卜以十有二月丁酉葬其母夫人孙氏于扬州江都县东兴乡马坊原先茔之右，吉，举君丧从焉，且命其子书思以荥阳郑君佸之状属某铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209646_comment'></div>某与书思友善，义不获以不敏固辞，于是论次其事而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209646_comment'></div>君讳处厚，字纯甫，其先汉州绵竹人，后徙居江都，今为江都人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209646_comment'></div>曾大父允恭，西京左藏库副使、康州刺史，赠左监门卫大将军，与其兄允升、弟允元有功太祖、太宗时，事载国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209646_comment'></div>大父告，谏议大夫，当仁宗时为名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209646_comment'></div>父闳，大理评事，景祐、庆历间赫然以文擅誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209646_comment'></div>君其仲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209646_comment'></div>宝元初，谏议以祀南郊恩奏补郊社斋郎，为婺州浦江县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209646_comment'></div>秩满，主楚州淮阴县簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209646_comment'></div>会亲嫌者，对移亳州永城，后为永康军录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209646_comment'></div>荐者应格，当改官，久不得代而疾作不起矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209646_comment'></div>时熙宁四年五月初二日也，享年三十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209646_comment'></div>君早慧，非常童比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209646_comment'></div>谏议捐馆，恩加秘书省校书郎，不受，推与其弟处廉，识者奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209646_comment'></div>盖其天性之厚，成人或不逮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209646_comment'></div>在浦江时，年少耳，若老于治者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209646_comment'></div>俗有幸民，以赀自豪，市奸吏为欺谩，以避徭役滋久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209646_comment'></div>君察见其情，令罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209646_comment'></div>摄其政，即日按其比居痛绳之，使徭役如法，一县悦服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209646_comment'></div>永城直往来之冲，客有挟贵挠公者，君一待以理，不少屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209646_comment'></div>其他与在淮阴如在浦江时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209646_comment'></div>永康地控威茂，守者皆武人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209646_comment'></div>君虽参录军事，实于兵民之政无所不预，守者赖以称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209646_comment'></div>疾革矣，火发民家，连延迫公帑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209646_comment'></div>君扶疾救完之，众每以为不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209646_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209646_comment'></div>以君天性之厚，又强明劲正，奋不顾身，皆有以过人，若假之年，砥砺停畜，允臻大成，然后发之于云为之际，则其所诣岂易量邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209646_comment'></div>不幸不寿以死，可哀也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209646_comment'></div>娶孙氏，今朝散大夫致仕琬之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209646_comment'></div>子男一人，懋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209646_comment'></div>女一人，适乡贡进士仲彦明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209646_comment'></div>孙男三人，京、卞、充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209646_comment'></div>女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209646_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1209646'>才信美兮寿则啬，郁其苗兮秀不实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209646_comment'></div>持所以兮恍谁诘，与苍珉兮閟幽室。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1209646_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209672' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209672' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209672?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蓬莱县君狄氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209672")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209672_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209672'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209672'>夫人狄氏，其先太原人，唐梁公之裔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209672_comment'></div>曾祖希颜，赠兵部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209672_comment'></div>祖棐，枢密直学士、工部侍郎，赠兵部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209672_comment'></div>父遵礼，左朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209672_comment'></div>母邹氏，寿安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209672_comment'></div>夫人幼淑慧，父母爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209672_comment'></div>既笄，遂以归吴君克礼，龙图阁直学士中复之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209672_comment'></div>龙图方显于朝，所与婚皆一时望族，而夫人自初迄终，能使舅姑与其孝，娣姒安其和，急难德其施，宗党称其贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209672_comment'></div>自元祐元年十二月八日卒，至建中靖国元年，十有六年矣，其夫不忍娶以继其室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209672_comment'></div>享年四十有三，追封蓬莱县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209672_comment'></div>子男确，举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209672_comment'></div>女适进士谭泌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209672_comment'></div>孙男一人，女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209672_comment'></div>克礼今为朝奉郎、新绛州军州事，将以二年二月六日祔葬于南康军都昌县白凤乡之先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209672_comment'></div>谓某视夫人为外姊，属铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209672_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1209672'>夫老弗偕，子养弗逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209672_comment'></div>往其从之，舅姑所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209672_comment'></div>宅兆既安，松槚既成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209672_comment'></div>恩则不忘，俨如平生。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1209672_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　官扬州。有上蒲左丞书。<div id='poem_1209422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上蒲左丞书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209422")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209422'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209422'>浩尝读《泮水》之诗，窃思古先哲王之于诸侯，裂地而封之，疏爵以贵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209422_comment'></div>井牧相错，沟涂从横，提封之数，或五百里，土至广也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209422_comment'></div>黔首横目，倚走伏趋，蜂起蚁聚，各修其业，民至众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209422_comment'></div>典则轨度，政令赏罚，详要先后，罔不即叙，法至良也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209422_comment'></div>参伍众辅，设傅陈置，尊卑乘承，交赖以济，官至备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209422_comment'></div>广土待之而后守，众民待之而后理，良法待之而后行，备官待之而后功，以致外治，以蕃王室，任至大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209422_comment'></div>戴冕被服，凭几南面，目指手挠，莫不风动而皆至，权至重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209422_comment'></div>操重权、当大任，董正备官，举良法而措之巍然广土众民之上，力回丘山，气变寒暑，顾何为而不可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209422_comment'></div>况其陵夷以及春秋之际，而狙诈相笼、虎暴相噬以自取胜者十国而六七，则其为尤无不至，亦势使然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209422_comment'></div>而鲁侯乃独勤勤恳恳，以修泮宫为务，诚知所先后者，宜其诗人颂之，以耀后世而垂不朽欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209422_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「淮夷攸服，淮夷卒获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209422_comment'></div>憬彼淮夷，来献其宝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209422_comment'></div>泮宫既修矣，每以骄逸猾夏如淮夷者犹不止攸服而遂至卒获，不止卒获而遂至来献其宝，其所临莅之国人，尚安有不革心易虑以从其所好者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209422_comment'></div>《记》曰：「化民成俗，其必由学」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209422_comment'></div>此之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209422_comment'></div>浩读《诗》至此，盖尝三复其言，收视屏息，想见鲁国之盛，恨不生斯时，偕其国人，从公于迈，以承「匪怒伊教」之赐而底于成就，如藻茆生于泮水者，可采以荐羞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209422_comment'></div>所自幸者，全形躯，具耳目，不残于聋盲跛蹇，而儒衣儒冠，获取是诗而读之，以想见其盛而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209422_comment'></div>夫简编所载，直古人之糟粕尔，所以润泽而行之者，不可传也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209422_comment'></div>取而读之，想见其盛，亦足为幸，则夫亲遇其所以然者，其幸可胜计哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209422_comment'></div>恭惟某官禀灵峻岳，作瑞昌辰，简在帝心，夙跻膴仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209422_comment'></div>代言内职，文配《两京》，总辖中台，功昭九叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209422_comment'></div>方将宅百揆、均四海，越丙、魏而掩姚、宋，以追复阿衡之美，而遽以均劳，暂去廊庙，载膺天宠，易镇大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209422_comment'></div>稽之前载，武公由卫国而后相周，黄霸由颍川而后相汉，则阁下之正台席、执鸿枢，亦由扬州入矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209422_comment'></div>今之扬州，虽与《禹贡》所言者异，然实古上公之国，而学则泮宫也，天子命之教而为之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209422_comment'></div>圣朝留意为学，自熙宁逮元丰，七闰之间，再扫其弊而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209422_comment'></div>首辟廱，旋及四国，而泮宫之制，则具辟廱之体而微者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209422_comment'></div>命官主治，在东南盖无几，而扬居一焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209422_comment'></div>浩浙右鲰生，龊龊自整，非能解颐折角，从横而无双也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209422_comment'></div>偶因试可，获处是职，正在使节之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209422_comment'></div>而茷茷之旂，蹻蹻之马，浩行遂拭目而视；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209422_comment'></div>哕哕之鸾，昭昭之音，浩行遂倾耳而听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209422_comment'></div>岂徒以慰希企大贤、瞻仰馀光之诚而已，且期与多士沐浴道德之教，以药偕生之疾，则浩前所谓其幸不胜计者此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209422_comment'></div>它日《泮水》之颂不独在鲁侯，而又在阁下矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1209422_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　官扬州。是岁，扬州秩满，韩资政维荐充讲读科，公有谢启。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
定陶
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5323c8c3ca6642428455dc52598d8095_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5323c8c3ca6642428455dc52598d8095");'><span id='5323c8c3ca6642428455dc52598d8095_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>，29岁</div><div id='5323c8c3ca6642428455dc52598d8095' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　移雄州防御推官，知安州孝感县事，待次。侍亲保之公居广济军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年8月</a>　在广济军，作文。作品：计过斋记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八四一《计过斋记》题下注“元祐三年八月”）</span><div id='poem_1209606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>计过斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209606")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209606'>善乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209606_comment'></div>韩子之言过曰，非谓发于行，彰于言，生于其心，则为过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209606_comment'></div>是以群目之所不睹，群耳之所不闻，君子慎之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209606_comment'></div>仰天而不愧，俯人而不怍，君子乐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209606_comment'></div>苟非君子，则其过恶未有不形于言行之间者，欲其不生于心，其可得乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209606_comment'></div>虽然，圣人未尝深疾而遽绝之，为之广开自新之路，以待夫能自讼自艾而改其旧者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209606_comment'></div>惟其怙终不悛，圣人无如之何，然后不得已而弃之于不齿之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209606_comment'></div>《记》曰：「或安而行之，或利而行之，或勉强而行之，及其成功，一也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209606_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209606_comment'></div>圣人之心可以推此而知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209606_comment'></div>安而行之，无过者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209606_comment'></div>利与勉强，则不能无过，而能改之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209606_comment'></div>利而改之者，牵于有所慕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209606_comment'></div>勉强而改之者，胁于有所畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209606_comment'></div>如其成功，圣人不与安而行之者等焉，则世之完人几名氏耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209606_comment'></div>冠鸡佩豭之狂生，安得为孔门之高弟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209606_comment'></div>射虎斩蛟之恶少，安得为晋室之名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209606_comment'></div>而孟子之受窃屦，郭泰之慰犯法，真为姑息尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209606_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209606_comment'></div>此非圣人之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209606_comment'></div>仆行年壮矣，自惟其愚，固不甘心于小人之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209606_comment'></div>然天资不敏，不能中固其主，而物投隙以探之，则性以情挠，理以事夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209606_comment'></div>见其居家莅官、行己接人之际，过恶岂少哉，仆犹知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209606_comment'></div>况父母之所戒，师友之所责，乡党亲旧之所指告，而仆初不知者，抑又倍焉，真名教之罪人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209606_comment'></div>私窃自喜者，幸而知之，又幸而父母戒之，师友责之，乡党亲旧指告之，又幸而圣人恕以待人，而开其自新之路，又幸而无聋盲迷罔之疾，血气未衰，馀日未索，足以感刻自奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209606_comment'></div>简册所传大君子之事业，咸在鸡鸣而起，奉以周旋，夜则内省而计焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209606_comment'></div>日以为常，有不善者庶几扑其始然，拔其始生，非特言行之间不使炽，直且驯致不生于心，以自赎于名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209606_comment'></div>后之视之，宜有曰：「晋陵邹某果不为小人之归，如其志者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209606_comment'></div>于是即听事之右屏一斋，名以「计过」而为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209606_comment'></div>继今凡仆所至，燕私之居，必复以此名之，盖无往而不计云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209606_comment'></div>时侍亲为广济军录事参军，实元祐戊辰中秋未望之三日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1209606_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　在广济军，作诗。作品：感年。<div id='poem_515854' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_515854' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/515854?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感年</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_515854")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_515854_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_515854'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_515854'>一世三十年，我今二十九。<div id='poem_sentence_0_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_515854'>昔人当此时，事业已不朽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_515854'>颜渊语心斋，瞠若夫子后。<div id='poem_sentence_2_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_515854'>著录盈三千，独居四科首。<div id='poem_sentence_3_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_515854'>荀彧王佐才，智略子房偶。<div id='poem_sentence_4_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_515854'>脱身作谋主，谈笑解纷纠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_515854'>元宾与习之，二李相左右。<div id='poem_sentence_6_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_515854'>复命索玄微，词章配韩柳。<div id='poem_sentence_7_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_515854'>夙成更超伦，初不愧黄耇。<div id='poem_sentence_8_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_515854'>项橐实可师，仲尼安敢友。<div id='poem_sentence_9_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_515854'>孔融登龙门，元礼接弥厚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_515854'>叔度千顷波，能使荀淑忸。<div id='poem_sentence_11_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_515854'>陈蕃置一室，誓涤天下垢。<div id='poem_sentence_12_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_515854'>贾谊入朝廷，号咷动明后。<div id='poem_sentence_13_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_515854'>陆机文赋成，见者咸敛手。<div id='poem_sentence_14_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_515854'>祢衡孰比俊，帝室宜见受。<div id='poem_sentence_15_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_515854'>李贺锦囊中，佳句敌琼玖。<div id='poem_sentence_16_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_515854'>相望编简上，灼灼列星斗。<div id='poem_sentence_17_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_515854'>而我独何人，拟之一无有。<div id='poem_sentence_18_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_515854'>追维故时事，浃背汗如浏。<div id='poem_sentence_19_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_515854'>穷年坐井底，曾不辨齑臼。<div id='poem_sentence_20_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_515854'>多岐既亡羊，画虎欲类狗。<div id='poem_sentence_21_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_515854'>狂澜傥不回，何以刷兹丑。<div id='poem_sentence_22_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_515854'>吁嗟岁律逝，易于屈伸肘。<div id='poem_sentence_23_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_515854'>分阴所当惜，来者勿复苟。<div id='poem_sentence_24_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_515854'>譬彼力田子，耘锄肯卤莽。<div id='poem_sentence_25_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_515854'>所期嘉苗成，不使乱于莠。<div id='poem_sentence_26_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_515854'>血气况方刚，龙钟未为叟。<div id='poem_sentence_27_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_515854'>高名非我心，没齿庶无咎。<div id='poem_sentence_28_515854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_515854'></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_515854_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
许昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='137cefc2865e4ea5a5de16f12a8d9a8a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("137cefc2865e4ea5a5de16f12a8d9a8a");'><span id='137cefc2865e4ea5a5de16f12a8d9a8a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>，30岁</div><div id='137cefc2865e4ea5a5de16f12a8d9a8a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　改除颍昌府学教授，有谢启。作品：谢苏尚书颂启。<div id='poem_1209437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>到任谢苏尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1089年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209437")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209437'>师儒之任，盍妙简于真贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209437_comment'></div>蹇浅之人，猥荐承于休命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209437_comment'></div>朅来官守，仍处部封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209437_comment'></div>惟幸会之非常，但惊惭之倍积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209437_comment'></div>伏念某江乡末系，瓮牖寒生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209437_comment'></div>附凤攀龙，虽妄祈于远到；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209437_comment'></div>画虎刻鹄，几取笑于无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209437_comment'></div>因缘误入于泮宫，邂逅久留于淮甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209437_comment'></div>抠衣户外，焉能随叩而钟鸣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209437_comment'></div>著录数中，谁是有闻而蠋化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209437_comment'></div>顾蔑可书之最，宜干警众之刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209437_comment'></div>不失一同，已出大钧之造；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209437_comment'></div>复亲六艺，岂徒旧物之还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209437_comment'></div>况公朝之清明，尤教官之选择，傥匪簪裳之名士，必须邱壑之逸民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209437_comment'></div>爰交荐于公卿，始获司于庠序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209437_comment'></div>静言忝冒，祗益感铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209437_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官卓荦大儒，主张名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209437_comment'></div>谓化民成俗，当谨于本原；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209437_comment'></div>而开门受徒，实难于模范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209437_comment'></div>苟瑕疵之可掩，皆陶冶以无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209437_comment'></div>乃若至愚，蚤蒙盛德，不假先容于绍介，遂成接武于门墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209437_comment'></div>运匠石之斤，力去已漫之垩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209437_comment'></div>发醯鸡之覆，使窥未睹之全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209437_comment'></div>重叨月旦之评，以信朝廷之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209437_comment'></div>致兹考下，亦在彀中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209437_comment'></div>右《诗》左《书》，岂特诸生之是慰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209437_comment'></div>知新温故，抑欣素志之将成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209437_comment'></div>冀无屋鼠之熏，更赖庆云之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209437_comment'></div>遥瞻龙坂，徒罄葵心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1209437_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
阜阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='60266e090df74b7894ce83122415726e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("60266e090df74b7894ce83122415726e");'><span id='60266e090df74b7894ce83122415726e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1092')">1089-1092年</a>，30-33岁</div><div id='60266e090df74b7894ce83122415726e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　在颍昌府学教授职，有谢启。作品：谢胡右丞宗愈启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　在颍昌府学教授职，馆宾友于义斋。与田承君书、崔德符鸥俱颍昌阳翟人，公与相善，有唱和诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　在颍昌府学教授职。有铭文。作品：夫人林氏墓志铭(林將女)<div id='poem_1209669' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209669' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209669?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夫人林氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209669")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209669'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209669'>元祐四年七月六日，陈君讳某之妻夫人林氏卒，于是陈君卒八年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209669_comment'></div>其葬在兴化军某县谷山之先茔，其子舜昂、舜元将以某月某日举夫人之丧祔焉，前期，用其友人江陵府松滋县令、监开封府陈留县酒税王回之言以求铭于浩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209669_comment'></div>浩顷游太学，与舜元厚，后官扬州，又尝因之以定交于回也，不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209669_comment'></div>夫人某县人，父讳将，异其性，为择对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209669_comment'></div>既笄，归陈君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209669_comment'></div>迄白首，作止皆中义理，内外上下安之，为女、为妇、为母、为姑者至指以为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209669_comment'></div>陈君少有四方志，已而所向系輆，辄拂衣还里门，以《诗》《书》训诸子，且招善士为之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209669_comment'></div>夫人于时罄奁中物买地筑室佐其事，无一毫顾惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209669_comment'></div>七男子虽不幸死矣，然其成就如舜昂、舜元皆力学，而舜元尤以节行籍籍东南，盖不可以多得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209669_comment'></div>呜呼，夫人可不谓贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209669_comment'></div>享年七十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209669_comment'></div>有九男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209669_comment'></div>二女，嫁湖州乌程县丞刘佖、进士戴励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209669_comment'></div>孙三男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209669_comment'></div>六女，一嫁进士傅求，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209669_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1209669'>辅佐以义，以成其子，以卓荦乎多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209669_comment'></div>寿考以殁，以同其穴，以安于舅姑之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209669_comment'></div>呜呼，夫人流庆其未艾！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1209669_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　在颍昌府学教授职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　在颍昌府学教授职。有铭文。作品：长寿县君高氏墓志铭(高遵望女、李竞妻)<div id='poem_1209668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长寿县君高氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209668")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209668'>夫人姓高氏，亳州蒙城人，率府副率讳遵望之女，承议郎李君竞之妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209668_comment'></div>夫人生大族，耳目富贵，于其童时辄能以礼自饬，父母贤之，故以归李君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209668_comment'></div>其移所以处首施于其家，自为妇至为母、为姑，上下内外翕然宜之无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209668_comment'></div>李氏素雄于财，至承议君则磥砢有大节，不复以积蓄为事，日与幽人豪士相徉乎风尘之外而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209668_comment'></div>其后宦游四方，养生之具往往不继，夫人竟未尝动心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209668_comment'></div>承议君白首矣，方且栖栖筦库间，或以为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209668_comment'></div>夫人独勉之曰：「仕谁不愿达，其不得达者，命也，君如命何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209668_comment'></div>我闻为善必有报，姑教诸子以俟之可乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209668_comment'></div>平时奉佛甚谨，晨起诵其书有常数，数未满辄不饮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209668_comment'></div>元祐初年，从承议君监濠州酒务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209668_comment'></div>明年六月初十日，以疾卒，享年七十，累封长寿县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209668_comment'></div>子男四人：翊、𥫃、竬、竦，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209668_comment'></div>𥫃、竬皆屡试礼部，尤以文行称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209668_comment'></div>女一人，未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209668_comment'></div>孙男、女五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209668_comment'></div>越二年，翊等奉其父命，卜以某月某日祔葬于扬州江都县东兴宁乡曾祖谏议之茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209668_comment'></div>前期，来求余铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209668_comment'></div>余顷教授扬州，竬时为学正，相好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209668_comment'></div>不获辞，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1209668'>长寿之贤，信于稚齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209668_comment'></div>未嫔高门，益安义理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209668_comment'></div>丰约后先，岂易其视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209668_comment'></div>间关良人，颖脱诸子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209668_comment'></div>敬戒成就，弗怨弗鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209668_comment'></div>善报有期，云胡不俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209668_comment'></div>昭示无穷，庶几在此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1209668_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年3月</a>　在颍昌府学教授职。吕申公公著卒，公有祭文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年12月</a>　在颍昌府学教授职。上皇帝书。作品：上哲宗皇帝书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八二九《上哲宗皇帝书》文中注“元祐四年十二月某日”）</span><div id='poem_1209371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上哲宗皇帝书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1089年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209371")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209371'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209371'>元祐四年十二月某日，颍昌府教授臣邹浩谨昧死上书皇帝陛下：臣伏睹近降贡举敕，凡考试进士试卷，其习经术者以经术为去留，其兼词赋者以词赋为去留，其馀数场，止以品定高下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209371_comment'></div>所有以四场工拙通定去留高下指挥更不施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209371_comment'></div>臣窃惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209371_comment'></div>臣闻自先王宾兴之法扫荡不存，而后世所以取天下之士，一以空言而已，德行道义，不复谁何，以迄于今，莫之能改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209371_comment'></div>就令此法不行，士之所务犹在言而不在实，况既行乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209371_comment'></div>臣见天下之士不惟有愧于其实，又将有愧于其言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209371_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209371_comment'></div>法行之利，不胜其害，其弊必至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209371_comment'></div>何谓利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209371_comment'></div>两科之试，各以四场，故习经术者不敢忽策论，兼词赋者不敢忽大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209371_comment'></div>方其群居，欲无所不工，则亦无所不知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209371_comment'></div>欲无所不知，则亦无所不读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209371_comment'></div>今也专以其科之所主者为去留，则士止务其所主者，不必杂然并习，如前日之扰扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209371_comment'></div>一利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209371_comment'></div>士之取舍，一系有司，有司之好恶，又各系其所习之如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209371_comment'></div>故尚经术者斥词赋，尚词赋者斥经术，尚策论者又并二者斥之，交相毁誉，迄无定论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209371_comment'></div>而士之取舍，直以幸不幸耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209371_comment'></div>今也严之以法，使有适从，则有司虽欲奋私意，执偏见以自胜负，势有不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209371_comment'></div>二利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209371_comment'></div>何谓害？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209371_comment'></div>惟知经然后工于义，惟知子、史然后工于策论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209371_comment'></div>至于词赋，则往往裒诸家之集，纂《六帖》之类，左攘右窃，以速名第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209371_comment'></div>而一时有司，固莫之能辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209371_comment'></div>且以今举校之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209371_comment'></div>两科取士，初无轻重，然而不以经术应诏者，已十有八九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209371_comment'></div>今也重以去留之法导之，臣知天下之士自是以六经子史为弃物矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209371_comment'></div>盖士之所急者在去留，而高下非所恤故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209371_comment'></div>一害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209371_comment'></div>士之品有三，不待教者上智也，不足教者下愚也，教之则成，不教则废者中人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209371_comment'></div>而中人之才满天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209371_comment'></div>今也使之一趋于不该不遍之习，则是天下之才将沦胥以废而莫之振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209371_comment'></div>二害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209371_comment'></div>国家自庆历以来，天下州县遍置学校，自熙宁以来，天下州县始命学官，诚有意以义理养天下之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209371_comment'></div>今也一以去留摇荡其心，虽力以义理强之，亦安能胜其所习？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209371_comment'></div>然则所置学校特为虚器，所命教官徒耗廪禄，顾欲化民成俗，如古盛时，不亦难乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209371_comment'></div>三害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209371_comment'></div>上自辅弼之大臣，下逮州县之小吏，皆佐陛下行道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209371_comment'></div>非欲其若司马相如、枚乘、沈佺期、宋之问之属，以文词供奉，谄颂功德而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209371_comment'></div>而乃养之不以其道，用之不以其实，谁恃以成天下之务哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209371_comment'></div>四害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209371_comment'></div>臣愚伏观陛下南向以来，以天地之德亭育万物，以日月之光别白万微，黜陟群臣，因革政令，斟酌人心，若合符节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209371_comment'></div>至取士之法，最务之急者，甲以为可，乙以为否，五六年间，不知几变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209371_comment'></div>今又变焉，曾未足以厌天下之望，臣窃惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209371_comment'></div>陛下诚以其法为善，胡不尽罢数场之文，只以经术词赋试之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209371_comment'></div>然而不为者，臣知建言之臣虑失天下之士，不知有其名而无其实，其失犹在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209371_comment'></div>夫举事有名而无实，非朝廷之美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209371_comment'></div>万一所举复有与是比者，无乃重为圣政之累乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209371_comment'></div>《传》曰：「设教于本，其敝且末；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209371_comment'></div>设教于末，其敝奈何」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1209371_comment'></div>又曰：「为人君者，谨其所好恶而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1209371_comment'></div>君好之则臣为之，上行之则民从之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1209371_comment'></div>偏为去留，不可谓本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1209371_comment'></div>已著于令，不可谓非所好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1209371_comment'></div>陛下少须之，臣之二利四害之说行自判矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1209371_comment'></div>且臣四害之中，如人才不振，无以成天下之务，尤有所当虑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1209371_comment'></div>陛下视今日之人才果有馀邪，果不足邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1209371_comment'></div>以为不足，则岩廊未尝无辅弼，左右未尝无侍从，诸路未尝无监司，州县未尝无守令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1209371_comment'></div>凡中外之百执事，亦未尝不备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1209371_comment'></div>其待选、待次，去来吏部者又常倍蓰见任之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1209371_comment'></div>以为有馀，则自任以天下之重，辅导陛下与二帝三王比隆争治者几人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1209371_comment'></div>进退贤否惟其实，而不汲引亲旧、不遗弃疏逖以误陛下器使者几人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1209371_comment'></div>正色昌言，列百官之功罪，论庶事之得失，务存大体而不承望风旨以自媒者几人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1209371_comment'></div>持刺举之权以肃清所部，而不结权贵以殖私，不惜孤寒以示公者几人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1209371_comment'></div>承宣诏条，劝课农桑，使民安其所，不饮泣于猾胥黠吏之手者几人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1209371_comment'></div>夙夜修职，不敢苟且，以冀指摘之不吾及者几人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1209371_comment'></div>民贫，所当富也，则曰水旱如之何；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1209371_comment'></div>官冗，所当澄也，则曰人情不可扰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1209371_comment'></div>人物，所当求也，则曰从古不乏才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1209371_comment'></div>国用，所当裕也，则曰治世耻言利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1209371_comment'></div>风俗，所当厚也，则曰不切于时变；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1209371_comment'></div>边备，所当严也，则曰在德不在兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1209371_comment'></div>其他覼缕，臣不暇悉，要之为国谋不如谋其身，为百姓虑不如虑其子孙者众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1209371_comment'></div>陛下端拱一堂之上，方以覆载为度，固不规规焉察臣下之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1209371_comment'></div>然视朝之馀，省奏报、听讲读之暇，亦尝念其所以然之故乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1209371_comment'></div>此乃不明义理之验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1209371_comment'></div>夫以义理养天下之士，士方平时师圣贤、谈道德，其取舍去就之际，若无以易其操者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1209371_comment'></div>一旦用焉，犹或幡然无以副朝廷承庸之意，况不知所以养之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1209371_comment'></div>董仲舒曰：「不素养士而求贤才，犹不瑑玉而求文彩」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1209371_comment'></div>臣尝以为知言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1209371_comment'></div>臣愿陛下诏有司追用旧敕，以四场工拙通定去留高下，庶几经术策论之试不为虚文，而士亦知陛下所以期之甚厚，相与精白以承休德，而人才有馀矣，岂甚难者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1209371_comment'></div>昔孔子不欲去饩羊者，非为饩羊也，为告朔之礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1209371_comment'></div>孟子不欲毁明堂者，非为明堂也，为王者之政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1209371_comment'></div>饩羊不去，则告朔之礼犹可以意推；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1209371_comment'></div>明堂不毁，则王者之政犹可以迹考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1209371_comment'></div>臣之区区，实在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1209371_comment'></div>臣寒乡鄙人也，生长和气之中，沐浴仁厚之泽，备员学校，为日久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1209371_comment'></div>重念古者工执艺事以谏之义，故敢因执事所及，轻犯天威，冒献瞽说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1209371_comment'></div>惟陛下采其一得，而赦其万死，则天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1209371_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1209371_comment'></div>臣浩诚惶诚恐，顿首稽首，昧死谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_89_1209371_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年6月</a>　在颍昌府学教授职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　在颍昌府学教授职。有记。作品：义斋记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八四一 《义斋记》题下注“元祐四年六月”）</span><div id='poem_1209593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>义斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐四年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209593")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209593'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209593'>元祐四年春夏旱，至五月甲申大雨，穷晨夕不止，凡三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209593_comment'></div>距府北多广陂，实受西北群山之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209593_comment'></div>水既骤集，不得泄，于是南注府城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209593_comment'></div>逻卒驰告，方欲土长葛门，而水败门入矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209593_comment'></div>惟是南北斗起若长堤，约水而西，又薄子城，势益怒不可遏，遂决鄢陵门以出，故庐室之在东北隅者率以漂毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209593_comment'></div>其水所不到，则雨为之害焉，民之压溺死者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209593_comment'></div>闻老人谓建邦以来未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209593_comment'></div>时资政殿学士曾公知府事，具以闻，且请发仓廪以拯细民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209593_comment'></div>给度牒以完官舍，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209593_comment'></div>仆初教授頖宫，于是得钱一十五万，完所居之舍，因改治其厅东小室，以馆宾友，命之曰「义斋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209593_comment'></div>后二年，客或致诘曰：「子欺予哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209593_comment'></div>予观古义士大则轻一死于鸿毛，小则等千金于粪土，径脱人于艰危中，功成唾去，阒无留辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209593_comment'></div>其气节凛凛，与秋霜争严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209593_comment'></div>子果出于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209593_comment'></div>眇然儒生，君亲是徇，固难一死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209593_comment'></div>庖无盛烟，面有饥色，安得千金，徒以数椽馆宾友耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209593_comment'></div>遂以为义，子欺予哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209593_comment'></div>仆曰：「是非仆心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209593_comment'></div>仆家有书千卷，有琴一张，日以二物罗列左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209593_comment'></div>乡闾亲旧或不陋其为人，自远而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209593_comment'></div>其居是斋也，取六经读之，则圣贤之旨明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209593_comment'></div>取诸史读之，则治乱之迹明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209593_comment'></div>取百家众氏之书读之，则邪正是非之趣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209593_comment'></div>间而倦焉，横琴奏雅，以导其湮郁不平之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209593_comment'></div>以此卒岁而成其材，异时简拔以见于世，自其效一官至于均四海，随其巨细，蔚有事业，不愧所学与天下后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209593_comment'></div>苟不得志，则卷而怀之，立言著书，以越尘表，亦无秋毫怨尤意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209593_comment'></div>此其为义，孰与客谈者多」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209593_comment'></div>客矫舌久之，已而叹曰：「冥冥兮往昔，壤壤兮来今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209593_comment'></div>信耳目以自私兮，实不知予心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209593_comment'></div>客退，次第其语，且追载水害之本末，为之记云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209593_comment'></div>六月十二，晋陵邹某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1209593_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　在颍昌府学教授职。有序。作品：赵教授送行序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　在颍昌府学教授职。作品：孙寿朋墓志铭（孙安）<div id='poem_1209647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙寿朋墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐七年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209647")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209647'>元祐七年春大雪，长社令孙君寿朋久疾方愈，冒之以视防列，又走鄢陵境上集其吏民议积水之利害，回环累日，且不时食饮，于是疾作以归，至四月二十六日不起矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209647_comment'></div>自官府、闾井，虽不快君者亦莫不赍咨出涕，其田间老稚相与泣叹曰：「天夺我贤令」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209647_comment'></div>其家卜以六月八日葬君于汝州襄城县孟陵之先茔，既吉，谓僚友中与君厚莫如某，属铭诸墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209647_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209647_comment'></div>异时从容，君必语其平生无隐情，始以为偶然，今而思之，岂偶然邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209647_comment'></div>君讳安，寿朋其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209647_comment'></div>其先赵州平棘人，徙贯颍昌之长社，至君盖三世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209647_comment'></div>曾大父澄，赠工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209647_comment'></div>大父澄，给事中、集贤院学士，赠工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209647_comment'></div>父昂，左骐骥使、带御器械，赠左金吾卫上将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209647_comment'></div>御带捐馆舍，恩适及其一子，朝廷录其功，特许君与兄广分受之颍，差使于三班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209647_comment'></div>已而试经术异等，换太庙斋郎，且调蔡州西平尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209647_comment'></div>邑故多盗，未几犬不夜警，部使者以其捕获闻，迁令录，视其品为恩州清河县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209647_comment'></div>废罢，改长社尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209647_comment'></div>考满，用荐者转宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209647_comment'></div>时从父兄康简公以吏部尚书薨于位，还长社，上悼之，遂命君就知县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209647_comment'></div>颍昌，京西一都会，其封内皆剧邑，惟长社刺史在焉，又占籍多巨室，故前数十年未有以美政闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209647_comment'></div>君之来也，耆老相贺曰：「此前日贤尉也，使我露粟而积，开户而眠旧矣，我其受赐益大矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209647_comment'></div>君既揽印，则以民为身，以国事为家事，曾不以贵贱疏戚贰其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209647_comment'></div>岁尝大饥，众以赴诉，履亩者承风旨抑之，于其常税仅蠲一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209647_comment'></div>君愤然直于府，安抚使、资政殿学士曾公孝宽主其议，于是奏行之，且广及四邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209647_comment'></div>又有意在圭田而故疑诉之妄者，君乃先自蠲其所当得以折其谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209647_comment'></div>方复差役之初，法未画一，辄参俚俗以润泽之，或讥其非是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209647_comment'></div>比法成，悉与君合，郡县方且纷然更张，而长社固已按堵久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209647_comment'></div>君奉诏令，不束于文，而惟其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209647_comment'></div>釐正版图，逆绝奸倖，民造庭下，每每训谕，其怙终不悛，乃寘于刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209647_comment'></div>苟不必逮證，不食顷留也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209647_comment'></div>一方以君为蓍龟权衡，输送自集，狱以清简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209647_comment'></div>初，乡户置长以督其赋，一切取办，往往破产代偿，故例以上户为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209647_comment'></div>至是遂不复为重役，与他邑异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209647_comment'></div>异时夏秋，吏歛民以规利，谓之乞局，稍不从辄患生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209647_comment'></div>及君治效，弗获逞，其俗遂革，郊野间莫识吏面，吏亦迄用不触上位嗔，始虽侧目，终更德之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209647_comment'></div>民既挽君再留，逾年，又豫忧其去，走阙下就请通判府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209647_comment'></div>君谦慎，初不以此自多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209647_comment'></div>然名声四驰，千百里皆知长社有人，其讼至有叩监司以来君决者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209647_comment'></div>龙图阁待制陆公佃自邓入觐，躬欲访其治术，而君死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209647_comment'></div>士大夫道其境，见其民之聚泣，为之嗟异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209647_comment'></div>君羁贯即有志自建立，执经从师，寒暑风雨不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209647_comment'></div>康简公指以语人曰：「吾家令器也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209647_comment'></div>其与人交，乐告以善，惟恐其疵瑕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209647_comment'></div>其爱民出天性，疾革，与朋友谈莫非民事，一不为身虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209647_comment'></div>既死，箧无裳衣歛葬之具，赖赙禭以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209647_comment'></div>享年三十七，官止右通直郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209647_comment'></div>前娶魏氏，至是祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209647_comment'></div>后娶刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209647_comment'></div>男三人：宪、悫、愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209647_comment'></div>女五人，长适进士李纾，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209647_comment'></div>母陈氏老矣，无以为养，诸孤眇藐，无以为长计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209647_comment'></div>其异母兄弟与其族人恻然任其责曰：「我辈在，忍使失所」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1209647_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1209647'>环地百里，孰不分民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1209647_comment'></div>视民如己，有贤孙君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1209647_comment'></div>君久于位，我作我止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1209647_comment'></div>曰非我私，仁圣之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1209647_comment'></div>惟此下民，实天耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1209647_comment'></div>民父母之，天胡不福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1209647_comment'></div>不福以逝，民以怨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1209647_comment'></div>蔚其后昆，尚克高门。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1209647_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d90c9c3a0bc743b8a8cfe5b4eceb8aa3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d90c9c3a0bc743b8a8cfe5b4eceb8aa3");'><span id='d90c9c3a0bc743b8a8cfe5b4eceb8aa3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1094')">1093-1094年</a>，34-35岁</div><div id='d90c9c3a0bc743b8a8cfe5b4eceb8aa3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年</a>　冬，到襄州任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　在襄州任，有铭文。作品：夫人严氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1209670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夫人严氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐九年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209670")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209670'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209670'>毗陵张氏居张庄者为东南著姓，由稷虞卿而上，累世皆义居，至虞卿益蕃雄一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209670_comment'></div>其伯父老矣，委家事以自佚，而门内之治，惟虞卿之妇总焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209670_comment'></div>虞卿娶霍氏，生一男四女而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209670_comment'></div>夫人严氏实继以行，事其伯舅如其舅，抚其前子如其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209670_comment'></div>虞卿落落乡闾，与宾亲适其平生而不他虑，夫人力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209670_comment'></div>未几虞卿卒，夫人益务饬其子，故其男炳从师友为进士，其女归进士邹洞、胡明修、王辅世、胡谧、庄安常，皆不贻亲忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209670_comment'></div>里有贫女无归，夫人幼育而长嫁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209670_comment'></div>其自奉则一切薄约，游宴不辄出，见至亲有时，语人曰：「孀妇当如处女」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209670_comment'></div>中外族党睦然归心，侍婢白首不忍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209670_comment'></div>显官有贤其节者力求继其室，竟不夺初志，其母亦不忍夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209670_comment'></div>初得疾，即治歛具，比革，命家人取视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209670_comment'></div>顾其母年且八十在傍，泣曰：「儿不获终养矣，奈何」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209670_comment'></div>语绝逝去，实元祐八年五月十九日，享年四十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209670_comment'></div>父士元，母强氏，盖同郡儒家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209670_comment'></div>生二女，一女未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209670_comment'></div>炳卜以明年某月某日葬于某县某乡某原，谓余姻好，属铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209670_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1209670'>得夫而早殁，有子而非己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209670_comment'></div>诸孤恃焉，以迄于家室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209670_comment'></div>皎皎弗渝，秉其一德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209670_comment'></div>为女妇母，是迪是式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209670_comment'></div>有岿其丘，有蔚其殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209670_comment'></div>何千万年，夫人安宅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1209670_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　在襄州任，春，上书。作品：上胡提刑求迁学书。<div id='poem_1209427' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209427' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209427?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上胡宪求迁学书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209427")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209427_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209427'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209427'>某到学之日，升堂见诸生，顾两庑皆隘陋，已而相与周视庖湢之类，则又不得与两庑比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209427_comment'></div>因诘之曰：「襄阳名邦，士大夫以道德功名垂方册者历历如列星丽晴天，至今为天下想慕，学乃如是耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209427_comment'></div>朝廷选守，又多台阁之旧，有猷有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209427_comment'></div>既以信于天下，曾不知化民成俗必由于学，而乃忽之不问邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209427_comment'></div>诸生合而对曰：「此多士意也，怀之久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209427_comment'></div>郡守之来，有席未及温，慨然自欲新之者，有因见白而后欲新之者，然终莫之能新也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209427_comment'></div>盖因旧而举，则不惟地窄难广，不足以充规模，抑亦狱据其左，非所以崇风教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209427_comment'></div>必迁而可，则莫如州之东南隅，以阴阳家言之巽方也，最利建学，然而提刑司在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209427_comment'></div>幸而委废弗居且十年，但以前日诸公不纳其说，此所以欲新之而未能也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209427_comment'></div>某闻其语，退而窃访于识者，以求诸公不纳之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209427_comment'></div>或曰朝廷将还漕司于邓，则提刑当复居于此，不可为学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209427_comment'></div>或曰提刑行部至此，必舍以听事，不可以为学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209427_comment'></div>或曰后圃多橘，岁租于民，以给胥吏之费，不可以为学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209427_comment'></div>是三说者，浩尝思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209427_comment'></div>二司所在，朝廷既以为宜，安有辄然复徙之理？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209427_comment'></div>前日纷纷，直主者自疑尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209427_comment'></div>阁下所饫闻而所亲见也，其说不可用明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209427_comment'></div>行部至此，固有行衙，漕使居之不以为陋，则宪使似亦可居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209427_comment'></div>况按察虽久，不过浃日，何必旧司始为安便？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209427_comment'></div>其说不可用亦明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209427_comment'></div>橘利既以给胥吏之费，无名罢去诚不可，学钱粗有馀，视民岁出之数就出之，则其利如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209427_comment'></div>其说不可用亦明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209427_comment'></div>阁下久在朝廷，一旦出持使节，舆议郁郁不快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209427_comment'></div>上听政以来，每发德音，尤在人物，且多采舆议，往往公卿未之知者，一路八州，岂能更挽阁下于朝夕间哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209427_comment'></div>是以迁学之说，浩不敢徐以闻左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209427_comment'></div>浩虽愚，亦阁下之乡人也，参侍几席，早辱知遇，阁下必不以今日之事疑浩为犯分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209427_comment'></div>文恭公所至州，首兴学校、厚诸生而师诲之，因以取高第、登膴仕者甚众，搢绅先生以为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209427_comment'></div>阁下克肖先德，既已取信于上，而浩之亲炙，又不为无日，亦不敢以今日之事疑阁下为难，请阁下试留听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209427_comment'></div>审以浩言不妄，时为施行，一方士大夫且将以阁下盛德载之文字，刻之金石，耀之子孙，与学偕无穷，不亦美乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209427_comment'></div>《传》曰，「时者难得而易失」，阁下为提刑，吕公为郡守，而浩适以罪承乏为部吏，以获进是说，真其时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209427_comment'></div>惟阁下赐之，毋使识者重起易失之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209427_comment'></div>幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209427_comment'></div>幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1209427_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年4月</a>　在襄州任。以迁学作文。作品：告先圣文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（山阳乃今淮安，陈瓘或任职于此，但不见记载。）</span><div id='poem_1209681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭告先圣文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209681")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209681'>惟王之道神明博大，固不可以容声，而当时之士亲见所为，犹或咻咻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209681_comment'></div>况及后世，异端蜂起，汩没本真，以自为是，则其能不以彼易此而潜心王之道者谁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209681_comment'></div>力辟杨、墨，乃有孟轲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209681_comment'></div>自成一家，乃有荀况；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209681_comment'></div>折衷义理，乃有扬雄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209681_comment'></div>堤障末流，乃有韩愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209681_comment'></div>先后相望，虽参差不齐，而俾王之道皓皓乎百世之下，则随其浅深，咸有力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209681_comment'></div>今天子前言往行罔不灼知，于是追封此四人者，惟爵惟邑，有异有同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209681_comment'></div>公则配食，伯则崇祀，以示褒崇，以为学者之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209681_comment'></div>而维扬乡校将以塑绘其像于王之左右，而有司卜吉，龟筮协从，命工饬材，继今以始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209681_comment'></div>樽篚薄荐，敢告其由。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1209681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年7月</a>　在襄州任。新学成，作记。作品：奉安文宣王兖国公邹国公文。襄州迁学记。<div id='poem_1209595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>襄州迁学记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣元年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209595")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209595'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209595'>学旧在城外，庆历四年诏天下皆立学，明年春遂移建于城中，至是盖五十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209595_comment'></div>襄阳自古为镇，重山拥其西南，长江缭其东北，物象萧爽，冠绝荆楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209595_comment'></div>钟其气以生者，世有特立不群之士，后生取法，如仰星斗，宜其教化之宫，有以对仁圣长育之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209595_comment'></div>而乃湫溢卑湿，不与州称，因循不问，识者叹焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209595_comment'></div>今直秘阁、知荆南府吕公嘉问守襄之明年，绍圣元年也，思所以改作者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209595_comment'></div>会提刑迁治于邓，委旧宇久弗居，议请以为学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209595_comment'></div>时左朝奉大夫胡公宗炎方提点刑狱事，欣然曰：「此吾志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209595_comment'></div>遂相继以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209595_comment'></div>诏从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209595_comment'></div>于是委兵马监押、东头供奉官徐平董其役，又委知襄阳县、右通直郎田衍总其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209595_comment'></div>因以基址，革以制度，自四月之乙丑至七月之乙未，凡一百十有四日，而百九十有八楹烨然一新矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209595_comment'></div>繇重门而入，殿据其前，讲堂次其后，议道堂又次其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209595_comment'></div>直堂为阁，以藏书籍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209595_comment'></div>分庑为斋，以舍多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209595_comment'></div>祭器钱谷，悉皆有库；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209595_comment'></div>庖厨浴室，莫不得宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209595_comment'></div>又即其西所谓凤山堂者广之，以为教官之居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209595_comment'></div>即其东所谓射圃者规之，以为燕息之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209595_comment'></div>其恢宏伟丽，虽东南之学最盛者不能过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209595_comment'></div>窃惟国家稽古右文，累圣相授，至神宗皇帝时备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209595_comment'></div>故施于学者，本以经术，辅以三舍，率用党庠遂序书考贤能之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209595_comment'></div>今天子灼见本原，遹追前列，洋洋乎道德之泽，与乾坤并流未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209595_comment'></div>二公早被识擢，久践台省，深知上心之所存，故能相与奉承，曾不劳费，而学已成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209595_comment'></div>昔文翁以郡守变全蜀之风，常衮以部使者成七闽之俗，凛然功名，皆自学始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209595_comment'></div>安知后之视今，不犹今之视昔乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209595_comment'></div>虽士之自处，不以陋巷改其乐，当如颜渊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209595_comment'></div>不以环堵谓之病，当如原宪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209595_comment'></div>然公不以其自处者处焉，既使安其居如此，则士乌乎待哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209595_comment'></div>自其不可得而贵贱者以持养之，以尽夫修身之道，以达乎闺门乡党之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209595_comment'></div>繇此辅世，必有如隆中之勋业者出焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209595_comment'></div>繇此就閒，必有如鹿门之节义者出焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209595_comment'></div>盖可以指日俟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209595_comment'></div>然则士之所以报公与公之所以报国于是乎无愧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1209595_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年8月</a>　在襄州任。有铭文。作品：夫人程氏墓志铭(程端女、林师醇妻)<div id='poem_1209671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夫人程氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209671")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209671'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209671'>夫人程氏，世为常州晋陵人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209671_comment'></div>曾祖士邻，某官，赠某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209671_comment'></div>祖昌言，某官，赠某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209671_comment'></div>父端，某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209671_comment'></div>晋陵于浙右为士大夫最盛处，程氏于其间又为名族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209671_comment'></div>夫人生长家法中，早为父母所贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209671_comment'></div>年当行，会今婺州观察推官林君师醇醇中方中进士第，遂以归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209671_comment'></div>醇中幼失所怙，太夫人甘贫守节，训育诸孤，以至白首，盖已勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209671_comment'></div>自夫人归，凡委以肃助闺门与其施于上下内外，一如太夫人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209671_comment'></div>醇中不以位卑自少，所至奉条约修职甚谨，未尝开口乞怜上官，以故间关州县，人或不堪其忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209671_comment'></div>而夫人独以义命勉焉，且左右奉承，惟恐其动家室念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209671_comment'></div>闻者叹曰：「真林氏妇也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209671_comment'></div>间喜读书，一览辄成诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209671_comment'></div>尤笃信内典，涣若有得者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209671_comment'></div>醇中为寿州霍丘县尉，时夫人得疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209671_comment'></div>一日，与醇中语，皆超诣名理，神色不少变，已而逝去，实元祐七年九月十八日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209671_comment'></div>归林氏凡十年，年三十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209671_comment'></div>生一男一女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209671_comment'></div>后二年，绍圣元年，醇中卜以八月某日葬于苏州吴县某乡某山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209671_comment'></div>前期，状其行属予铭，且曰：「程氏生平雅好文字，且知君与我友善，庶几慰诸泉下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209671_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1209671'>移孝于姑，移顺于夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209671_comment'></div>克隆厥家，而弗与俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209671_comment'></div>彼茁者子，身后之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209671_comment'></div>虽则远矣，禀其如初。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1209671_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　在襄州任。次子栩生。有文。作品：洗幼子文。<div id='poem_1209625' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209625' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209625?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洗幼子文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209625")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209625_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209625'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209625'>分日月之末照以本汝之气，据潇湘之上游以洁汝之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209625_comment'></div>汝聪汝明，汝所固有；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209625_comment'></div>汝忠汝孝，汝勿妄行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209625_comment'></div>视汝父之不得安其位，则知所以修职业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209625_comment'></div>视汝父之不得养其志，则知所以奉晨昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209625_comment'></div>庄子曰：「为善无近名，为恶无近刑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209625_comment'></div>「缘督以为经，可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1209625", 1209625, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>保身</span>，可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1209625", 1209625, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>全生</span>，可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1209625", 1209625, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>养亲</span>，可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1209625", 1209625, "Clauses/17/Comments/1")'>尽年</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209625_comment'></div>吾既以此训汝之兄矣，汝其从兄而恭命，勿使失坠，以对吾生育之恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1209625_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e8d2c26adcef411cbdae3f43f31b1eb8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e8d2c26adcef411cbdae3f43f31b1eb8");'><span id='e8d2c26adcef411cbdae3f43f31b1eb8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>，36岁</div><div id='e8d2c26adcef411cbdae3f43f31b1eb8' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在襄州任。著《论语解义》十卷、《孟子解义》十四卷。作品：论语解义。孟子解义。<div id='poem_1209495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论语解义序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209495")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209495'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209495'>圣人，体道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209495_comment'></div>其发越以抚世，则所以益无疆者皆见之行事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209495_comment'></div>其韬晦以就间，则所以规不朽者惟载之空言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209495_comment'></div>载之空言固不如见之行事为深切著明也，然而讳穷久矣而不免，求通久矣而不得，道固无积，而时命碍之，则虽欲无言，而言终不废，岂其得已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209495_comment'></div>《论语》之作，有由然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209495_comment'></div>所谓析理而使昧者之必达谓之论，所以应问而使叩者之必受谓之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209495_comment'></div>是书也，后世豪杰之士随绳望表以自立言者犹能探赜索隐，中伦合度，凡学者虚心焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209495_comment'></div>况本出于圣人者，此传所以莫大于《论语》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209495_comment'></div>且以六经之言，孰不出于圣人乎，然而其于《易》也，因伏羲之卦、文王之爻而系之以辞而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209495_comment'></div>其于《诗》、《书》也，因众多之辞、帝王之迹而删之以趋全而已。<div class='inline'
