id='poem_sentence_9_1209495_comment'></div>其于《春秋》也，因纪实之信史而修之以示褒贬而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209495_comment'></div>其于《礼》、《乐》也，因固有之情文而正之以教中和而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209495_comment'></div>要之虽皆出于圣人，而非纯乎圣人之言者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209495_comment'></div>纯乎圣人之言，意其为《论语》乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209495_comment'></div>夫以《论语》为纯乎圣人之言，而二三子之言亦错杂其间，如之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209495_comment'></div>曰：治金为钟，捖革为鼓，声固藏其中矣，不考则不鸣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209495_comment'></div>圣人曷尝先声以邀彼之我应哉，亦随所考而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209495_comment'></div>然则不有二三子之言，何以见纯乎圣人之言也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209495_comment'></div>是故达其所谓「五十而学《易》，可以无大过」之类，则《易》之道得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209495_comment'></div>达其所谓《诗》可以兴、观、群、怨之类，则《诗》之道得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209495_comment'></div>以至《书》也，《春秋》也，《礼》《乐》也，苟悟其一言，未有不冰解冻释以诣于道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209495_comment'></div>从是观之，其书虽简，其所该则详；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209495_comment'></div>其言虽近，其所根则远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209495_comment'></div>非自覃思而精之，岂能抽其绪以莹晦焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209495_comment'></div>顾浩蹇浅，何足以与此，姑荐所闻，与有志于道者讲之而已矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1209495_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孟子解义序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209496")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209496'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209496'>孔子没，世衰道丧，百有馀岁，以及孟子之时，其害尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209496_comment'></div>以汤武为弑君，以周公为未智，以匡章为不孝，以仲子为廉士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209496_comment'></div>非特此也，不动心如告子，犹外义而莫悟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209496_comment'></div>事豪杰如陈相，犹倍师而自若；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209496_comment'></div>则道之不明可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209496_comment'></div>以利国为先务，以殃民为可为，以战必克为良臣，以逢君恶为无罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209496_comment'></div>非特此也，可与有为如齐宣王者，其所问惟桓文之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209496_comment'></div>可与有言如公孙丑者，其所冀惟管晏之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209496_comment'></div>则道之不行可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209496_comment'></div>孟子于此时，上下无知而信之者，操不售之具，以周游其间，不少贬焉，非以道自任而能若是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209496_comment'></div>其道则自古以固存而孔子之所传者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209496_comment'></div>孔子之于道，不得已而载之，后世君子孰不可以得之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209496_comment'></div>然而有目同视而所见者近，有耳同听而所闻者浅，有心同思而所得者他而不正，则争以自取胜，而大道斯为天下裂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209496_comment'></div>然则孔子之后，能绍其传者，孟子一人而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209496_comment'></div>与太和为一而充塞于两间，上足以配道，下足以配义，其所养之气有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209496_comment'></div>由父子之仁而极于天道，由可欲之善而极于神，其所造之妙有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209496_comment'></div>于《诗》则以意逆，于《书》则取二三策，其通经有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209496_comment'></div>敷陈于齐宣、梁惠之前，训告于万章、乐克之徒，曲而中，多而类，其出言有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209496_comment'></div>见与不见皆不以人枉己，受与不受皆不以利废义，其制行有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209496_comment'></div>以其所养之气，发其所造之妙，无施而不可，则其为通经也，出言也，制行也，皆馀事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209496_comment'></div>奈何天未欲平治天下，而「舍我其谁」之志终不获伸，是以其功止于距杨、墨以承三圣而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209496_comment'></div>虽然，使杨、墨之道息，孔子之道著，天下后世咸知父子有仁，君臣有义，不沦胥而为禽兽，则其志虽不伸于当时，固已伸于后世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209496_comment'></div>以道论功，如之何其可及也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209496_comment'></div>其后名世之士，有出于汉而能知之者，莫如扬子，故论其道则曰「不异」，论其功则曰「扩如」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209496_comment'></div>有出于唐而能知之者，莫如韩子，故论其道则曰「醇乎醇」，论其功则曰「不在禹下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209496_comment'></div>非苟知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209496_comment'></div>窃自比焉，则庶几孟子之道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209496_comment'></div>攘斥佛老，则庶几孟子之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209496_comment'></div>夫二子之不如孟子易见也，有所庶几且无与并，况孟子乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209496_comment'></div>故韩子曰：「学者必谨于其所道，求观圣人之道，必自《孟子》始」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209496_comment'></div>浩尝闻之于师曰：「诵《孟子》之书非难，深明其意之所在为难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209496_comment'></div>深明其意之所在非难，能以其所以自任者矜式而行之为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209496_comment'></div>昔孔子之门人，如仲弓之有闻于仁，则请事斯语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209496_comment'></div>如子张之有闻于行，则必书诸绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209496_comment'></div>今《孟子》七篇之所载，非直孔子答问之际一二言耳，学者或尚愧于仲弓、子张之贤，则以其所以自任者矜式而行之，其可忽乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209496_comment'></div>浩不敏，敬受此言久矣，愿与诸君子共之，勿徒诵其书、明其意，资以为速化之术而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209496_comment'></div>颜渊曰：「舜何人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209496_comment'></div>予何人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209496_comment'></div>有为者亦若是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209496_comment'></div>呜呼，岂独颜渊之于舜为然哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1209496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在襄州任。有文。作品：答何道乡《论孟子解书》<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4116b53424b34ad9b936a96cb63cfab5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4116b53424b34ad9b936a96cb63cfab5");'><span id='4116b53424b34ad9b936a96cb63cfab5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，35岁</div><div id='4116b53424b34ad9b936a96cb63cfab5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　在襄州任。有记。作品：永州法华寺经藏记。<div id='poem_1209608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永州法华寺经藏记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209608")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209608'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209608'>零陵郡城中旧无禅刹，元丰四年，郡守李杰始以太平请于朝，赐额为元丰太平禅寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209608_comment'></div>元祐六年，权守杨宗惠又以法华请焉，诏因旧额以为禅寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209608_comment'></div>明觉大师义霞实为法华初祖，霞既受疏，升座为潭州龙兴智传禅师焚香，举扬一大事因缘，于是彻旧宇而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209608_comment'></div>南为三门，北为法堂，又北为暖堂，又北为方丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209608_comment'></div>东为五百罗汉堂，为香积厨，为库院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209608_comment'></div>西为大圣菩萨殿，为云会堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209608_comment'></div>而释迦佛殿据中，为尊禅居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209608_comment'></div>规模亦云备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209608_comment'></div>顾念《般若经》六百卷，《宝积经》一百二十卷，《华严经》八十卷，《般涅槃经》四十卷，于大藏中卷数特多，号四大部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209608_comment'></div>寺所有者，乃后唐清泰中宁远军节度使马存之所施也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209608_comment'></div>分散多处，惧不克久，遂即西廊为殿三间，中为机轮，函经于其上，为佛菩萨以周其四面，为神龙以绕其四柱，若形若色，妙绝众巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209608_comment'></div>岁时邦人来会，稽首作礼，藏为旋转，或三或五，至于七，人人欢踊，各满志愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209608_comment'></div>夫世习移人旧矣，鸡鸣而起，随所好而趋焉，扰扰纷纷，奚暇有所决择？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209608_comment'></div>一旦睹相虔恭，诸缘骤息，虽未足以语教外别传，然卷开而善心亦开，藏转而妄情亦转，则经之不可思议，一念皆圆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209608_comment'></div>纵未能造次颠沛常必于是，其为利益亦何可胜言哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209608_comment'></div>争讼由此衰，和协由此兴，风俗由此厚，岂不能助守长承流宣化，如父如母之意乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209608_comment'></div>岂不能助主上博恩广施，如天如地之意乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209608_comment'></div>初，霞之图为此藏也，囊无系蚁之丝，厨绝聚蝇之糁，形孤影独，朝不谋夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209608_comment'></div>而命工选材，反急于衣食计，人以为狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209608_comment'></div>已而得郡人高齐倡导暨蒋嵩等欣助，为钱逾一百五十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209608_comment'></div>自绍圣元年三月肇基，至八月毕功，为日才三甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209608_comment'></div>孟子曰：「至诚而不动者，未之有也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209608_comment'></div>霞之谓与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209608_comment'></div>惟记之久未立也，属某贬谪至此，且于循省之隙取经阅焉，以启迪昏蒙，以洗湔衅咎，以仰称仁圣矜容，使之自新之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209608_comment'></div>霞以故恳请记其本末，遂为之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1209608_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4ad6bd44bb4a49c8a14c67ef6688f992_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4ad6bd44bb4a49c8a14c67ef6688f992");'><span id='4ad6bd44bb4a49c8a14c67ef6688f992_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1103')">1102-1103年</a>，43-44岁</div><div id='4ad6bd44bb4a49c8a14c67ef6688f992' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年10月3日</a>　到永州。有诗。作品：除名别零陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年1月</a>　除名勒停，昭州居住。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7b4c271dd77f4c43a2d677df767ac47b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7b4c271dd77f4c43a2d677df767ac47b");'><span id='7b4c271dd77f4c43a2d677df767ac47b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>，46岁</div><div id='7b4c271dd77f4c43a2d677df767ac47b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年12月19日</a>　游永州澹崖，有诗。作品：训狐六一崖。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='41426d96b89244a38a6566d679aa341e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("41426d96b89244a38a6566d679aa341e");'><span id='41426d96b89244a38a6566d679aa341e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>，40岁</div><div id='41426d96b89244a38a6566d679aa341e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年10月</a>　公谪新，道潭州，州守温益下逐客之令，旅店不敢舍。夜绝湘江，会天大风雨，扁舟掀舞几覆。既抵岸，有岳麓山惠光寺，僧列炬迎之。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
新兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='55227491a89c4d5183ddd74dedb340b8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("55227491a89c4d5183ddd74dedb340b8");'><span id='55227491a89c4d5183ddd74dedb340b8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>，40岁</div><div id='55227491a89c4d5183ddd74dedb340b8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年10月</a>　十月赴新州。张太君、沈夫人俱自京师归常州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宜春
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='728a1a0fc241425e88969975f0e69328_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("728a1a0fc241425e88969975f0e69328");'><span id='728a1a0fc241425e88969975f0e69328_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>，41岁</div><div id='728a1a0fc241425e88969975f0e69328' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年2月</a>　复宣德郎，添监袁州酒税。作品：叙复宣德郎谢表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《叙复宣德郎谢表》云：“臣浩言：十月初十日，伏奉告命，叙宣德郎，臣已即時望闕謝恩祗受訖。忽由望外，越在赦中，還陟文階，倍增感涕。中謝。”）</span><div id='poem_1209338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叙复宣德郎谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209338")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209338'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209338'>臣浩言：十月初十日，伏奉告命，叙宣德郎，臣已即时望阙谢恩祗受讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209338_comment'></div>忽由望外，越在赦中，还陟文阶，倍增感涕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209338_comment'></div>伏念臣顷从荒远，获赐言归，乡居甫阅于三年，瘴发屡濒于九死，赖袭太平之和气，得存垂绝之残生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209338_comment'></div>暑往寒来，不出衡门之下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209338_comment'></div>昏定晨省，用宽老母之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209338_comment'></div>为幸已多，复何所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209338_comment'></div>岂谓非常之造，曲加久废之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209338_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下道贯两仪，躬膺八宝，备帝王之多福，集祖宗之大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209338_comment'></div>政广周仁，施每先于无告；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209338_comment'></div>泽深汉德，犹下及于重泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209338_comment'></div>矧沟壑之未填，曾轩墀之夙侍，肆令收叙，俾与光荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209338_comment'></div>臣敢不笃励诚心，坚完晚节！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209338_comment'></div>无捐躯之路，虽莫报于隆恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209338_comment'></div>和击壤之音，但永陶于至化。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1209338_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a0b4b4c78a6e4476a19fb97329cd734f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a0b4b4c78a6e4476a19fb97329cd734f");'><span id='a0b4b4c78a6e4476a19fb97329cd734f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>，43岁</div><div id='a0b4b4c78a6e4476a19fb97329cd734f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年6月</a>　闰六月甲寅朔，至京口，有文。作品：蔡苏丞相公。<div id='poem_1209642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故观文殿大学士苏公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209642")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209642'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209642'>苏氏出己姓，颛帝之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209642_comment'></div>裔孙吴回为重黎，生陆终，陆终生昆吾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209642_comment'></div>昆吾之子封于苏，今邺郡之西苏城是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209642_comment'></div>三代时，苏忿生为周司寇，世居河内，后徙武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209642_comment'></div>至汉平陵侯建徙平陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209642_comment'></div>七世孙章为并州刺史，又五世生魏刚侯则，又八世生绰，为周度支尚书，封邳公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209642_comment'></div>邳公生威，相隋，封房公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209642_comment'></div>曾孙瑰相唐中宗、睿宗，封许公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209642_comment'></div>许公生诜，为徐州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209642_comment'></div>徐州之孙奕元和中终光州刺史，家固始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209642_comment'></div>光州之孙益自固始随王潮入闽，为王氏领军使，国初赠隰州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209642_comment'></div>隰州生光诲，石晋初与留从效诛泉南叛将黄绍颇，从效表为漳州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209642_comment'></div>泉帅陈洪进畏其英杰，不为己下，以计召之至同安，为大第留不遣，而密使人之漳州夺其位，遂为泉州同安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209642_comment'></div>开宝末盗起，劫漳州为盟主，馀党环城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209642_comment'></div>监郡何承矩与州将乔维岳欲屠城，遁去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209642_comment'></div>漳州一夕殪盗魁十馀人，送首级于州，馀众皆溃，城门始开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209642_comment'></div>归朝赏功，迁左屯卫将军，官其子十人，即公之高祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209642_comment'></div>子某仕江南，为漳州行军司马、检校国子祭酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209642_comment'></div>初，漳州既夷群盗，祭酒急索帐中，得贼所募人名籍千馀纸，火之，皆得不诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209642_comment'></div>漳州闻之，语人曰：「吾儿有阴德，其后必大」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209642_comment'></div>以公贵赠司空，大夫张氏赠代国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209642_comment'></div>生福公，讳某，少魁杰，有文武术略，举贤良方正能直言极谏，被召，会罢六科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209642_comment'></div>后与魏公同登进士第，既而覆落，改三班官，非其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209642_comment'></div>历提点荆湖南北路刑狱公事，知宜、邵、复三州，所至有风绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209642_comment'></div>终左屯卫将军，赠太师、福国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209642_comment'></div>初娶刘氏，陈留郡君，赠随国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209642_comment'></div>再娶翁氏，长安郡太君，赠徐国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209642_comment'></div>刘夫人生魏公，讳某，仁宗时以贤良方正决科，登侍从，入翰林为学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209642_comment'></div>数纳忠论事，特被知遇，赫然为天下伟人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209642_comment'></div>不幸早世，终侍读学士知河阳府，赠太师、魏国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209642_comment'></div>娶陈氏，河南郡太君，赠魏国太夫人，生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209642_comment'></div>公机警夙成，性知礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209642_comment'></div>三岁时，魏公为宜州推官，公犹未离怀抱，与人语，出则从官府之称，入则如家人礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209642_comment'></div>州将日召至其家与语，谓人曰「儿异人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209642_comment'></div>既就外傅，则与老生大儒讲论六经指义，无不通贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209642_comment'></div>建安黄晞、福唐王皓、南城李觏，临川蔡元导、元翰，建阳陈洪辈皆与为忘年友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209642_comment'></div>十八预进士高荐，大为吴公育所重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209642_comment'></div>魏公任子恩当得京秩，公力辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209642_comment'></div>再举，为别试第一，考官欧阳公修、张公方平谓人曰：「吾所试题，非通天人之奥、穷制作之原者不在首选也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209642_comment'></div>遂中庆历二年乙科，调汉阳军判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209642_comment'></div>以魏公奉诏修建北京，改宿州观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209642_comment'></div>魏公持福公丧，又改知江宁府江宁县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209642_comment'></div>建业承李氏后，版籍赋舆皆无法制，每有发敛，府移追扰，吏系缧于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209642_comment'></div>公至则曰：「此令职也，府何与焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209642_comment'></div>每因治诉，旁问邻里丁产多寡，悉得其详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209642_comment'></div>一日，召乡老更定户籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209642_comment'></div>民有自占不实者，必曰：「汝家尚有某丁某产，何不自言」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209642_comment'></div>相顾而惊，无敢隐者，一县以为神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209642_comment'></div>又为刬革蠹弊，更设条教，简而易行，诸县取以为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1209642_comment'></div>他日，诸令长造门，领县长拜廷下，谢曰：「此曹获免追逮，皆公之赐也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1209642_comment'></div>民有忿争者，至诚喻以乡党宜相亲善意，若以小忿而失欢心，一旦缓急，将何赖焉，往往谢去，或至半道思公言而归，县以大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1209642_comment'></div>时监司王鼎、王绰、杨纮皆以部吏少许可，及观公施设，则曰：「非吾所及也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1209642_comment'></div>寻以魏公忧去职，用治命葬京口，故今为润州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1209642_comment'></div>服除，为南京留守推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1209642_comment'></div>留守欧阳公一以府政委之曰：「子容处事精审，一经阅览，则某不复省矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1209642_comment'></div>杜岐公老居睢阳，一见公，深器之，每间数日，必折简召，常曰：「如君，真所谓不可得而亲疏者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1209642_comment'></div>且自谓平生人罕见其用心处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1209642_comment'></div>遂自小官以至为侍从、宰相，所以施设出处、先后本末，悉以语公，曰：「以子相知，且知子异日必为此官，老夫非以自矜也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1209642_comment'></div>其后公出入中外，荐历清要，至为宰辅，还政退居，名德终始略相似焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1209642_comment'></div>皇祐四年，翰林学士赵槩与诸禁从列荐公文学才行宜在朝廷，召试学士院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1209642_comment'></div>明年，改大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1209642_comment'></div>时公与冯公京同试，入最优等，除馆阁校勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1209642_comment'></div>至和初，同知太常礼院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1209642_comment'></div>嘉祐二年，改集贤校理，编定集贤院书集，再迁太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1209642_comment'></div>前后在馆九年，官冷俸薄，而奉翁夫人、陈夫人，养诸姑姊妹与外族之无归者凡数十人，躬自刻厉，甘旨无阙，婚嫁以时，妻子衣食之用常不足，而公处之晏如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1209642_comment'></div>时富郑公、韩魏公为相，务推尚廉退有德之士，以劝励风俗，知公久次儒馆，不干荣利，屡问所欲，惟力求外，以便亲养，遂除知颍州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1209642_comment'></div>后富公遗公书曰：「若吾子出处，可谓真古之君子矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1209642_comment'></div>考课，进祠部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1209642_comment'></div>英宗即位，迁度支员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1209642_comment'></div>仁宗山陵，有司不知故事，调发严急，吏挟事势，多以不时难得之物赋诸郡，旁郡皆取于民，至胁以军法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1209642_comment'></div>公谕吏曰：「遗诏山陵务从俭约，岂有土不产可强赋以害民乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1209642_comment'></div>至纤至悉，躬自区处，民既便之，而事以集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1209642_comment'></div>召为开封府界提点诸县镇公事，陛对称旨，赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1209642_comment'></div>岁大旱疫，公请转邻路粟以补匮乏，且委本司与诸县审蠲租税，免自朝廷差官以重劳扰，民赖以济甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1209642_comment'></div>又言周制六军盖出六乡之众，在王畿四郊之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1209642_comment'></div>唐设十二卫将军，亦散布辅畿郡县，又以关内诸府分隶之，皆所以临制四方，为上国蕃卫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1209642_comment'></div>国朝禁兵多屯京城及畿内东南诸县，虽于运粮供馈为便，而西北两面武备或阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1209642_comment'></div>今中牟、长垣直都门要冲之路，二鄙驿置皆由此出，而旧不屯兵，至于城守防传，居常乏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1209642_comment'></div>请置营益兵，以备非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1209642_comment'></div>明年，杜文等乘饥啸聚长垣，贼杀官吏，人莫不服公之先见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1209642_comment'></div>公即请以获盗多寡立县令殿最法，以为巡检、县尉但能捕盗，而不能使民不为盗，能使民不为盗者，县令也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1209642_comment'></div>且州县物务岁课稍亏，则官佐有罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1209642_comment'></div>今良民罹剽劫之害，而亲民官独不任其责，可乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1209642_comment'></div>迁三司度支判官，为治平四年寿圣节接送伴使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1209642_comment'></div>虏使还至恩州驿舍，夜火，左右白请与虏使出避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1209642_comment'></div>州兵叩门，欲入救，公闭门不纳，令曰「妄动者寘之法」，徐使防卒扑灭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1209642_comment'></div>郡人恟恟以为虏反，州兵亦欲因缘生事，飞语至京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1209642_comment'></div>公还入对，神宗首以问公，闻奏本末，喜曰：「朕始亦疑之，使人密诇，皆如卿言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1209642_comment'></div>闻卿措置甚得宜，其所镇遏多矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1209642_comment'></div>覃恩改工部郎中，迁为淮南转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1209642_comment'></div>神宗收揽万机，厉精政事，尤留意人物，自在藩邸闻公名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1209642_comment'></div>及使事还，益被知遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1209642_comment'></div>至陛辞日，咨访治道，因问入馆之年，曰：「何濡滞久耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「臣自选调被召，才改官即入馆，历计资级，未为濡滞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1209642_comment'></div>于是有用公意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1209642_comment'></div>未几，光禄卿史炤为淮南转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1209642_comment'></div>因对，上曰：「苏某有学识，与卿同事甚善」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1209642_comment'></div>后数月，召修《起居注》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1209642_comment'></div>先是，记注久阙员，资望无踰公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1209642_comment'></div>丞相韩魏公数荐公，会执政以亲嫌为言，故有使淮之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1209642_comment'></div>至是上自擢焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1209642_comment'></div>公与秘阁校理李大临并命，官同而除同，以公职集贤，在大临上，公以年齿推先大临而居其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1209642_comment'></div>兼同判礼部、祠部，又判三司磨勘司，改同判太常寺兼礼仪事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1209642_comment'></div>熙宁元年，召试知制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1209642_comment'></div>故事，外制不过六员，时阙其一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1209642_comment'></div>上不欲独试大临，命公同试，员遂溢数，乃特恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1209642_comment'></div>入谢，赐金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1209642_comment'></div>俄充北朝皇太后生辰国信使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1209642_comment'></div>是岁郊恩，加朝散大夫，封南阳县男，食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1209642_comment'></div>二年，兼通进银台司兼门下封驳事，同详定命官使臣过犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1209642_comment'></div>又为北朝贺生辰馆伴使，同知审官院，权审刑院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1209642_comment'></div>时知金州、比部郎中张仲宣坐枉法赃罪至死，法官援李希辅例，贷死杖脊，黥隶海岛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1209642_comment'></div>公奏曰：「希辅、仲宣均为枉法，而情有轻有重者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1209642_comment'></div>上愕然曰：「枉法岂复有轻者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「希辅知台州，受赇数百千，额外度僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1209642_comment'></div>仲宣则以所部金坑发檄巡检体究无甚利，土人惮兴作，遂以金八两求仲宣不差官比较，止系违令，可比恐喝条耳，故枉法为轻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1209642_comment'></div>上曰：「免决黥之，如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「士大夫有罪，可杀则杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1209642_comment'></div>古者刑不上大夫，仲宣官五品，有罪得乘车，令贷其死而黥之，使与徒隶为伍，所重者污辱衣冠，顾其人无足矜也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1209642_comment'></div>上曰：「免决与黥，流岭外」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1209642_comment'></div>公再拜奉诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1209642_comment'></div>自是命官犯赃抵罪者遂以为例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1209642_comment'></div>又兼提举兵吏司封官诰院，详定天下印文，判司农寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1209642_comment'></div>三年，权知贡举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1209642_comment'></div>四月，朝廷特除前秀州军事判官李定为太子中允、监察御史里行，知制诰宋敏求以为弗循旧制，封还词头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1209642_comment'></div>翌日辞职，罢之，词头复下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1209642_comment'></div>公适当制，即奏：「去岁诏旨专令中丞举官，虽不限资品，犹以京秩荐授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1209642_comment'></div>今定自支郡幕职官入居纠绳之地，近岁未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1209642_comment'></div>议者或谓唐世自诸侯幕府入登台省者多矣，定之此除不为过，臣以谓不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1209642_comment'></div>在唐方镇盛时，有奏辟郎官、御史以充幕府者，由此幕府增重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1209642_comment'></div>祖宗深鉴此弊，一切釐改，州郡僚佐皆从朝廷补受，大臣出镇或许辟官，亦皆随资注拟，满岁迁秩，并循铨格，非复唐世之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1209642_comment'></div>而今之三院又重于昔时，况定不由铨考擢授朝列，不缘御史之荐直寘宪台，虽朝廷急于用才，度越常格，然隳紊法制，必致人言，所益者小，所损者大，未敢具草」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1209642_comment'></div>复送李大临，大临如公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1209642_comment'></div>又送公，公又言：「祖宗朝天下初定，士或弃草莱而不用，故有起孤远而登显要者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1209642_comment'></div>自真宗后，每有除授，虽幽人异行，亦不至超越资品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1209642_comment'></div>今朝廷清明俊乂，并用进士，台阁动有成规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1209642_comment'></div>定以远州幕官，非有积累之资，明白之效，偶因召对，一言称旨，便授台官，它日或有非常之人又过于此，则复以何官处之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1209642_comment'></div>浸渐不已，诚恐高官要秩或可以岐路致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1209642_comment'></div>臣切谓威福之柄，人主得以自专；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1209642_comment'></div>官守有责，臣下得以固执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1209642_comment'></div>若朝廷以定才实非常，则当特与改官，别授职任，随资超用，无所不可，不必遂弃近例，处之宪纲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1209642_comment'></div>疏奏，手诏曰：「二十八日上殿来，有事指挥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1209642_comment'></div>公入对，上曰：「卿所谓李定事虽善，然熙宁二年诏书，奏举台官，不拘官职高下令兼权，则定之除命正合诏意，不为越法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1209642_comment'></div>宜以举官条赴院商量，速为草制，久格诏命，恐将得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1209642_comment'></div>卿宜思之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「臣闻治道在察臣下之邪正，邪正之分，惟所操守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1209642_comment'></div>若臣前以为不可，今蒙陛下召谕，遂变前言，乃奸邪固位之臣所为也，陛下亦将察而罪之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1209642_comment'></div>熙宁二年诏书臣亦讲论，若于臣心无疑，岂敢久格诏命」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1209642_comment'></div>退而复论曰：「从前台官须于太常博士以上、中行员外郎以下奏举，难得资序相当之人，故朝廷又令不拘官职高下令兼权，盖谓不限博士与中行员外郎耳，非谓选人亦许奏举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1209642_comment'></div>所谓兼权者，如三丞已行，未可为监察，故令上权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1209642_comment'></div>前行员外郎，不可为侍御，故令下兼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1209642_comment'></div>皆不为选人设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1209642_comment'></div>若不拘官职高下选人在其间，则是秀州判官亦可以兼权里行，不必更改中允也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1209642_comment'></div>臣所以喋喋有言者，但为爱惜朝廷之法，遵守有司之职耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1209642_comment'></div>缴而复下，至于七八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1209642_comment'></div>后虽大临当日，而堂劄批「圣旨与除李定系特旨，不碍近降条制」，促公撰词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1209642_comment'></div>公又奏：「定初等职官，超授朝列，兼权御史，不应近制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1209642_comment'></div>若果出圣意，则须非常之才，然后可以厌伏群议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1209642_comment'></div>昔马周为条陈当世切务，唐太宗拔于布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1209642_comment'></div>近世张知白上书言事，论议卓越，真宗拔于河阳职官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1209642_comment'></div>此二臣者，可谓有显状矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1209642_comment'></div>然周犹召直门下省，明年方用为御史；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1209642_comment'></div>知白召还，奏对称旨，亦命试舍人院，然后授以正言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1209642_comment'></div>若定果足副特旨之擢，别授一官，寘之京师，俟见实状，进用未晚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1209642_comment'></div>遂与大临俱落知制诰归班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1209642_comment'></div>凡岁馀，虽大寒暑、甚风雨，未尝一日移告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1209642_comment'></div>执政或喻公请外官闲局，公曰：「方以罪谪，敢求自便乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1209642_comment'></div>士大夫益推重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1209642_comment'></div>四年，大享明堂恩，始知婺州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1209642_comment'></div>溯桐庐，江水暴迅，挽舟卒力不胜，樯折，舟横覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1209642_comment'></div>魏国太夫人在舟中几溺矣，公哀号赴水救之，舟忽自正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1209642_comment'></div>太夫人甫出及岸，舟反覆，溺公一子与妹与甥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1209642_comment'></div>皆不救，独太夫人脱危难，水不入口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1209642_comment'></div>众以谓公诚孝所感，阴相之所致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1209642_comment'></div>婺学逼双溪，每秋潦溪涨，浸殿堂水数尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1209642_comment'></div>公乃迁于近南爽恺之地，多士四集，导以礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1209642_comment'></div>自此士益向学，登第者相继，文物之盛，前数十年无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1209642_comment'></div>移知亳州，七年，召还，勾当三班院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1209642_comment'></div>是岁用郊祀恩复集贤院学士，加护军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1209642_comment'></div>八年，出知应天府，兼南京留守司事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1209642_comment'></div>十月，彗星出，赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1209642_comment'></div>始，公与李大临同得罪，而当涂者特不喜公，至是三更赦，大临复待制，独于公以久不磨勘为言，止除秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1209642_comment'></div>岁终，复召勾当三班院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1209642_comment'></div>因对奏言：「本朝自庆历中因营妇逃亡，指赦而出，始有不用赦原之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1209642_comment'></div>臣在南都，见有犯罪在数十年前，虽屡经赦宥，不得沾恩者，则无知之民一犯禁令，无自新之路矣，甚可矜恻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1209642_comment'></div>上以为然，其后遂诏法官议而改焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1209642_comment'></div>寻兼知通进银台司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1209642_comment'></div>九年，以吴越荐饥，选知杭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1209642_comment'></div>一日出，遇百馀人遮道泣诉曰：「某等以转运司责所逋市易缗钱，昼系公庭，夜禁厢院，虽死无可偿者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「吾今释汝，使汝得营生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1209642_comment'></div>衣食之馀，悉以偿官，期以岁月而足，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1209642_comment'></div>皆曰不敢负，于是纵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1209642_comment'></div>转运使大怒，欲奏公沮坏法令，而民偿责者乃先期而至，遂不复言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1209642_comment'></div>一日，燕有美堂，闻将兵结集，谋害官吏，郡人喧传，恐惧不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1209642_comment'></div>公谈笑自如，密谕兵官多捕首领十数辈，械送狱中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1209642_comment'></div>逮暮夜会散，而坐客不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1209642_comment'></div>十年，召修仁宗英宗正史，俄兼提举中太一宫、兼集禧观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1209642_comment'></div>是岁，再充北朝生辰国信使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1209642_comment'></div>郊礼成，进右谏议大夫，封开国子，加食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1209642_comment'></div>在虏中，遇冬至，本朝历先北朝一日，北人问公孰是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「历家算术小异，迟速不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1209642_comment'></div>谓如亥时节气当交，则犹是今夕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1209642_comment'></div>若踰数刻，即属子时，为明日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1209642_comment'></div>或先或后，各从本朝之历可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1209642_comment'></div>虏人深以为然，遂各以其日为节庆贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1209642_comment'></div>使还奏之，上喜曰：「朕思之，此最难处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1209642_comment'></div>卿之所对，极中事理」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1209642_comment'></div>因问虏中山川形势、人情向背，公曰：「虏讲和之日久，颇窃中国典章礼义以维持其政令，上下相安，未有离贰之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1209642_comment'></div>昔人以谓匈奴直百年之运，言其盛衰有数也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1209642_comment'></div>上曰：「虏比自耶律德光至今，何止百年」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「汉武帝自谓高皇帝遗朕平城之忧，虽久动征讨，而匈奴终不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1209642_comment'></div>至宣帝，呼韩单于稽首称藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1209642_comment'></div>唐自中叶以后，河湟陷于吐蕃，宪宗每读《贞观政要》，慨然有收复意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1209642_comment'></div>至宣宗时，乃以三关七州归于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1209642_comment'></div>由此观之，夷狄之叛服不常，不系中国之盛衰也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1209642_comment'></div>上深然之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1209642_comment'></div>京尹缺，上欲用公，吴丞相充以史院才难得人为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1209642_comment'></div>上宣曰「苏某久历藩府，详练政事」，遂擢权知开封府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1209642_comment'></div>未半岁，都邑称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1209642_comment'></div>上谕宰臣等曰：「苏某到府，决遣无滞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1209642_comment'></div>会祥符令孙纯罢官，欲之新任，贷其所部门僧钱百千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1209642_comment'></div>它日，同院僧告门僧还往倡家，且持钱百千出，疑有奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1209642_comment'></div>公判曰：「告非干己事，不当治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1209642_comment'></div>钱隶常住，非官给，无贷贷法，然纯闻事作，已偿之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1209642_comment'></div>乃杖僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1209642_comment'></div>言者谓公纵出纯罪，有诏鞫治，而公止坐失出杖罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1209642_comment'></div>案成，御史舒亶驳奏，以谓纯乃苏某女婿堂姊之子，实为近亲，不可以失论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1209642_comment'></div>是时公女新嫁李徽之子，李大族，公固不知其为亲也，不复自辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1209642_comment'></div>降授秘书监、知濠州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1209642_comment'></div>公在府日，尝治国子博士陈世儒狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1209642_comment'></div>世儒妻李氏恶世儒所生母，欲其死，谕群婢曰：「博士一日持丧，则汝辈欲留者多与金，欲去者厚遣之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1209642_comment'></div>语多类此，终不明言使之杀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1209642_comment'></div>狱成，而法吏以李氏无杀姑语，情虽切害，而法不至死，案屡驳而情不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1209642_comment'></div>一日，因奏事，上谓公曰：「人言卿与所司欲宽世儒狱，此人伦大恶，当穷竟，不可纵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「臣备员京尹，有罪者皆付之有司，一有轻重意，则有司观望，遂致刑名出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1209642_comment'></div>此事臣固不敢言宽，亦不敢喻之使重」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1209642_comment'></div>公既出，而狱久不决，移治大理寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1209642_comment'></div>大理即以李氏之母吕乃枢密副使公著之妹，公著与苏某厚，必尝请求，请遣官即讯，而已移劾御史台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1209642_comment'></div>公自濠赴台置对，御史曰：「公素长者，必以交旧之情不能违，速自言，毋重困辱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「使某诬人，虽死不可为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1209642_comment'></div>若自诬以得罪，虽甚重不敢避」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1209642_comment'></div>遂手书数百言付狱吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1209642_comment'></div>上览奏牍，以为疑，诏御史求实状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1209642_comment'></div>御史反覆究治，无所得，乃诘大理狱吏所以得吕某请求之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1209642_comment'></div>吏穷，吐实曰：「此乃大理丞贾种民增减其文而为之也，今其稿尚在家」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1209642_comment'></div>取而视之，信然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1209642_comment'></div>于是公得辨明，止坐尝闻同列语世儒帷箔事，应曰诚有之，为泄狱情，罢濠州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1209642_comment'></div>未几，除知河阳，以魏公捐馆河阳辞不行，改知沧州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1209642_comment'></div>入辞，曰：「如卿宜在朝廷，朕知卿久矣，每欲用卿，辄为事所夺，岂非命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1209642_comment'></div>卿直道久而自明」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1209642_comment'></div>公顿首谢，因言：「臣母畏寒，俟春和可行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1209642_comment'></div>上曰：「卿母谁氏」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「龙图阁直学士陈从易女」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1209642_comment'></div>上曰：「天圣间侍从耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「臣外祖天圣间以直昭文馆知广州还，不市南物，辇见俸过岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1209642_comment'></div>仁宗闻之，即日擢知制诰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1209642_comment'></div>上曰：「清节过于马援矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1209642_comment'></div>到沧数月，复大中大夫，召还，判尚书吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1209642_comment'></div>中书舍人舒亶言公复官未应叙法，中批以旧官判吏部，又兼详定官制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1209642_comment'></div>先是，唐制文选掌于吏部，武选则兵部主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1209642_comment'></div>神宗谓自三代至汉未尝有文武之别，议者不知所处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1209642_comment'></div>公言：「唐制，吏部有三铨之法，分品秩而掌选事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1209642_comment'></div>今欲文武一归吏部，则莫若分左右曹以掌两选，又以品秩课格分治之，无所不可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1209642_comment'></div>上从之，于是吏部有四选之法焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1209642_comment'></div>后因进对，上曰：「朝廷与契丹通好岁久，故事仪式遗散者多，每使人生事无以折正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1209642_comment'></div>朕欲集国朝以来至昨代州定地界文案，以类编次为书，后来得以稽据，非卿不可成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1209642_comment'></div>然此书浩繁，卿自度几岁可毕」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「臣愿尽力二年」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1209642_comment'></div>因令置局于枢密后厅，仍辟官检阅文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1209642_comment'></div>如期书成，凡十有八门，合二百五十卷，为事目总叙奏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1209642_comment'></div>上览之嘉叹，赐名《华戎鲁卫信录》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1209642_comment'></div>元丰五年，为北虏贺正馆伴使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1209642_comment'></div>虏使郑颛明辩有才智，上命副使张山甫谕以「近命苏颂修《信录》，欲以重两朝盟好之固」，颛感激称谢，见公益恭逊，私觌礼物，皆异常时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1209642_comment'></div>遣使喻旨曰：「闻虏使以卿儒学酝藉，赠遗特殊，今以小龙茶琉璃器赐卿，可予之以答其意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1209642_comment'></div>颛复遗公异锦一端，即日进之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1209642_comment'></div>后因奏事语及，上曰：「禁中所无也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1209642_comment'></div>复大中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1209642_comment'></div>官制行，改通议大夫、吏部侍郎，以尝领详定，特迁正议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1209642_comment'></div>六年，上幸尚书省，迁光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1209642_comment'></div>是岁，增上列圣徽号，为礼仪使，乘辂奉册入庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1209642_comment'></div>郊礼成，加上护军，进开国侯，食邑千三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1209642_comment'></div>七年，魏国太夫人寝疾在告，同曹侍郎权引选人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1209642_comment'></div>上顾左右，问苏颂安在，左右以实对，令枢密承旨张诚一喻旨曰：「太夫人疾幸有间，宜亟出视事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1209642_comment'></div>会太夫人薨，遣中使就第抚问曰：「早闻太夫人之丧，想卿情极哀慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1209642_comment'></div>方暑，宜少抑摧踊」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1209642_comment'></div>明日，又遣使赐白金千两，诏有司假官舍以居，州郡应副葬事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1209642_comment'></div>元祐初服除，进刑部尚书，俄兼详定重修敕令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1209642_comment'></div>二年，迁吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1209642_comment'></div>八月，兼侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1209642_comment'></div>奏言：「国朝典章，大抵沿袭唐旧，史官所记，善恶咸备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1209642_comment'></div>乞诏史官、学士采录新、旧《唐书》中臣主所行，日进数事，以备圣览」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1209642_comment'></div>遂诏经筵官遇非讲读日进汉、唐故事二条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1209642_comment'></div>公每有所进，可为规戒、有补时事者，必述以己意，反复言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1209642_comment'></div>公前后掌天官四选五年，是时新法行，吏无所觊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1209642_comment'></div>每选人改官，京朝官、使臣关升磨勘，或以功过当升降者，吏洗垢求瑕，故为稽滞，且引失自首，以沮格之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1209642_comment'></div>远方寒选待次辇下，动经岁时，不见得否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1209642_comment'></div>公至则敕吏曰，某官缘某事当会某处，仍引合用条格，具委无漏落状同上，自是吏不得逞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1209642_comment'></div>每诉者至，必取案牍使自省阅，诉者服乃退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1209642_comment'></div>其不服者，公必往复诘难，度可行行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1209642_comment'></div>苟有疑，则为之奏请，或建白都堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1209642_comment'></div>故士大夫受赐多，不得者亦以为无可憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1209642_comment'></div>四年，迁翰林学士承旨，兼掌皇弟五王笺表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1209642_comment'></div>明年三月，迁尚书左丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1209642_comment'></div>公自至和入中，馆居京久，闾巷之人皆闻公名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1209642_comment'></div>至是登用，莫不相庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1209642_comment'></div>明日，语执政曰：「苏颂甚慰人望」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1209642_comment'></div>七年，纳皇后，讲修六礼，为册礼使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1209642_comment'></div>六月，进右仆射兼中书侍郎，开国公，加食邑七百户、实封三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1209642_comment'></div>是岁郊礼恩，加千户、实封四百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1209642_comment'></div>公自与闻国政，务在奉行故事，使有司奉法遵职，执事量能授任，杜绝侥倖僭差之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1209642_comment'></div>深戒疆埸之臣邀功生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1209642_comment'></div>每庙堂论议，援古證今，出入经史，所未安者必力争之，毅然不可回，与同列浸不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1209642_comment'></div>会牵复前侍御史贾易知苏州，争不决，至论于上前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「易与臣本无雅故，以其为御史不避权要，号为敢言，又法应牵复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1209642_comment'></div>既已为监司矣，乃徙知苏州，则是虽更赦，反下迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1209642_comment'></div>兼其馀当牵复者甚众，使人人如易，则赦令为虚文矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1209642_comment'></div>众欲加易以直馆阁职，公亦以为不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1209642_comment'></div>有旨再议，而御史杨畏、来之邵言公稽留诏命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1209642_comment'></div>公闻之，即舆归私第待罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1209642_comment'></div>三上章乞致仕，不许，又再以老病辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1209642_comment'></div>八年三月，拜观文殿大学士、集禧观使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1209642_comment'></div>九月，出知扬州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1209642_comment'></div>时宣仁太后上仙，哲宗始亲政，因公陛辞，尤加眷礼，问为政大略与人才能否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1209642_comment'></div>公对甚久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1209642_comment'></div>明年，西京留守阙，首命除公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1209642_comment'></div>公以老再辞，不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1209642_comment'></div>既行而卫国夫人薨，恳请南归，时绍圣初年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1209642_comment'></div>复知扬州，明年，再请还政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1209642_comment'></div>章累上，遂拜中太一宫使，居京口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1209642_comment'></div>后二年复请老，乃以太子少师致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1209642_comment'></div>今上即位，拜太子太保，增邑四百户，实封一百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1209642_comment'></div>建中靖国元年五月戊寅日北至，公起居膳犹如常，三接宾客，甚款至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1209642_comment'></div>已而草遗表数百言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1209642_comment'></div>逮暮，与诸子语如平时，无一及家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1209642_comment'></div>明日稍就枕，即屏左右、却药饵，召常所用医工亲谢遣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1209642_comment'></div>夜半，犹起就坐，达寅而薨，实二十日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1209642_comment'></div>讣闻，上辍视朝二日，制赠司空，遣中使赙恤其家，恩意甚至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1209642_comment'></div>公天资仁厚，宇量闳博，喜愠不形于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1209642_comment'></div>事亲孝，睦九族以慈，处朋友以义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1209642_comment'></div>幼自偪束，尤谨礼法，虽燕居，必正衣冠危坐，家人莫见堕容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1209642_comment'></div>平生未尝问家人有无，晚际会，所得俸赐，随即散用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1209642_comment'></div>其自奉养至俭薄，每食不过一肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1209642_comment'></div>始薨之日，吊哭者造其寝堂，见其居处服用，无不叹愕咨嗟，以为寒素不若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1209642_comment'></div>自少所交，皆当世贤杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1209642_comment'></div>及居显近，务推挽正人吉士，不问识与不识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1209642_comment'></div>性酷嗜学，晚岁弥甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1209642_comment'></div>自书契以来，坟史所载九流百家之说，至于图纬、阴阳五行、律吕、星官、算法、山经、本草、训故、文字，无所不通，不独见于论议文章，必欲验之实事，以扶助世教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1209642_comment'></div>其于名理，所造尤精诣，所至为政，务大体，深戒虚名，因时乘理而实利及下，莫见其迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1209642_comment'></div>既去，则人莫不思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1209642_comment'></div>在相位时，避远权势，门无杂宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1209642_comment'></div>其进退士大夫无纤毫私意，以故人不归恩，而怨讟亦不切至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1209642_comment'></div>为馆职时，尝被命补注《神农本草图经》、《千金方书》，而医家赖以活人甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1209642_comment'></div>元祐中，建请别制浑仪，因命公提举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1209642_comment'></div>公既邃于律历，又以吏部令史韩公廉晓算术、有巧思，奏用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1209642_comment'></div>且授以古法，为台三层，上设浑仪，仪中设浑象，下设司辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_354_1209642_comment'></div>贯以一机，激水转轮，不假人力，时至刻临，则司辰出谷，星辰躔度，所次占候，测验不差晷刻，昼夜晦明，皆可推见，前此未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1209642_comment'></div>至和中，文潞公为相，尝请建家庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1209642_comment'></div>事下太常，公议以为《礼》：大夫、士有田则祭，无田则荐，是有土者乃为庙祭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1209642_comment'></div>有田则有爵，无土与爵则子孙无以继承宗祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1209642_comment'></div>是有庙者止于其躬，子孙无爵，祭乃废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1209642_comment'></div>若参合古今之制，依约封爵之令，为之差等，锡以土田，然后庙制可议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1209642_comment'></div>若犹未也，即请考案唐贤寝堂祠享仪，止用燕器常食而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1209642_comment'></div>嘉祐中，诏礼院议立故郭皇后神御殿于景灵宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1209642_comment'></div>公以谓敕书云「向因忿郁，偶失谦恭」，此则无可废之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1209642_comment'></div>又云「朕念其自历长秋，仅周一纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1209642_comment'></div>逮事先后，秪奉寝园」，此则有不当废之悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1209642_comment'></div>又云「可追复皇后，其祔庙谥册并停」，此则有合祔庙及谥册之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1209642_comment'></div>请祔郭皇后于后庙，以成追复之义，备荐享之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1209642_comment'></div>众论未定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_368_1209642_comment'></div>一日，白事至都堂，丞相曾公问曰：「学士议郭后事甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_369_1209642_comment'></div>然郭后是上元妃，若祔庙则事体重矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_370_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「国朝祖宗三圣贺、尹、潘皆元妃，事体正相类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_371_1209642_comment'></div>今止祔后庙，则岂得有同异之言」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_372_1209642_comment'></div>曾公曰：「议者以谓阴逼母后，是恐伤万岁后配祔之意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_373_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「若加一怀哀悯之谥，则不为逼矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_374_1209642_comment'></div>曾公叹重久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_375_1209642_comment'></div>后群牧判官宋公敏求谓公曰：「闻议郭后事引敕语，此是先人宣献为参政时自撰，甚有微意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_376_1209642_comment'></div>云『后有知礼者当行之』，盖当时有沮此议者，非公莫能见也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_377_1209642_comment'></div>然竟不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_378_1209642_comment'></div>熙宁初，经筵官请坐讲，下礼官考议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_379_1209642_comment'></div>公以谓：「天禧旧制，侍臣皆赐坐，讲官别设本于前列坐而听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_380_1209642_comment'></div>乾兴后，侍臣皆先就坐，赐茶讫，彻席立讲，讲毕复坐赐汤而从容焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_381_1209642_comment'></div>其尊德重道，固已重于三公矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_382_1209642_comment'></div>然事出上恩，虽微贱赐坐，于义无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_383_1209642_comment'></div>若人主不命而自请之，则为非礼矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_384_1209642_comment'></div>且侍从之官见于天子，若赐之坐，有所顾问，犹当避席立对，况执经人主之前，本欲便于指陈，则立讲为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_385_1209642_comment'></div>若谓其传道近于为师，则今侍讲但解诂旧儒章句之学耳，非有为师之实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_386_1209642_comment'></div>自乾兴以来，侍臣立讲仅五十年，足为定法，岂可一旦以为有司之失而轻议变更乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_387_1209642_comment'></div>神宗竟从旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_388_1209642_comment'></div>尝议学校，欲博士分经课试，诸生以行义为升俊之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_389_1209642_comment'></div>议贡举，欲先士行而后文艺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_390_1209642_comment'></div>去封弥誊录之法，先行州县，使有司得专参详考察，庶几存乡举里选之遗范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_391_1209642_comment'></div>又请每岁考进士量留人数，以广制科遗逸之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_392_1209642_comment'></div>又谓尚书，古之天台，朝廷万事之本皆由此出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_393_1209642_comment'></div>仁宗朝大臣尝请移审官院归吏部，三班院归兵部，审刑院归刑部，庶稍近古制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_394_1209642_comment'></div>而当时议者不深惟其本，苟惮兴作，遂不果行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_395_1209642_comment'></div>请先制朝臣两员，振举纲维，俟其葺有绪，然后议移审官等三院还省，则南宫故事可举而行，一代典章，于斯为盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_396_1209642_comment'></div>其后诏博士分经，以三舍取士，兼考行义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_397_1209642_comment'></div>又十馀年而官制行，皆略如此言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_398_1209642_comment'></div>又请重加役流法以代配隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_399_1209642_comment'></div>又尝因对，神宗从容问宗子主祭承重之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_400_1209642_comment'></div>公言，礼典久废，服属亲疏有所未明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_401_1209642_comment'></div>古者贵贱不同礼，诸侯、大夫世有爵禄，故有大宗、小宗主祭专重之义，则丧服从而异制，匹夫庶人亦何预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_402_1209642_comment'></div>传曰：「父为长子，何以三年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_403_1209642_comment'></div>正体于上，又乃将所传重也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_404_1209642_comment'></div>近代不世爵，宗庙因而不立，尊卑亦无所统，其长子孙与众子孙无以异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_405_1209642_comment'></div>今《五服敕》嫡孙为祖、父为长子犹斩衰三年，生而情礼则一，死而丧服独异，恐非先王制礼之本意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_406_1209642_comment'></div>而世俗之论乃以三年之丧为承重，而不知为承大宗之重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_407_1209642_comment'></div>尝闻庆历中朝廷议臣僚应任子者，长子与长孙差优与官，馀皆降杀，亦近古立宗之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_408_1209642_comment'></div>乞诏礼官、博士参议礼律，合承重者，酌古今收族主祭之礼，立为宗子继祖者，以异于众子孙之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_409_1209642_comment'></div>及士、庶人不当同用一律，使人知尊祖，不违礼教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_410_1209642_comment'></div>为左丞时，尝权枢密院，边帅遣种朴入奏，得谍言，阿里骨已死，国人未知所立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_411_1209642_comment'></div>蕃官赵纯忠者信谨可任，愿乘其未定，以劲兵数千拥纯忠入其国立之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_412_1209642_comment'></div>众议欲如其请，公独曰：「不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_413_1209642_comment'></div>昔晋赵鞅以师纳蒯聩于卫，其子辄犹拒之而弗受，以尊王父之命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_414_1209642_comment'></div>今越境而入其国，事未可知，使拒而不受，得无损朝廷威重乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_415_1209642_comment'></div>徐观其变，俟其定而抚辑之未晚也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_416_1209642_comment'></div>已而边奏至，阿里骨故无恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_417_1209642_comment'></div>公学问渊博，无施不宜，其大者固已发于朝廷，垂之典册；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_418_1209642_comment'></div>其小者亦足以警动一时，诱掖后进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_419_1209642_comment'></div>元丰五年，神宗御集英殿放进士，有暨陶者，主司误呼为「暨」<span class='inlineComment2'>（去声，）</span>三呼不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_420_1209642_comment'></div>上顾公，公对曰：「当呼为『暨』」<span class='inlineComment2'>（居乙切。）</span>果应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_421_1209642_comment'></div>上曰：「卿何以知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_422_1209642_comment'></div>出何书乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_423_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「臣尝记三国时吴有暨艳造营府之论，恐其后也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_424_1209642_comment'></div>问陶乡里，乃建人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_425_1209642_comment'></div>上喜曰：「果吴人」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_426_1209642_comment'></div>褒谕再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_427_1209642_comment'></div>又问曰：「字书中训何义」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_428_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「字书不出何义，止云人姓氏，当从旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_429_1209642_comment'></div>今旦字缺下一画者，盖俗书避唐代宗名耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_430_1209642_comment'></div>又尝接伴至雄州，虏使问：「适过市，其榜有『仉』家，此何姓也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_431_1209642_comment'></div>公曰：「音与掌同，出《姓氏谱」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_432_1209642_comment'></div>虏人叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_433_1209642_comment'></div>每公卿会集，有僻书疑事，必以问公，公随为言之，常倾一坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_434_1209642_comment'></div>诸公好事者时时造前，听语经史微旨，前代典故，至近世名臣阅阀，无不厌服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_435_1209642_comment'></div>公亦喜为讲道，或终日清谈，亹亹忘倦，客有退而记录其言至盈编秩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_436_1209642_comment'></div>平生于人无纤芥仇怨，在杭州日，有要人以事属公，公不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_437_1209642_comment'></div>后其人当言路，怀忿抵巇，或谓其事迹书札具存可辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_438_1209642_comment'></div>公笑曰：「吾岂为是者」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_439_1209642_comment'></div>在颍州日，通判赵至忠本归明人，所至辄与守竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_440_1209642_comment'></div>公待之以礼，具尽诚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_441_1209642_comment'></div>他日，至忠泣曰：「某虏人也，然见义则服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_442_1209642_comment'></div>平生诚服者，唯今韩魏公与公耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_443_1209642_comment'></div>累官太子太保，职观文殿大学士，爵赵郡公，食邑四千七百户，实封一千三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_444_1209642_comment'></div>所著文集若干卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_445_1209642_comment'></div>初娶凌氏，屯田郎中景阳之女，追封吴国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_446_1209642_comment'></div>继室辛氏，驾部员外郎某之女，封魏国夫人，追封徙韩国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_447_1209642_comment'></div>男六人，熹、嘉皆朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_448_1209642_comment'></div>駉，朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_449_1209642_comment'></div>诒，承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_450_1209642_comment'></div>京，奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_451_1209642_comment'></div>携，通直郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_452_1209642_comment'></div>女三人，长适婿朝议大夫李孝鼎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_453_1209642_comment'></div>次二前卒，婿朝散郎刘琯、襄州录事参军贾收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_454_1209642_comment'></div>孙男十九人，象先，奉议郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_455_1209642_comment'></div>处厚，承事郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_456_1209642_comment'></div>德舆、行冲、季辅，皆承奉郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_457_1209642_comment'></div>长庆、馀庆、公绰、彦伯、道孙、简求、陶孙、伯孙、朝孙、叔孙、文孙、镇孙、季孙、公孙、葛孙，皆未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_458_1209642_comment'></div>孙女十二人，婿宣德郎李德严、知相州录事王琮、天平军节度推官朱邦彦、湖州武康尉王騠、明州定海主簿吕无忌、郊社斋郎曾怘，馀皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_459_1209642_comment'></div>曾孙男八人，直孙、赵孙、朱孙、磻孙、房孙、迎孙、瀛孙、信孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_460_1209642_comment'></div>曾孙女四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_461_1209642_comment'></div>卜，将以某年某月某日葬公于某所，某孙属某编次历官行事而为之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_462_1209642_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_463_1209642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_463_1209642_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年6月18日</a>　诏责授衡州别驾，永州安置。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年7月</a>　赴永州，沈夫人偕行。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宜昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5e5205a84c9c41a9a8d3e19b4055703a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5e5205a84c9c41a9a8d3e19b4055703a");'><span id='5e5205a84c9c41a9a8d3e19b4055703a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>，43岁</div><div id='5e5205a84c9c41a9a8d3e19b4055703a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年9月7日</a>　舟次黄陵庙下，有祭文。作品：祭告湘君湘夫人祝文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八四八题为《黄陵廟祝文》）</span><div id='poem_1209720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209720?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄陵庙祝文<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　崇宁元年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209720")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209720_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209720'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209720'>维崇宁元年岁次壬午九月癸未朔初七日己丑，责授衡州别驾、永州安置邹浩谨以清酌茗果之奠，敢昭告于湘君、湘夫人二妃之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209720_comment'></div>浩元符中以谏官论中宫不当立，削籍流新州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209720_comment'></div>明年，今天子嗣兴，召复秩序，遂隮禁从，为中书舍人，又为尚书吏部、兵部侍郎，又以宝文阁待制出帅杭、越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209720_comment'></div>顾虽报效未昭，而宿罪往愆亦埽然尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209720_comment'></div>日者元符皇后重有诉述，于是复窜湖外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209720_comment'></div>其所以播告天下，有特降之诏，有中出之疏，典刑所被，竦动一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209720_comment'></div>在神聪明，宜已洞察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209720_comment'></div>惟神以尧为父而嫔于虞，虞帝之所以去四凶，所以命九官，所以辨真伪是非之实而待君子小人各当其分，神固得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209720_comment'></div>用以昭物，岂不明哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209720_comment'></div>唐韩愈黜守潮阳，舟次祠下祷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209720_comment'></div>蒙神之福，启帝之心，以获位于朝，人到于今仰之<span class='inlineComment2'>（〔一〕）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209720_comment'></div>浩愚不肖，不足以方愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209720_comment'></div>傥其诚果在所享，庶几亦徼大庇，早获旋归，以奉老母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209720_comment'></div>若夫获位于朝如愈之前日事，则非所敢望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209720_comment'></div>惟神其听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209720_comment'></div>尚享。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1209720_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d924e7a45d4543f3824daf26c4cb569c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d924e7a45d4543f3824daf26c4cb569c");'><span id='d924e7a45d4543f3824daf26c4cb569c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>，47岁</div><div id='d924e7a45d4543f3824daf26c4cb569c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年2月29日</a>　过黄陵庙，复有祝文。作品：黄陵庙祝文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷二八四八《黄陵廟祝文》题下注“崇寧五年二月”）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　赴常州途中，有喜陈莹中瓘同预归田之命并寄曾敷文诞诸诗。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
平乐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ab0aa72c1dfb46d382166c79dd0daede_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ab0aa72c1dfb46d382166c79dd0daede");'><span id='ab0aa72c1dfb46d382166c79dd0daede_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1105')">1103-1105年</a>，44-46岁</div><div id='ab0aa72c1dfb46d382166c79dd0daede' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年3月21日</a>　至昭州，沈夫人与两子仍留永州.有诗。作品：将往昭州示柄。<div id='poem_515997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_515997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/515997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>将往昭州示柄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年3月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_515997")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_515997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_515997'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_515997'>与汝暂相别，南作昭州行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_515997'>昭州距零陵，坦坦十日程。<div id='poem_sentence_1_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_515997'>音信易来往，勿动异乡情。<div id='poem_sentence_2_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_515997'>但自勤读书，思索厥义精。<div id='poem_sentence_3_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_515997'>圣贤如日月，为汝出光明。<div id='poem_sentence_4_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_515997'>脩身识根本，力践以其诚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_515997'>发为文字间，笔墨自纵横。<div id='poem_sentence_6_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_515997'>零陵豪杰士，张邓尤高名。<div id='poem_sentence_7_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_515997'>汝其师事之，北面听指令。<div id='poem_sentence_8_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_515997'>分阴古所惜，况乃汝后生。<div id='poem_sentence_9_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_515997'>省定<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作定省）</span>汝母外，谨勿他事萦。<div id='poem_sentence_10_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_515997'>皇恩极天地，我罪终从轻。<div id='poem_sentence_11_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_515997'>还家知有时，欣见汝向成。<div id='poem_sentence_12_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_515997'>用为祖母寿，慰叔及弟兄。<div id='poem_sentence_13_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_515997'>携汝返乡国，重增门户荣。<div id='poem_sentence_14_515997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_515997'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_515997_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年8月</a>　在昭州，有铭文。作品：铭张明墓。<div id='poem_1209667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>铭张明墓<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁二年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209667")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209667'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209667'>役者张明以熙宁丁巳十月二十四日生宿州柳子镇，以崇宁癸未八月十一日死于昭州朝天坊，其服役予家盖十有九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209667_comment'></div>初，予之窜永州也，僮奴率惮行，独明求行甚力，后又随予至昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209667_comment'></div>昭于广西最为恶地，桂之城门号昭州门者不敢开，开则瘴大作，以故南人自畏之，商旅弗由其途，监司弗饮其水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209667_comment'></div>予至之日，适又甚焉，素巾满郊廛，丧鼓连昼夜，故老言数十年无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209667_comment'></div>尝于苍埃白雾中怪鸟正飞而堕，鸡豚狗彘正行而颠仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209667_comment'></div>问之他人，则曰发瘴然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209667_comment'></div>然随予居者无一不染此疾，呼医治药，朝夕以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209667_comment'></div>于其呻吟呕泄间，予形影兀兀，寝食几废，但幸其皆救耳，明卒不救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209667_comment'></div>呜呼，其偶然邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209667_comment'></div>非偶然也邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209667_comment'></div>以其死之明日，具棺敛葬于仙宫山之阴而为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209667_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1209667'>生于北斗之北，谁汝生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209667_comment'></div>死于南箕之南，谁汝死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209667_comment'></div>汝之所以然者，吾无得而诘焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209667_comment'></div>汝之体魄，其安于此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1209667_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　在昭州，有记。作品：翱凤亭记。<div id='poem_1209597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>翱风亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209597")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209597'>昭州荒僻，才数百家，无馀屋可以寓人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209597_comment'></div>余之来也，偶得进士王氏拾青阁居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209597_comment'></div>前俯乐川，后倚宝山，修竹高松，环作清奥，非初望所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209597_comment'></div>王氏驯驯类有识者，特为规山腰松竹最深处筑亭以避暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209597_comment'></div>余题其榜曰「翱风亭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209597_comment'></div>客未喻，请所以名意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209597_comment'></div>余曰：「此汉王褒语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209597_comment'></div>褒对诏，有所谓『恩从祥风翱』者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209597_comment'></div>圣王时如是，是之取耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209597_comment'></div>曰：「引古明今，厥意安在」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209597_comment'></div>曰：「余罪多矣，不可以一二数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209597_comment'></div>余罪大矣，不可以赦宥除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209597_comment'></div>前年窜新州，去年放永州，今又废弃于此，委亲弗得养，委家弗得顾，举世言忠孝者，莫不以余戒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209597_comment'></div>今天子孝弟，尊奉先烈，拔一时之英豪，而亟用之，以昭好恶，以正是非，以严纲纪，以沛膏泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209597_comment'></div>如天地焉，无不覆载；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209597_comment'></div>如日月焉，无不照烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209597_comment'></div>问之万民，万民有不乐其业者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209597_comment'></div>问之万物，万物有不遂其生者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209597_comment'></div>问之蛮夷戎狄，蛮夷戎狄有不安其所而不愿为臣妾者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209597_comment'></div>至和薰蒸，鼓为祥风，恩实从之，以游以翱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209597_comment'></div>昭虽远邦，固已动化于其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209597_comment'></div>余既获全馀生，又居此土，登此亭，导迎此风，以延致萧爽，以祛逐炎歊，瘴氛不能侵，邪气不能袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209597_comment'></div>一旦仁圣哀悯，刊石丹书，还身故里，老老幼幼，怡怡愉愉，歌咏时雍，为太平幸民，则是上恩之翱，未有如此其遭遇者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209597_comment'></div>此余所以名亭而见意也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209597_comment'></div>客欣然离席曰：「敢不倾耳而听，拭目而视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209597_comment'></div>指日而造门，为先生贺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209597_comment'></div>客退，书为记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1209597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　在昭州。郡守王藻以公寓居易拾青阁为来僊，公有诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　在昭州，有记。作品：拱北轩记。<div id='poem_1209596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拱北轩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_1209596")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209596'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209596'>拱北轩者，所居对堂之小轩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209596_comment'></div>昭人屋向皆东南，独此居面北，轩又正在北方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209596_comment'></div>先圣言北辰居其所而众星拱之，故取以名焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209596_comment'></div>因窃自念，君者，北辰也，拱者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209596_comment'></div>群臣者，众星也，拱之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209596_comment'></div>今在内为辅弼，为侍从，为六曹寺监之属，拱北可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209596_comment'></div>在外为监司，为守令，为诸路郡邑之属，拱北可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209596_comment'></div>而某则名除于仕版，身废于炎荒，既已陨坠而为石矣，尚奚丽天者之拟邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209596_comment'></div>又窃自念所除者名耳，拱北之心未尝除也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209596_comment'></div>所废者身耳，拱北之心未尝废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209596_comment'></div>夫未尝除而自除之，未尝废而自废之，非某所忍为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209596_comment'></div>某于是轩朝夕焚香，稽首再拜，上祝皇帝寿千万岁，长与天同，久与地并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209596_comment'></div>拱于内者，辅弼尽辅弼之道，侍从尽侍从之宜，六曹寺监之属尽所以为六曹寺监之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209596_comment'></div>拱而为外者，监司尽监司之分，守令尽守令之才，诸路郡邑之属尽所以为诸路郡邑之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209596_comment'></div>上下相承，如源流之一水；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209596_comment'></div>先后相应，如首尾之一形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209596_comment'></div>自京师而眺瞩之，虽远在蛮夷戎狄之外，犹且四序平、万物遂，重译效贡，拱我圣人，而况九州之内乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209596_comment'></div>和气浮于上，则景星见、卿云飞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209596_comment'></div>和气动于下，则朱草生、醴泉涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209596_comment'></div>凡是祥瑞之物，莫不纷纶毕至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209596_comment'></div>祖宗之功德，由此而弥光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209596_comment'></div>朝社之安荣，由此而弥固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209596_comment'></div>前古以来，未有太平若此其盛焉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209596_comment'></div>某之所以拱北，在是而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209596_comment'></div>且既已为石矣，亦为有触之而起者，始自肤寸，遄充太虚，于是滂沱，未必无助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209596_comment'></div>然则区区素定之心，又安敢自弃而莫之笃欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209596_comment'></div>又窃系以词曰：七曜兮可西，五岳兮可移，我心湛然兮如初时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209596_comment'></div>我不见穷达、得丧之殊途兮，惟拱北之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209596_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209596_comment'></div>高高无私兮，日监在兹。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1209596_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　在昭州。著《易解成》，作序。作品：易系词序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　在昭州，有诗。作品：与道人徐清。在昭州寄蓬莱并示柄诗。<div id='poem_516568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_516568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/516568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道人徐清自南来彦和莹中才叔并令寄声</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33143, "北宋", "邹浩", "poem_title_516568")'>邹浩</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_516568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_516568'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_516568'>吉语传来喜可知，岂无神物共扶持。<div id='poem_sentence_0_516568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_516568'>但怜四载遭三黜，偶与三公作四夔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_516568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_516568'>海上飓风应骤息，岭边炎瘴亦潜衰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_516568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_516568'>相从会有还归日，却向江乡话此时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_516568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_516568'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_516568_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年9月</a>　在昭州。诏徒元祐党人于近地，惟不得至畿甸。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bd2dcc8641234a16ac52d43e273960a7_label'><a href='javascript:
